Ruaidri Sinnach hi id Marta.
Calann Enair for Dardain & aenmad fichet
Cathal mac Taidc meic Cathail Meic Diarmata do gabail rigi Mugi Luirg
Magnus Conchobair mar aen re a fuair leis do Connachtaib & d'Ib Briuin & do Conmaicnib do techt do gabail rigi Connacht do fein, d'aithrigad a derbbrathar fein Cathail meic Conchobair Ruaid, & techt daib co hAth Slisen, ait a raibe Cathal cona shochraide.
Acus cumusg do thabairt daib leth ar leath diaroile & Cathal do gabail and & maidm do thabairt ara muintir, & do hathrigad he fein & do hairged urmor Connacht don chur-sin; acus rigi do gabail do Magnus ar eicin in tan-soin ar belaib a hsindserbrathar iarna beith secht mbliadna co leth inti, ut ait poeta:
Mac Conchobair rigda Ruaid fa ri Connacht theass is tuaid lethbliadain is a seacht soin rigi Cathail a Cruachain.
Dondchad Riabach mac Magnusa meic Murcertaig Mumnig.
Tech do gabail isin gemred cetna-sin for Magnus Conchobair do Toirrdelbach mac Eogain Conchobair isin Ros Mor & do Maelechlainn Flannacan maille ris, & do komuirli Fiachra Flainn doronad in gnim-sin, cur loited Magnus fein ann sin, & Ragnall Mag Ragnaill toisech Muintiri hEolais do marbad ann sin d'oenorchur tsoigti & Niall Gelbude Conchobair do lot ann sin, & daine do marbad dib & blad da n-echaib maithi do bein dib.
Sluagad la Magnus Conchobair a Sil Muredaig dar es a legis, cur gab a mbraigti
Sluagad lasin Iarla Ruad Risderd mac Uater Iarla Ulad meic Ricairt Moir meic Uilliam Congcur in Gabaltais dochum Connacht, co tanic co Ros Chomman d'indsaigid Magnusa meic Conchobair Ruaid ri Connacht in tan-sin, & d'indsaigid Meic Gerailt & muintiri in Rig, & do tinolsat uli ara chinn & do grendaigsid ant Iarla fo thecht secha sin.
Conid i comuirli dorone ant Iarla ann sin imthecht asin tir amach & a sluag do scailed iar sin.
Sdeffan ardespoc Tuama Da Gualann & Giustis na hErenn.
Uilliam Mac Feorais do togha dochum ardespocoite Tuama.
Calann Enair for Sathurn & aili uathad
Tadc Flannacan toisech Clainni Cathail.
Matha Scingin ollam Ceneoil Conaill.
Espoc Conmaicne an Gaillespoc, Milis a ainm.
Simon Finnachta aircideochain Ola Find.
Sluagad la Ricart Diuit & la Gallaib na Mide & Magnus Conchobair ri Connacht mar oen riu dochum Mailsechlainn & fer Mide archena, co tucad maidm forra and sin, & ro marbad Ricart Diuit and in barun is uasli do bi a n-Erinn ann sin do Gallaib & a braithricha amaille ris, & Siacus mac ind espaicc Cellaig do marbadh and beuss.
Fiachra Flainn
Sil Mailruain, in fer rob ferr icht & firinde & comarci & enech & engnam do thuisechaib Connacht uli, do dol do denam clemnusa re Gallaib, cur marbsat mac Ricairt Finn meic Uilliam Burc & Mac Feorais i mmebail e.
Sluagad mor la Mac Muris et la Mac Feorais dochum in Chalbaig Moir Conchobair & na mac rig Laignech archena, & tucad maidm mor forra inar marbad Mailir d'Exetra & Gaill imda aili and & imad da n-echaib do bein dib bos.
Calann Enair for Domnach & tres c;
Cairpre Mailsechlainn ri Mide do marbad do Mac Cochlan & do Delbna i mebail.
Congalach Mag Eochacan
Ceneoil Fiachach meic Neill Giallaig.
Uilliam Mac Feorais do gabail eirdespocoiti Tuama.
Int espoc Setachain espoc Cilli Meic Duach.
Sluagad la Domnall mac Briain Neill i Cenel n-Eogain gur cuir Niall Neill ar ecin esti & gabais fein in rigi ar los a lama.
Aed Domnaill do aithrigad da derbbrathair budein do Thairrdelbach Domnaill & in rigi do gabail do fein tria cumachtaib chinid a mathar Clainni Domnaill & galloclaech imda aili.
Calann Enair for Luan & cethair
Endecas.
Toirrdelbach mac Eogain Conchobair, in fer ba mo & ba hailli & ba ferr enech & engnam & dob ferr d'adbar rig, do marbad le Niall n-Gelbuide Conchobair.
Sluagad mor la hIarla Ulad a Tir Eogain dar athrig se Domnall mac Briain Neill, & do rigad les Niall Culanach Neill; & mar do faccaib int Iarla an tir marbthar in Niall-sin la Domnall, & do rigad a hucht an Iarla cetna mac Aeda Buide Neill & curthar Domnall asin tir amach tre nert an Iarla cetna.
Sluagad lasan Iarla a Tir Chonaill dochom Toirrdelbaig Domnaill, cur airc an tir uili etir chill & tuaith & conar faccaib breit for altoir na lebur aifrinn na coilech aifrinn i cellaib Ceneoil Conaill, & tucc an creich-sin leis a Connachtaib & tanicc co hOil Finn iar sin & tucsat Connachta felbraigti do in tan-sin, & do imtig iar sin.
Conchobar Dubta ri Fiachrach do badad for Sinainn ic techt i coinne inn Iarla cetna.
Comtocbail cocaid do denam do Chathal Conchobair & do Niall Gelbuide & do cech oen bai imailli friu etir Gallaib & Gaidelaib, do athrigad Magnusa Conchobair ri Connacht, & imrisain do tabairt doib da cheli hi Caraid Culmaili, & Cathal do lot ann sin & Murchad mac Taidc meic Andrias Conchobair & daine eli do marbad la Niall n-Gelbude Conchobair, eich imda do buain do muintir Magnusa & maidm do thabairt fair fein & a dola as fo laim; & crecha mora do denam do muintir Chathail & do Niall Gelbuide a Cairpri, uair ni rabi Cathal fein isin bali tar es a luit, & ro aircsit Cairpri uli o Cnucc Laigen inniar co hEs Dara.
Dala Magnusa immorro ar techt t-Sila Muredaig & a aesa grada fein & Gall Rosa Coman chuice da furtacht tar eis in mmadma-sin, tanicc iarnabarach hi coindee na crechsin & rucc se forra ic Sraith in Ferain & fon Aenach & benais a crecha dib & tuc maidm forra; & ted Niall fein ar ecin as & marbthur Tomas & Dauid da mac Meic Gostilb and, no do hainced Dauid and & marbthar ana lamdichus, & moran eli do marbad don tsluag etir Gallaib & Gaidelaib; & tocht do Niall isin tir iar sin ar sith iar sin & a ferann fein do tabairt do uile.
amles & imcosait do denam eturro iar sin & fobairt felli do indisin do Magnus do denam do Niall fair & fobairt an tire do facbail do Niall iar sin & crech mor do denam do Magnus for Niall iar sin & a arcain uli do, & a innocbail do thornem co mor lesna crechaib-sin.

Diarmait Flainn toisech Sil Mailruain.

Calann Enair for Mairt uathad
Sluagad lasan Iarla docum Magnusa Conchobair co tanic co Rus Comman & do impo aris can giall can etiri do gabail.
ro len Magnus he co Milicc tar sarugad Connacht & dochuaid ina tech & fuair cech ni ima rabi uad don cur-sin.
Sluagad aili lasan Iarla cetna cur airc urmor Lugne, & cid ed ni thanicc Domnall Egra ina tech & ni tuc giall na hetiri do don dulad-sin.
Niall Gelbuide Conchobair mac Muredaig Dechti meic Aedo Daill meic Toirrdelbaig Moir Conchobair ri Erenn do marbad do Thadc mac Andrias Conchobair & do Thuathal mac Murcertaig meic Muirchertaig Muimnig

Calann Enair for Dartain & sesed
Magnus mac Conchobair Ruaid meic Murcertaig Mumnig meic Toirrdelbaig Moir, ri Connacht fria re mbliadan co leth, amail forgles in fili:
Conchobair an chnis gil, mac meic Murcertaig Mumnig, coic bliadna co leth ria luad ba ri Magnus na marcsluag, do ecc iarna beith raithi i ngalar, fer ba mo grain & coscur i cathaib & i comracaib, Ri rob ferr engnam & enech do rigaib Erenn uile, for Loch Caircin.
Aed mac Eogain Conchobair do rigad don Giustis & do muintir Rig Saxan iar sin, & inmad la tar eis a rigtha a gabail do Mac Gerailt i mmebail & da muintir do marbad & creca mora do denam air iar sin.
Cathal Ruad Conchobair do gabail rige iar sin & a marbad i cinn rathi do Ruaidri mac Donnchada Riabaig Conchobair i mebail, & Aed mac Eogain do lecad immach & rige Connacht do gabail do tre nert an Giustis.
Murchad Mailsechlainn ri Mide do ecc
Fergal Raigillig taisech Muintiri Mailmorda fria re da bliadan dec do marbad ar lar a longpuirt fein do Thellach Dunchada
Tasi Patric & Coluim Cille & Brigti do foillsiugad do Nicol Mag Mailisu do chomarba Patric du beith i Saball Patraicc & a tocbail do, & iarna tocbail do ferta & mirbaili mora do denam doib, & a cur do-sam a scrin cumtaig co honorach iar sin.
Mor ingen Fedlimid Conchobair.

Tresna holcaib-sin tanic milled Connacht

Calann Enair for Aine & sechtmad fichet
Murcertach mac Magnusa Conchobair int adbar rig is ferr do bai do Connachtaib, do marbad le Tadcc mac Andrias & la Domnall mac Taidc, & becan da muintir do marbad maille ris.
Aed mac Eogain Conchobair do denam crech ar Clainn Murcertaig.
Maelsechlainn Flannacan toisech Clainni Cathail do marbad do Chathal mac Taidc Meic Diarmata ar srait Slicig isin bliadain-sin.

Dondchad Mac Con Snama taisich Muintiri Cinaith.

Cathal mac Taidc Meic Diarmata ri Moigi Luirg, in fer rob ferr enech & engnam.

Caislen Slicig do lecad la hAed Conchobair.
Maelruanaid mac Gilla Crist do gabail rige Moigi Luirg.
Int Iarla do gabail do Mac Gerailt & buaidred Erenn uili triasan ngabail-sin.

Calann Enair for Sathurn & ochtmad uathad
Int Iarla cetna do lecad as do Mac Gerailt tre nert Rig Saxan & ar braigtib maithi a cinid fein d'fagbail as do Mac Gerailtt.
Brian mac Aeda Buide meic Domnaill Oicc meic Aeda Meith ri Ceneoil Eogain do marbad le Domnall mac Briain Neill, & ar mor do Gallaib & do Gaidelaib maille ris.
Domnall Cellaig ri Mane do ecc a n-abit manaig leith i manistir Cnuic Muade.
Conn Mac Branan taisech Corca Athclann do marbad le macaib Cellaig & se for lurcc a ech iarna ngaid uad.
Tomaltach Mac Branan do gabail taisechta ina inad iar sin & a marbad la macaib Conallan i ndigail a n-aithrech do marbad do Tomaltach reme-side.
Caislen Maigi Duma & caislen an Baili Nua & caislen Moigi Brecraigi do lecad la Sefraid Fergail.
Cocad mor etir Ri Franc & Ri Saxan.
Cocad mor i Tir Conaill.
Braigdi Briain Mec Samradan & Gilla Isa Meg Dorchaid do gabail do Gilla Isa Raigillig.
Calann Enair for Domnach & noemad c vi;
Aed mac Eogain Conchobair do aithrigad da oirecht fein & Clann Murcertaig do thabairt isin tir ina inad & cennus in tire & a braigti do tabairt do Conchobar Ruad mac Cathail Ruaid Conchobair & in tir uile do milled etir cill & tuaith tresan athrigad-sin do denam doib.
Crich Cairbri uli do loscad & do milled do Chlainn Murcertaig & dol doib fo templaib in tire, & do digail Dia & Colum Cille & Mure isa tempaill do saraiged ann sin in gnim-sin forra and sin.
Dala immorro Aeda Conchobair do tinol-side sluag mor do Gallaib & do Gaidelaib fo Uilliam a Burc & fo Teboit a Burc co tancatur co manistir na Builli, & batur ceithri haidchi inti & ro millset arbanna & imenna in tiri co ler, & tancatar toisig an tiri uli ina tech ann sin & rucsat leo iad co tech in Iarla do denam sithai fri hAed Conchobair, & gero gellsat niro comailset in sith, & do aentaigsit aris ar techt da tig re Clainn Murcertaig.
Dala Aeda Conchobair iar sin tanicc isna Tuathaib & tuc Fergail & Mag Ragnaill cona n-imercechaib les & do chuir techta dochum Meic Diarmata & docum Flannacan, & impait-sin isin tir lasna techtaib-sin.
in tan atchonnairc Conchobar Ruad int impad-sin do len iat & dorone creich forro iar sin.
Impait-sim a toraigecht na creiche & berit fuirri
Aed Conchobair cona sluag & a tinol do denam crech mor ndigla for Clainn Murcertaig in la cetna-sin.
Lochlainn mac Conchobair do dallad doib iar sin & a ecc d'uthur in dalta-sin.
Gilla Isu mac an Liathanaig espoc Oli Finn i r Rus Coman aidchi ria mac Beltaini & a adlacad hi manistir na Builli.

in monasterio canonicorum Fontis Patricii.

Calann Enair for Mairt & dechmad fichet
Conchobar mac Taichlig meic Diarmata meic Conchobair meic Diarmada meic Taidc ri Muigi Luirc & Artig, sinserbrathair & tigerna Muintiri Maelruanaid uli, fer rob ferr cor & commarci, gal & gasced, troit & tachor, indsaigid & anad, din & termond, firinne & flaithemnus ina amsir fein, & a adlacad a manestir na Builli i lleba a athar & a senathar.

Uilliam Dubthaig espoc Cluana do marbad d'escur ar tuitim da ech.
luagad le hEdubart Ri Saxan isin Fraincc co muirn & co mormenmain, & tanic asti cin tren cin tresi don duladsin.
Mailsechlainn Mac Briain abb na Builli do gabail espocoiti Oli Finn & Marian Donnabair do toga reme-side, & a dola do Roim a n-imchosnam na hespocoiti & a ecc don turas-sin.
Ulad h. Anluain & a derbrathair & Aengus Mag Mathgamna & moran do maithib a muintiri do marbad do Gallaib Duna Delcan ic impad doib on Iarla isin bliadain cetna-sin.

Calann Enair for Mairt uathad mac
Nicol Mag Mail Isa ardespoc Aird Macha, int aenclerech is diada degeinche do bi a n-Erinn ina amsir fein.

Donnchad Flannacan ab na Builli do gabail espocoiti Oli Finn iarom.
Diarmait Flannacan taisech Tuaithi Ratha & a da mac maille ris do marbad do muintir Domnaill meicc Andrias Conchobair, & daine maithi eli da muintir maille ris, ar techt do denam creichi i Carpri doib.
Toirrdelbach Domnaill ri Tiri Conaill do marbad la hAed n Domnaill a derbrathair fein & daine imdo amaille ris Murcertach Mag Lochlainn & Donnchad Cathan & Dondchad Mac Menman mac in Fir Leginn Domnaill & Niall mac Neill Buigill & Mac Ugosa & a mac & a derbbrathair & Addam Cendal.
Gaill & Gaidil imdo eli maille riu-sin do marbad ann beus.

Teboit a Burc derbbrathair an Iarla do ecc i Carraic Fergusa aidchi Notlac iar techt don tsluagad-sin.

Cocad mor etir Aed mac Eogain Conchobair Ri Connacht & maithi t-Sil Muredaig maille ris & Aed mac Cathail Conchobair co moran do macaib rig & taisech Connacht mar oen ri, co toisechaib & co n-orechtaib na Brefne & cona hairechtaib archenai, iman Sinainn fria re tri mis no a cethair, co ndernatur drem do macaib rig Aedo meicc Cathail forbais isna Tuathaib mar oen re sochraiti moir, cur gabsat crecha mora & airgne, & toir mor do breith forra.
Flann mac Fiachrach Flainn damna toisig Sil Mailruain & Brian mac Dondchada Riabaig Conchobair mar oen ria doinib imdo aili do marbad for lurg na creichi don toir; moran d'fastad dona crechaib-sin & blad eli dib do breith ass.
Is iat tra ba ferr do bai arna crechaib-sin Ruaidri mac Cathail Conchobair & Dondchad mac Conchobair in Copain meic Fergail meic Dondchada meic Murcertaig Meic Diarmata adbar rig Moigi Luirg ar ad & ar enech & ar engnam connice in laithi-sin.
Is ed rani rem Isin co longport Conchobair & loscis pailiss Rig Connacht mar aen re tigib in longphuirt.

Donnchad Mumnech Cellaig ri Mane, sai coitchenn d'feraib Erenn uli im biad & im etach & im or & im ellach, do ecc iar mbreith buaid o deman & o doman, & Tadc Cellaig a mac-side do ecc iarom.
Lurint Lachtnan abb Esa Ruaid & abb na Builli athaid eli, & ab Cnuic Muaide iar sin & espoc Cilli Meic Duach fo deoid.
Conchobar mac Fiacra Flainn, duine occ ba ferr cocad & fogail ar Gallaib a n-aenamsir fris fein da rabi do Connachtaib uili, do ec & a adlacad a manistir na Builli co huasal onorach mar oen ria a brathair.
Echdruim Maine do loscad la dreim do Manechaib, da macaib rig budein.
Goill Rosa Coman uili do marbad le Dondchad Mumnech Cellaig sel rena ecc fein, a n-Ath Escrach Cuan do sundrad, du a torchair Pilip Munter & Maidiu Driu mar oen re etir marbad & gabail, ait inar gabad Serriam Rosa Coman & Diarmait Gall Mac Diarmata & Cormac Mac Cethernaig, & ro leced a sochraite as beuss & ro leced iat fein ar trill, & doronsatt sith ar son an baili do loscad le hEmann Buitiller iar sin.
Edubart Mor Ri Saxan & Bretan & Alban & Duice na Gascune & tigerna na hErend isin coiced bliadain ar fichit a flaithiusa & isin sesed bliadain sescat a aise.
Coroin Rig Saxan & Bretan & Erenn & Alban do thabairt d'Edubard mac Edubairt iar sin.
Dondchad Flannacan abb na Builli fri re mbliadan & espoc Oli Find fria re tri mbliadan co leth, feichem coitchenn craibdech cridechair Iarthair Eorpa uli, fer nar er dam na deoraid & nar imderg nech riam fa biad na fa mainib, cend congbala comarci & cadais in coicid co coitchenn, fer lan do gais & do glicus & do cosnam cacha caingne fa tabrad a lam, fer dercach dadcridech, fer sochraid sochartanach, fer bulid binnbriathrach se milla macaemda macachta, iar mbuaid ongtha & aithrigi & treblaiti re hed mis, Kalendis Iuilii.
Domnall mac Taidc meic Briain meic Andriasa meic Briain Luignig meic Toirrdelbaig Moir Conchobair taniste Connacht uili & in damna rig dopo mo toice & conach, dop ferr enech & engnam & ba ferr enech & flaithemnus & ropo mo ferannas boi a Connachtabi sic, ar rop e fed a feraind o Corrsliab na Segsa co Cael Usce, do marbad ar imruagad la hAed mac Brefnech mac Cathail Ruaid Conchobair; & is e ros gon Diarmait mac Simoin na Traga; & ros gab Dia he, ar ro bi se beo in aidchi-sin & tarraid sacart he & corp Crist & ongad & atbath mochrach arnamarach; & rucad ann sin e docum in Chorrslebi, & ni ruccad isin amsir-sin le duine marb comet a rucad d'almaib & d'eitib & d'indilib, do marcsluagaib & do chosigib & do cheternaib leis dochum a chilli; & do adlaiced e i manistir na Builli iar tain co huasal onorach.
Tadc mac Mailsechlainn meic Dondchada meic Domnaill meic Magnusa meic Toirrdelbaig Moir Conchobair do marbad le Cathal mac Domnaill meic Taidc Conchobair.

Aed mac Eogain meic Ruaidri meic Aeda meic Cathail Crobdeirg ri Connacht & adbur Rig Erenn ar uasli & ar engnam & ar enech, ar delb & ar denam, do marbad la hAed mac Brefnech mac Cathail Ruaid Conchobair a Coill in Chlachan i crich Brefne & moran do maithib Connacht maille ris Conchobar Mac Diarmata & Diarmait Ruad mac Taidcc meic Andrias Conchobair & Diarmait mac Cathail Carraig Meic Diarmata & Aed mac Murcertaig meic Taidc meic Mailruanaig.
Diarmaid Occ hElide flaithbrugaid fial fostinech, & Maeldomnaig Galloclaech, & Gilla na Naem Mac Aedacan ollam Connacht re fenechas & sai coimdes coitchenn in cech cerd archena do toitim don lucht soir isin lo cetna, & Fagurtach Dobailen do lucht tigi Tomaltaig Meic Dondchada, & daine imdo aili maille friu-sin, & nir luga ina cet a n-esbaid diblinaib.
Aed Brefnech do tocht isin tir iar sin & na Tri Tuatha do techt ina tech.
Imthusa Mailruanaig Meic Diarmata rig Moigi Luirc doberar os aird sunna coleicc.
Tanic-side cona toichim teglaig ina timchell ar larmedoin Sila Muredaig do cosnam rigi & oirechais da dalta d'Fedlimid Conchobair, & do chuir techta dochum a charad Gall & Gaidel ar cech leth uad & d'indsoigid Uilliam Burc cona braithrib, & tanic-side co tindesnach risin techtairecht-sin; & do suidestur ar Fiad Ratha Cruachan co setrech sirchalma a mesc imircech an tiri da tathugad ar ecla & ar oman na n-orecht-sin d'aentugad re hAed mac Brefnech mac Cathail, & do gab fein tigernus na toisech & orlamus na n-oirrigh & do thabaig se a cis & a coranna & a chanachus, & fos ro thabaig seta fine & flathai rig Connacht uili, & tucsad Sil Muredaig uili a lughedha & a ndaingen na tibradais a tigernus do neoch aili; & tanicc Uilliam Burc iar sin mar oen ria Sil Muredaigh co hOil Find.
Dala Aeda meic Cathail immorro dochuaid i coinni in Iarla isin Mide, & do impaset na Tri Thuatha fair dia es, & ar techt d'Aed asin Mide do suidestair ind Uachtar Tiri & dorone creich mor ar Aedh Flannacan iar sin & ro chaithistur in creich-sin ina longport fein i nd Uachtar Tiri.

Conne do denam do mac Cathail & do Macc Uilliam Burcc fo Ath Slisen & brised conni do techt eturro & maidm do thabairt ar mac Cathail & drem da muintir do marbad and sin.
Uilliam Burc do dol co manistir na Builli iar sin & Clann Murcertaig do techt a Tir n-Oilella iar sin & arbur imdo do loscad & do milled doib.
Mac Uilliam do dol tar Sliab sis & mac Cathail do chur asa longpurt do, & Dondchad Findachta do marbad do tosach sluaig Meic Uilliam & daine eli nach arimther sund.
Crech do denam la Mac Uilliam ar Clainn Fermoigi & crech eli leis co Beind Gulpan & tarsi bud thuaid.

Endecas.
Tanaide Maelconaire ollam Sil Muredaigh Muillethain meic Fergusa re filidecht & senchus do ecc i tosach na bliadna-sa isin errach cruaid.
Crech mor frisi n-aburti Crec in Toten do denam d'Oed Brefnech mac Cathail Conchobair ar Maelruanaig Mac n-Diarmata a Clochar Murgili, & Dondchad mac Dondchada Meic Diarmata do gabail ann & a ben ingen Flannacan do marbad ann beuss; mna & lenim & daine imdo eli do marbad & do loscad ann beus & longpurt do gabail doib a n-Uachtar Tiri re hucht Meic Diarmata & t-Sila Muredaig.
O'tchuala Uilliam Burcc in ni-sin do gab longpurt hi Cill Lomat ar inchib Aeda meic Cathail.
Is ann sin ro chuir Aed mac Cathail techta co hinchlethe uad dochum a brathar Ruaidri meic Cathail do rada ris maille rena fedain dol co caislen Bona Finde tar es Uilliam Burcc da facbail.
Dala Ruaidri immorro & Aed meic Magnusa & muintiri Aeda Brefnig do tinolsad diblinaib & do aircsid & do loiscsed caislen Bona Finne cone uili maithes.
Dala Aeda meic Cathail is amlaid ro bai-side in tan-sin & cethern congbala do buanadaib ina fochair aca comed Seonacc Mac Uidilin cend congbala na ceithirne-sin.
o'tconnairc se mac Conchobair co huaicnech d'es a muintiri do dol uada ar sibal Bona Finne, arna cocur reme sin & ar ngellad a marbtha d'Ulliam Burc do chind luaigi, do edestar he fein in tan-sin cona muintir, & marbthar Aed Brefnech mac Cathail Ruaid Conchobair ann sin, int aenmac rig as ferr bai a n-Erinn ina amsir fein, da ndeonaiged Dia do
O ranicc immorro fis marbtha Aeda Brefnig dochum Uilliam Burc & dochum Meic Diarmata & t-Sila Muredaig archena co Cill Lomat, do gluaisetar a cetoir for crechaib dochum muintiri Aeda Brefnig & do lecsid a sirthe co Bendan Brechmaigi fo thuaid & co Mag Cedne na Fomorach, & impoais Uilliam Burc iar sin na fritheing co larmeodon Sila Muredaig & coindmis da cet sersenach forra Mac Uigilin cona ruta, & ni raibi baili i Sil Muredaig uli cen gnathbuana, na tuath cin tabach, na flaith cin forrach, re hed urrlamais Uilliam Burc forra tar es Aeda.
O'tconnairc Maelruanaid Mac Diarmata a dalta arna dilsiugad foa duthaig & truma thabaig cache tuaithi ina timchell, & ro mothaig co mor Gaill oca cengal dochum becnerta, ar ba demin le Gallaib da mbad anfand e-sim 'na aenar comad leo fein coiced Connacht co comlan fa a commas, & is hi comuirli ar ar cind in cungid a dalta do degtocbail & a rigad ar ecin, & rucustur leis he co Carn Fraich meic Fidaich & do rigustur arin carn he do rer nois na naem & Daconna Esa do sundrad, amail is rigda & is airechda & is linmairi do rigad aenduine da cined fein o re Briain meic Echach Muidmedoin anuas cosin laithi-sin Fedlimid mac Aedo meic Eogain.
ar feis d'Feidlimid mac Aeda meic Eogain re coiced Connacht doronne a oiti a frithhailem an odchi-sin do rer cumne na seduine & na senleeabar, & is Isin banais rige is oiregdo doronad a Connacht riam cusan laithi-sin.

Calann Enair for Cetain & ochtmad fuirri, v;
Edubard mac Roberd Briuis Iarla Cargi do toidecht dochum Erenn ar orer Ulad bud thuaid, lucht long a lin, cur combuaidir & cur crithnaig a idna aig & irgaili Eriu uile co coitchenn etir Gall & Gaidel, & ro aircc a cetoir forcla Ulad & ro loisc Raith Mor Muigi Line & Dun Delgan & do marb a ndaine, & do loisc Ath Fir Diadh meic Daman iar sin & du gab se braigti & tigernus Chuicid Ulad uili cin fresabra, & do deonaigsidur a gairm do thabairt ina Rig Erenn & do aentaigset Gaidil Erenn a tigernus do tabairt do & do goiretar Ri Erenn de.
O'tchualaid Risdert a Burc Iarla Ulad Eduuard aca indsoidig do thinoil sluag mor as cech aird ina comdail cu Ros Comman ar tus acus as-side co hAth Luain & ar fiarlaid na Mide & Muige Breag, acus Feidlim Conchobair Ri Condacht maille fris acus timchall fhichet cath a comairem; & nir chaicletar Gaill don dulad-sin naem na neimed da neimnige, na cill na tuath na termann, cen cnam & cen commilled ar fiarlait Erenn o Sinaind bu deas co Cul Rathain bud thuaid & co hInis Eogain; acus o rancatar ar aenconair in imricci adbal aensluaiged-sin cu Bregaib atchondchadur cuco ina comdail Emand Butiller Giustis na hErenn tricha cath comcengailti arna comarem don cur-sin, & ro thormisc int Iarla a tocht-sin ina toichim & ina tinol, ar ba doich leis he fein cona sluag do dichor Alpanach a hErinn; & is ann bai ant Iarla an adaich-sin a n-Ath Fir Diad re taeb Slebi Breg & Edubard a Briuis mar oen fria hUltaib & Albanachaib ag Inis Cain meic Dega, & dasiacht int Iarla arabarach ina ndiaid & do ghab sosad & longport hic Lugmag, acus docuaid Uilliam Burc d'fagbail eluime ar Edubard cona Albanachaib ann sin & do mmarbad uathad etarru ann sin.
Imtusa Etuuard cona fhedain, tre fhurail Neill & Ulad arcena do gluais remii arabarach ar uidedaib imthechta co Cul Rathain fo thuaid & co horer Indsie Eogain & ro leagsat droichet Cula Rathain re hadaig an Iarla, & lenais int Iarla iat & gabais longport a Cul Rathain ar inchib Ulad & Edubart imon abaind, conar facaibset diblinaib coill na machaire na gort na gemur na sosad na saball na cill cin dod & cin loscad.
Uair nirbo comsich cummaiscc no cathaigti na sluaig-sin re 'roili, oir do bi an Banna bruthmur borbdomain oca n-etrain; acht aenni, do bitis debtha dermara eturro adiu & anall imon abaind cech lai.
o'tchuala Edubard febas Feidlim Conchobair Rig Connacht do chuir fesa falaig da indsaigid do thaircsin Connacht cin comrainn fora comus & hetlod do on Iarla do cosnam in cuicid cetna, & do eist Fedlim na fuigli-sin co foditnech & ro aentaig re hEdubard.
Imtusa Ruaidri meic Cathail Ruaid Conchobair, o'tconnairc Connachta arna folmugad do gluais uathad d'agallaim Edubaird co Cul Rathain ar fiarlait Ceneoil Conaill sair & do gell se d'Edubard an tan-sin co ndichuirfed uad Goill o cennuse onnacht, & do deonaig Edubard do iarsin cagad do denam ar Gallaib & cen fogail ar Feidlim na imthecht a feraind.
Ni hed sin dorone Ruaidri acht ro tinol Condachtaig & Brefnig & galloclaich imdo maille riu & ro indsaig co certlar Sila Muredaig & Connacht arcena, & do loisc a cetoir sratbaili Slicig & Ath Cliath in Coraind & caislen mor Chilli Chalman & Baili Topair Brigti & Dun Imdan cona chaislen & Ros Coman & Rind Duin & Ath Luain mar oen risna huilib tigibh batur in cech conair dar imdig, & ro sir se tend & tigernus ar Mac n-Diarmata iar sin & ni fuair giall na heteri uad, & ro gab geill & braigti Sil Muredaig archena & fos do rigsad he for Carn Fraich meic Fidaig iar sin, & ro bi ac furech etir Sil Muredaig and sein re hed & re hathaig ag cnam cach comursann ina timchell narbat riaraig do & fos ac furech re fathaib Feidlim & in tsluaig boi i n-Ulltaib ina fochair.
Imtusa Feidlim Conchobair Ri Connacht o'tcuala Ruadri 'na rigeing docum Connacht do cosnam rigi do fein, do tuic mar tarla da turus do & do innis don Iarla co ngebad Ruaidri cnaim cocaidh da eisi ina ferann, & fagbais int Iarla co teindesnach & tanicc dochum Connacht da cosnam; & ni socair fuair-sim na sligti reme, uair ni rabi aenla cin creich no can cath fiarlait Ulad & Oirgiall, noco ranaicc co Granard & co Coill na n-Amus & co sochraiti Seain Fergail derbrathair a mathar, ait ar dithaiged a daine & ar n-etlad a n-etala uada-san cona fedain & do cetaig da taisichaib & da oirrigaib batur ina fochair arin tsluagad tuaithbil-sin a n-inad fein d'indsaigid & dol doib docom rigi Ruaidri resiuu no betis ar aneol ana fochair-sim: ' Uair mad tren dam-sa arithisi beti-se acam; acht aenni, o nach insitha m'oti-si & Ruaidri re'roili bemitt ar aenconair ar ndis re hed ar cocaid.
Imtusa inn Iarla & Uilliam Burcc & na n-Gall archena.
O nach facatur Feidlimid occa furtacht, & a sluag fein ar fainnseol, ro impotur ara n-ais o Cuil Rathain co Caislen Conderi.
O'tcondcatur Ultaig & Alpanaig in ni-sin do lensat co tindesnach ant Iarla co Connderi & ar comriachtain doib docum troda do thabairt da cheli do gabad Uilliam Burcc cona ritirib ann sin & da mac Meic in Miled, & ro teith ant Iarla fein cin furich ar uidedaib imthechta otha sin co ranicc a Connachtaib; & ro indsaigseatt a cardi Gall do cech leth int Iarla ar toidecht do a ndochas an Iarla da fortacht & da forigtin, & tancatur a chardi Gaidel a n-aenfecht ina tech an tan-sin mar in cetna, & is iatt ba ferr tanicc ann Fedlim Conchobair Ri Connacht & Murcertach Briain ri Tuadmuman & Maelruanaid Mac Diarmata ri Muintiri Maelruanaid & Gillibert Cellaig ri Mane, iarna ndichur on duthaig uili; & o'tconnaircc Mac Diarmata imat na n-athrig & na n-indarptach i n-aentig do gab nari e, & tucc da breithir nach aremtha he fein mar athrig a n-aentig doridisi, acht do rachad rea oirbert fein ina tir duthchais amail do torberad in toice do, & tanicc ar inchib Taidc Cellaig & doroinne Tadg cosmailes sida do re Ruaidri do cinn a duthaigi & braigti do thabairt do Ruaidri mac Cathail do-som.
Aed Ballach mac Magnusa meic Conchobair Ruaid meicc Murcertaig Mumnig do marbad a fill la Cathal mac Domnaill Conchobair & Aed mac Airt & Diarmait mac Simoin na Traga do marbad doib beus a ndigail a n-athar do marbad do Diarmaid.
Crecha mora do denam do clainn Domnaill ar Clainn Murcertaig arabarach & Magnus mac Magnusa & Domnall mac Magnusa do marbad le clainn Domnaill ar lorg na creichi-sin, & Tomaltach Mac Dondchada do gabail fos don lucht cetna-sin, & imthecht doib a n-ucht Gall d'es na n-echt-sin do commaidem.
O'tchuala Feidlim Conchobair na hechta mora-sin do gluais uathad da aes grada mar a rabatur clann Domnaill Conchobair Ruaidri & Magnus, Cathal & Murcertach, Dondchad & Seoan, meic Domnaill meic Taidc Conchobair, mar oen rea mbraithrib archena; & o tharraid a taris Isin dorone creich moir ar Brian Dubda a cetoir, & fos dorone creich moir aile and Artich ar Diarmait n-Gall mac n-Diarmata, & do marb moran da muintir & do loisc a arbanna & a tigi, & fos doroine creich aili a cetoir ar clainn Cathail Flannacan; & is i conair a rucad an crech-sin dochum Carad Chula Cuir, & nir fedad a himain re maithi na mona & re linmairi & re truime na tora.
Oir rucsat forcla glaslaithi na Tuath & forcla clainni Cathail fuirri
o'tconnairc Mac Diarmata comairc na creiche docom na Carad ro len lorg na creichi co Cull Bathur & atconnaircc in creich arna cuitichad & arna fastad, oir ni he sin rop ail leosam acht gan a faccbail oca fiadnaib, & ro fech ara hescardib co hanniarda urbadach & tucc tar & tarcusal forra cerbo huathad ina farrad, & o'tconnairc an laem lethan lasamain lanimda do bai ar comair na troda da thornem.

Imtusa Ruaidri o'tcuala na crecha & na hechtasin do denam do Mac Diarmata & a dola ar aenseol rena dalta, dorone tinol co tindesnach & doroine foslongport i mac Bali Mor Flainn, & ro mill cadus Qilli Athrachta & Esa Da Conna & manistrech na Builli & na n-eclais archena fo ellach & arbannaib.

is ann sin dochuaid Diarmait Gall ar Cruachan.
Tanicc Tadc Cellaig fos in tan-sin cona sochraite hi furtacht Ruaidri meic Cathail do lenmain a slanaigechta ar Mac n-Diarmata ar coilled a caingne re Ruaidri, & dochuadar diblinaib i llenmain Feidlim & Meic Diarmata & na n-oirecht bai ina fochair co Letir Lugne & co slesaib Slebi Gam & co Glend Fathraim do sondrad, ait anar marbadar ilmili do buaib & cairaib & do chaiplib, & do nochtadur mna uasli & do millset lenib beca & mindaine don turus-sin, & nir milled re cumne daine riam in ured-sin d'ellach ar aenlathair cin tarba.
Imtusa Maelruanaig Meic Diarmata o'tchuala Diarmait Gall do suidi a cathair chadusa a cinid & hi Carraicc Lochaa Ce & a cur for Cruachan da rigad, & ar n-orlech a bo fein a n-Glind Fathraim, do gluais cona lucht tige & cona teglach budein co Calad na Cairrci, & tucustur druim re Sinainn & ro aircestur o Sinaind co Caraid, ait a rabatur oirechta na Tri Ciarraigi Ciarraigi Iatharach & Ciarraigi Moigi Ai & Ciarraigi Artig cona n-ellaigib uli & cona n-indilib, & ni doig co ndernadh isin amsir-sin indsaigid bad croda & bad mo edal ina in crech-sin.
Uair ro crithnaig an coiced co comlan & bos rucad ben Diarmata Gall i cimidecht isin creich-sin co n-uathad da bantrachtaib amailli ria, & nir gab Diarmait same na sescurecht riam dar es na creichi-sin; & fos do indised d'Feidlimid Conchobair & da oiti ba do beith a Moig Luirg tar es na creichi-sin & dochodur da n-iarraid & do aircsid a fuaradur do buaib & d'eachaib i Moig Luirg, & fuair Diarmait Gall robad rompa don chur-sin & nirbo tarba do.
Cerbo trom a toir & a tinol aracind nir facaibsed a creich & ba faen falam Mag Luirg uli o sin amach.
Uair ni rabi din na diten i termand cilli na tuaithi inti, acht a hellach & a harbar do fuatach ona haltorib & a tabairt do galloclaechaib na ndligtinus.

Ricard a Clara.
Edubard a Briuis fer millti na hErenn uli co cotcend etir Gallaib & Gaidilaib do marbad la Gallaib Erenn tria nert cathaigti & crodacht oc Dun Delgan, & Mac Ruaidri ri Innsi Gall & Mac Domnaill ri Oirir Gaedeal do marbad mar oen ris and maille re n-Albanchaib maille Et ni dernad o thus domain, o do dichured Fine Fomra a hErinn, gnim bad ferr d'feraib hErenn uli ina in gnim-sin.

Echmarcach Mac Branan
Corca Athclann do marbad Tomaltaig Mailbrenaind, & Echmarcach fein do dol da gonaib tres la da esi sin.
Domnall Neill ri Tiri hEogain d'indarba asa rigi & asa flaithes tre nert Gall & Clainni Aeda Buide, & crecha mora do denam la Feraib Manach a fell fair.
A rigi fein do gabail do aridisi.
Brian mac Domnaill Neill do marbad le Clainn Aeda Buide.

Conne mor etir Chathal Conchobair & Maelruanaig Mac Diarmada co ndernsat sid cunnail cardemail, & Mac Diarmata do thecht isin tir iar sin.
Fell do denam don Chathal cetna-sin ar Mac n-Diarmada ar Mullach Doramnach & a gabail and, & Grane ingen Meic Magnusa ben Meic Diarmada do gabail a Purt na Carrgi, & in tir do lomarcain iar sin, & Mael Isa Dond Macc Aedacan & a mac & Tomaltach Mac Dondchada tigerna Tiri Oilella do gabail and fos.
Aed mac Taidcc Conchobair degadbur Rig Connacht ar delb & ar denam & ar uasli & ar enech do marbad do Mac Martin, & a marbad fein ina digail.
Mathgamain mac Domnaill Connachtaig Briain tanaiste Muman do marbad do Clainn Culen.
Mor ingen Baigill ben Fergail.

viii; CB.
Mailsechlainn O Raigillig tigerna Muintiri Mailmorda do gabail & do lot do Gallaib na Mide & a fuaslacad ar braigdib & a dol d'ecc da gonaib ina tig fein iar sin.
Tornech & tentich anbail isin bliadain-sin, gur milled moran do mes & do torad Erenn uli, & cur fasadur arbanna finna fasa.
Teidm galair co coitchenn ar fud Erenn uili frisi nabarthai slaedan re hed tri la no cethair ar cech nech da ngabad, gur bo tanaiste bais do hee.
Int Iarla Donn do techt a n-Erinn Uilliam Burc mac Sir Seoan meic inn Iarla Ruaid.
Dondchad Ruad Gadra & cocer da cined fein maille ris
Conchobar Mac Branan adbar taisig Corca Athchlann do marbad la Muintir Angaili.
Daibed Mac Gilla Comgain galloclaech & cethri fir da muintir maille ris do marbad la Dondchad n-Gall mac Domnaill Conchobair, & Dondchad fein do tromlot andd beuss.
Dubesa ingen Elide ben Domnaill meic Andrias, an ingen macoclaich is ferr do bi a n-aenamsir fria & dob ferr clu & dobo mo conach, do ecc isin bliadain-sin.
Gaeth mor dofulachta isin tsamrad & terca bid & imad etaig.
Crech mor la Uater a Burc ar Connachtaib cur harced moran leis d'aes grada Toirrdelbaig Conchobair Rig Connacht.
Sir Seon Mac Feorais Iarla Lugmaig ant aenbarun doba beoda & dobo brigmure & dob ferr enech & dopo mo tindlaicti do bi a n-Erinn, do marbad a fill da muintir fein do Gallaib Oirgiall, & moran do Gallaib & do Gaidelaib maithi do marbad mar oen ris.
Ri na Senma Maelruanaid Mac Cerbaill in Gilla Caech & derbrathair aili do marbad mar oen ris, & ni fes co tani na co ticcfa choidchi a commaith do timpanach.
Muris Gibillan ardmagestir Erenn a ndliged nua & a sendliged, hi Canoin & i lex, fellsom fesa & fireoluis, sai ndana & n-ogmorachta & eladan n-imda eli, Canonach corad hi Tuaim Da Gualann & a n-Oil Find & a n-Achad Conari & i Cill Alaid & a n-Enach Duin & i Cluain Ferta Brenaind, Oificel & Brethem coitchend na hardespocoiti.
Tomas Mellaig espoc Enaig Duin do ecc hi cuirt an
Brian mac Tomaltaig Meic Dondchada do marbad do Brian mac Taidc Meic Dondchada.
Uilliam Iarla Ulad do tinol tsluaig moir fa Toirrdelbach Conchobair Ri Condacht & ba Murcertach m Briain ri Tuadmuman & Muman archena, a n-agaid Briain Bain Briain.
Maidm le Brian mac Ban O mac Briain ar Ua mac Briain, du anar marbad Conchobar Briain degadbar Rig Erenn ar met & deilb & ar enech, maille re cethri fichit etir maith & saith.
Condi mor fa Ath Cind Locha Deichet etir Uater mac Uilliam Burc & Gilliberd Mac Gosdelb don dara leith & Maelruanaid Mac Diarmata & Tomaltach a mac & Tomaltach Mac Dondchada & Clann Maelruanaid archena don dara leith.
Bresimh madma do thabairt ar Mac Uilliam dar marbad Brian mac Taidg Meic Dondchada lea brathair fein a ndigail Briain mac Tomaltaig Meic Dondchada do marb-som reme-sin.

tanicc milled Gall Condacht & a chinid fein trit-sin.
do gab Toirrdelbach Conchobair nert Connacht iar sin & do hinnarbad Emann mac Uilliam Burcc a Connachtaib amach & do milled tuatha & cella Iarthair Connacht uli; & ro tinol Emand a Burc coblach mor do longaib & do barcaib ro bai ar olenaib na farrci re hed ciana.
Lugni & in Corand do folmagad & do fassugad & a tigernus do gabail da n-Gaidelaib duthcusa budein ar ndichur a n-Gall esib.

Comtocbail cocaid moir etir Manechaib etir Tadc mac Taidc Cellaig, da tucc Toirrdelbach Conchobair urlamus Mane, & Uilliam mac Dondchada Mumnig Cellaig, cur cured Uilliam mac Dondchada Mumnig asin tir amach, & ro lensat uli e cur impo Uilliam friu & cur marbad Donnchad mac Aeda Cellaig & cur gabad Tadc Cellaig & cur loted, & a ecc da lot iarom.

Clann Ualgairg Ruairc Domnall & Aed & Gilla Crist & Ruaidri do dol ar creich dochum Cathail meic Aeda Brefnig, & doronsat creich lanmoir & do marbad Conchobar mac Dondchada Riabaig meic Magnusa meic Murcertaig Mumnig leo in la-sin & moran aili maille ris; & is i-sin cetfola Muintiri Ruairc & clainni Murcertaig Mumnig meic Toirrdelbaig Moir; & dorone Cathal mac Aeda Brefnig in toraigechd croda iar sin, dar fostad moran don creich & dar marbad Domnall Ruairc aenraga mac rig na Brefni uili & dar gabad Gillacrist Ruairc & Mac Consnama & dar marbad moran eli ann fos.
Tadc mac Ruaidri meic Cathail Conchobair do bi a llaim ac Ruairc do lecon amach ar comfuaslacad & Gilla Crist Ruaircc.
Aed mac Fedlimid Conchobair do gabail la Toirrdelbach Conchobair ri Connacht & a cur a Caislen Rosa Coman da comet.
Cocad mor & esaenta adbal do ergi etir Conchobair & Mac Diarmata triasan gabail-sin & cur milled moran eturra diblinaib.
Guasacht mor d'fagbail d'O Chonchobair o Mac Diarmata isin Corand cur cuired da aindeoin e astech a mac Bali in Muta; & sid do denam doib asa haithli-sin re cheli.

cuit do galloclaechaib Conchobair do marbad doib fan constapla fa Mac Ruaidri.

Fell granna do denam ar Clainn Uilliam Burc tre forgall Conchobair, dar marbad Tomas a Burc le Clainn Muris & se ana n-oirechtus fein, & Seonin a Burc do marbad arin asti cetna le Clainn Ricairt.

Fergal mac Gilla Crist Finn Meic Cormaic do marbad arin cocad cetna-sin.
Bresim brogda da thabairt do Mac Diarmata & da macaib rig ar Conchobair a mac Beol Atha Slisen, dar linged ant ath fair & dar marbad and Diarmait mac Briain Fergail fer a aisi fein is ferr do bai do Chonmaicnib uile, & mac Hoberd a Burc & Conchobar mac Dondchada Duib Elide.
Seoan Mag Mathgamna sai n-enig & n-engnama, ri Orgiall, do dola ar creich dochum Roailb Meg Mathgamna & a marbad cona galloclaechaib ar dered a creichi, & is commor do marbad & do baided iad.
Cormac mac Ruaidri meic Domnaill Conchobair do gabail le Conchobar mac Taidc & le Ruaidri mac Cathail Conchobair isin bliadain cetna-sin, & Conchobar do gabail le Brian mac Ruaidri & a thabairt a laim Conchobair Meic Diarmata & a cor do iar sin arin Carraic da comed.
Domnall Dochurtaig taisech Arda Midair, sai n-enig & n-engnama, derci & doennachta, do ecc ina tig fein, & Seoan Dochurtaig do gabail a inait da esi.
Sil Muiredaig uile itir deoin & aimhdeoin do dilsigudh Rig Connacht Toirrdelbaig meic Aoda mic Eogain Chonchobair, & is iat is oiregda ro erig do in tan-sin Emund mac Uilliam Burc & Conchobar Mac Diarmata ri Moigi Luirg cona brathrib & cona oirecht uili, Aed mac Aodu Brefnig mic Cathail Ruaid hI Chonchobair, Tadg mac Ruaidri Chonchobair, & Cathal mac Oeda Brefnig mic Cathail Ruaid, & sochraide Brefne & Conmaicne, & Aed mac Fedlim meic Aeda meic Eogain; & Toirrdelbach do chur asin tir amach leo uli, mar narb ingnad.
conad i comurli tucsat a charaid do iar sin dol do tig Meic Diarmada isin oidche.
fuaratur Clann Murcertaig fis na comurli-sin & do indlitur reme ar sligtib & ar bernadaib baeguil an longpuirt, & tanicc-sim tarsib sin uili isan adaig redorcha dis no triar marcach, & do erged do ar tochar in longpuirt & dochuaid tarrsa ar tarad a lama laitiri & do loit se Cathal mac Aeda Brefnig, & ni raibi a fiss sin ag Mac Diarmata noco cuala se comairc an mallaigti & in marcnech ar fot an longpuirt chuice, & do erig co hopand & do foir se Conchobair & do chuir daine tarisi leis da chur isin Carraicc; acus do bai forglai sechtmaine inti & do teigdis daine maithe in tire chuce cech lai ar cuairt, acus ni fh uair Mac Diarmata ced sitha fris, & o nach fuair do tindlaic he co caislen Rosa Coman & ro faccaib and sin he.

Toirrdelbach, Mac Subne Ard.
oidchi feli Catrich Fina Banogi isin gemred iar caithem mbliadan & raithe hi lanrigi Connacht, amail forgles an fili Mailin Mailconaire and i nduain in Reme Rigraide:
Fuair Ruaidri, rigda an snaithi, a se dec is degrathi ar Cruachain Ai gan irgail, mac tacharborb Toirrdelbaig.
Da ri do denam ina inat iar sin Toirrdelbach Ruad mac Aeda meic Fedlimid do rigad do Macc Diarmata & do Clainn Murcertaig Mumnig & do taisechaib Connacht archena do thaisichaib Sila Muredaig, ocus Toirrdelbach Occ mac Aeda meic Toirrdelbaig do rigad d'O Chellaig & do Clainn Ricairt & do Domnall mac Murcertaig Conchobair & do Clainn Dondchada.
Cur fas cocad coitcend hi Condachtaib uli iar sin & co ndernsatur uilcc imda & urtha & aircne da esi sin.

Maelruanaid Mac Diarmata
Moigi Luirg do dol an oidchi-sin co manistir na Buille, & a fuair se do biad a manistir na Buille do chor ar Carraig Locha Ce do.
lorg na fedna-sin d'fagbail do Conchobar cona muintir & in lorc do lenmain doib co hEchdruim mac n-Aeda a tir m Briuin na Sinna & tempall Echdroma do loscad forro & Conchobar mac Fergail Meic Diarmata do marbad and, & Maelruanaid Mac Diarmata do gabail ann & moran da muintir do marbad and & a n-eich & a n-etid do bein dib.
Sluagad la Murcertach mac n-Domnaill Conchobair i Tir Aeda Ruaid meic Baduirn dochum Domnaill, & ni rucsat ar edail ann & a n-impod iar sin.
Aed Durnin da lenmain a toraigecht & imruagad do thabairt doib a mac Beol Atha Senaig & ech Aeda do lot & a escur fein di, & tiug an tsluaig do loigi air & a marbad la Clainn Donnchada; & Sean mac Muredaig Ruaid do marbad arin toraigecht-sin.
Loch Farbach do gabail la Ruaidri mac Aeda Meic Diarmata la ridamna Moigi Luirg, & ni deochaid a comarem a frith d'edail air.

a manistir Lethratha a lebaid a athar & a senadur.

o braithrichaib budein.
Morindsaigid la Mac Uilliam Burc & la clainn Cathail Oic for Slicech & in baili do loscad & do lomarcain doib.
Cing Risderd Ri Saxan do tocht a n-Erinn & Art Mac Murchada ri Laigen do beith a n-amnert mor on Rig & o Saxanchaib archena.
Mac Murchada do dol ar indsaigig & Gaill Laigen & na Mide do breith fair & moran do sluag Saxan & cetherna congbala Meic Murchada do marbad and im clainn Donnchada Duind Cerball & Eogan co maithib a muintire maille riu, & Uilliam mac Cerbaill Meic Gilla Patricc & mac Diarmata Ruaid Meic Gilla Patraic do marbad and beuss.
Sluagad la Conchobair Ruad & la Conchobar Mac n-Diarmata ri Moigi Luirc i Tir n-Oilella co rancadur a scemelta co Magh Tured na Fomorach & argni more do gabail doib & a tabairt fo Choilltib Conchobair, & a cethern congbala & a glaslaithi do imtecht lea n-étalaib & Conchobair & Mac Diarmata & Somarli Budi mac Marcusa Meic Domnaill consabla Meic Diarmata do fachail da muintir fein i nd-uathad sluaig.
Murcertach mac Domnaill & Maelruanaid Mac Dondchada ri Tiri hOilella do breith forro cona sochraiti diblinaib i Cnucc in Cromai & a madmachad ann-side, & Somurli Budi cona muintir do marbad i Cnucc in Croma & lam des Conchobair do crechtnugad co mor d'aithius aenorchuir forin sluagad-sin.
Mac Muris Budi Morda, droched dam & deorad Erenn, tigerna Slebi Mairg.
Art Cam Faelan.
Ingen Briain Fergail uxur Ulpis.
Findguala ingen Cathail Madadan.

Fer Cell Februarii.

Dondchad Sinnach tigerna Muintire Tadcan & ri Fer Tethba de iure.

euerunt i Calainn Auguist.

Grigoir mac Tanaide Mailconaire adbur ollaman t-Sila Muredaig Muillethain & sai forbthi ina cerd budein do marbad co tubuisech d'oenbuille gai do laim Uilliam Gairb meic Dauid for tachar Duin Imdain a nd-amricht, & tucad se ba & it bo ina ericc.

Conchobar Mailsechlainn
Medie de iure a tert Calainn April isin Lethinnse Muigi hElli in bona fine.
Murcertach Oc mac Murcertaig Moir Meg Eochacan do marbad i tert Noin Octimbir i mac Beol Atha lmper d'oenurchur gai la Geroit mac Robed Dalutun i comescur oidchi d'es a muintiri do cur uad ar indsaigid isin mac Brenad Muintiri Gillgan.

i n-Almain Laigen o Gallaib in pridie idus Maii.

Cathal Ruad Mag Ragnaill
Muintire hEolais do marbad a n-Druim Cubra le Sefraid mac Mailechlainn Meg Ragnaill hi cind mis d'errach hi
nt noin Marta.
Maelruanaid mac Cathail Ruaid Meg Ragnaill do marbad la clainn Mailsechlainn Meg Ragnaill in bliadain cetna a lurg a creichi.
Da Mac Uilliam do denam dar es Tomais a Burc Mac Uilliam do denam d'Uillec mac Ricairt Oicc & Mac Uilliam eli do denam do Uater mac Tomais a Burc, & a credemain do Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricairt ar sindsirecht.

per dolum la Conchobar mac Seain Meic Branan.

Uilliam Occ hUicinn
clainn Cathail na mac Banfigech Meg Flannchaid etir da abaind

Crecha do denam do clainn Domnaill meic Murcertaig ar Mac n-Diarmada
Carraic Locha Ce do gabail do clainn Fergail Meic Diarmata & daine imda do marbad & do bathad ina timchell, & lucht a comeda da tinnlacad do cind comad.
Fedlimid mac Cathail Oicc Conchobair do marbad do mac Conchobair Duinn.
Gres an Chabain do denam la clainn Ruairc Tigernan Occ & Aed Budi & Tadg, & do clainn Meg Samradan for Maelmorda Raigillig, & foslongpurt ag Muintir Mailmorda ara n-eis, & ni hurusa a arim ar milled and-side do dainib & mainib, & do loisced bert etid ann, fa Mac in Biataid tanicc do congnam la Muintir Raigillig, & do benad dait ech dib beus.
Cocad aduathmur do ergi etir Toirrdelbach mac Neill Gairb meic Aeda Domnaill & ridamna na n-Eoganach Brian mac Enri Amreid Neill, & foslongpurt Clainni Dalaig & Toirrdelbaig meic Neill Gairb tigerna na Conallach d'indsaigid co drochcomarlech dimsach la mac Enri & sraenmaidm sechranach do ben asta do tus lai co latir lanchalma; & mar nach ted olc cin indiched na dal cin digaltus ni dechadur na dala-sin can digaltus co degthapaid o Chenel Conaill; & is amlaid doraladur na dala-sin doib mac Neill d'fagbail i n-huathad sluaig deod lai & crech Enri Garmlegaid remi, & ro benait na crecha-sin de-sim la Cenel Moan; & rob e sin ant aithes co n-anaithes do Chenel Moan, ar ro marb-som mac Garmlegaid d'oenbulli claidib; & asa haithl Isin do iadsad Cenel Conaill uli a timchal in trenmiled & do maided in morecht-sin la Toirrdelbach n Domnaill, & do marbad Niall mac Neill Gairb Domnaill & Maelsechlaind mac Flaithbertaig Ruairc tus an lai-sin la hEoganchaib & dobo lanmor a n-esbada o sin amach, acht nach roich a n-arem uli ar oman an emiltis.
Calann Enair for Domnach & fuirri, mii;
Cocad adbalmor etir Iarla Urmuman & Iarla Desmuman & in da Mac Uilliam do dol diblinaib do furtacht Iarla Urmuman.
Fergal mac Aeda Ruaircc mac rig Brefne & adbur rig m Briuin
ina tig budein la Lochlainn Colach Mac Caba per dolum caictigis ria Caiscc & a adlucad a manistir t-Slicig.
Carraic Lacha Ce do gabail iterum la Conchobar Occ mac Aeda Meic Diarmada co harrachta inces for clainn Fergail Meic Diarmada.
Niall Occ mac Neill Moir meic Aedo Moir Neill ardri coicid Ulad do ec hi fogmar na bliadna-sa iar mbreith bairi arin saegal-sa do chlu & d'enech & d'ardnos o lucht an bethad frecnairc, & curro archisi Dia dia anmain & Patraic.
Murcertach mac Dondchada Dubda, fer nar er duine riam im ni ar doman & a beith aice, do ecc in bono fine a samrad na bliadna-so
a n-Ard na Riad.

Cuchonnacht mac Magnusa meic Concondacht Raigillig ridamna Brefne & aenmac Una ingine Tairrdelbaig Conchobair do ecc a n-amsir fogmair.
Brian mac Domnaill Flaithbertaig ridamna Cairn Gecan.
Tomais meic Seaain na Tuaithe.

Tadc mac Cathail Oicc Conchobair
la clainn Toirrdelbaig Oicc Conchobair & la hEogan mac ind Apad Conchobair for Machaire na n-Oilech fo fel Brigti
llebaid Cathail meic Domnaill a senathar.
Conchobar Anabaid Cellaig ri Mane, nathair neme na n-Gaidel ar beodacht & crecharecht do ecc iar n-ongad & iar n-aithrige
a manistir Eoin Basti hi Tir Mane manistir arar mor a commain budein.
Cathal Dimusaig ridamna Clainni Mailugra
la Gallaib, & aithrisidd an fiallach dana cur maith a enech & a engnam.
Brian Dimusaig a derbrathair do marbad do Gallaib i cind mis iar sin.
Fedlimid Dimusaig do marbad la Gallaib beus.
Findguala ingen Toirrdelbaig Conchobair uxor Mailechlainn Cellaig ri Mane, an ben robe ferr clu & cloth do bi a n-aenamsir fria-si i nd Erinn uli.
Sluagad adbalmor la Conchobair n-Donn & la Murcertach mac Bacach mac Domnaill tigerna Slicig i nn Uachtur Connacht & tigernus Eogain Madadan meic Murchada do gabail doib don dulad-sin; & dol doib a Clainn Ricairt iarom do congnam la hUillec mac Ricairt i n-adaig Manech, & do gabadur tren don turus-sin ar Manechaib & tancatur can tobem cen tubaist dia tigib iar sin.
Murchertach Bacach mac Domnaill meic Murcertaig Conchobair tigerna Ichtair Connacht do ecc iar mbreith bari ara bidbadaib in cech aird d'Erinn uili in Aine iar fel Micheil.
Cocad mor do fas etir Brefnechaib & Clainn Donnchada, dar marbad daine maithi Tomaltach Oc mac Tomaltaig Meg Dorchaid deodflaith Ceneoil Luachain do marbad etarro, & Murcertach Og hElidi brugaid cetach conaich do marbad arin cocad-sin.
Maelmorda mac Con Connacht meic Gilla Isa Ruaid do gabail tigernais Muintire Maili Morda
Eogan mac Seoain Ruairc do gabail la Maelmorda Raigillig.
Sean mac Taidg meic Ualgairc Ruairc do gabail & do lot la Muintir Mailmorda & cocad do ergi as-side etir Muintir Raigillig & Muintir Ruairc; & Mathgamain mac Gilla Crist meic Flaithbertaig Meic Capa do lot in la-sin la muintir Ruairc; & is ann so doronnad gres an Cabain amail adubramar romaind mad iar n-araili libur.
Murcertach Garb Sechnusaig ridamna Fiachrach Aidne do marbad la Mainechaib.

o Clainn Maicne Eogain Cellaig & o clainn Hoberd Dalataun.

Mailsechlainn Meg Orechtaig
Muintiri Raduib isin Domnach meonach don Chargus
a r Rus Comman.
Conchobar Occ mac Aeda Meic Diarmata ri Moigi Luirg & bethir ar beodacht, do ecc etir feil Micheil & Samain, & Tadg mac Aedo Meic Diarmata do rigad ina inad timchell na Samna iar sin.
Cormac Mac Diarmada do marbad ar imruagad a Clainn Ricairt la marcsluag Clainni Ricairt & Tuadmuman archena i cind mis don fogmur cetna-sin, & dob e-sein an bainni ria frais do Moig Luirg Cormac ria Conchobar.
Ingen Conchobair Falgi ben Gilla Patricc Morda.
Cathal Mac Dondchada i Purt Indsi ina longport fein iar mbuaid n-aithrigi
Cill Meic Callain.
Domnall mac Enri Neill do gabail rigi in Coicid.
mac Oengusa meic Domnaill Oicc Meic Domnaill la Dondchad Cellaig.
Gallra imda i nd Erinn & galar na leptai co sundradach.
Morchad Occ mac Conchobair Meic Sithig.
Tomais Cendetig lethri Urmuman la Domnall mac Pilip Cennedig.
Maidm Atha Duib la Gilla Patraic Morda ri Laigse for Gallaib & moran do marbad ann & eich imda & arm & eded do bem dib beos.
Donnchad mac Cennedig Duinn do ecc hi lamdichus aca braithrib budein
Iarla Uurmuman cenn crodachta na hErenn.
Mac Cathmail
Ceneoil Feradaig
Dondchad Baccach Mailconaire ollam Sil Muredaig Muillethain re senchus.
Gilla Dubin Mac Cruitin ollam Tuadmuman re sencus.
Feidlim Tuathail ri Muredaig.
Cerball Dalaig ollam dana Corcu Modruad.
Fingen mac Eogain Mec Carthaig.
Mac Raith Suilleban.
Domnall mac Dondchada Dalaig Bolg an Dana.
Flann Occ mac Seoan Domnallain ollam dana sil Muredaig.
Cormac mac Aeda meic Feidlimid meic Gilla Isa Ruaid Raigillig.
Cocad d'ergi etir Mag Carrthaig lu Suilleban Budi & clainn Diarmata Meg Carrthaig, & Toirrdelbach Meith Mac Mathgamna ina longseoir ag Mag Carrthaig in tan-sin, & breith do ar Suilleban ar fairrgi & ar clainn Diarmata diblinaib & Suilleban do bathad Dondchad mac Diarmata & Domnall mac Eogain do gabail do beuss.
Andriu Baroid do marbad la hIb Murchada.
Eogan mac Murchada meic Cathair Conchobair Falgig do marbad la hIarla Cille Dara.
Nuala ingen Domnaill meic Murcertaig Conchobair ben Fergail meic Cormaic Meic Donnchada.
Uilliam radain ollam bretheman na Caemanach.
Fergal mac Teboid Mailmuaid.
Dond Cathaig mac Muredaig Meg Senlaich, brugaid cetach conaich do Corco Athclann & lanfer grada do Ruaidri Conchobair do Rig Condacht, & fer fora rabi cach uli sonus coa bas, & fuair logad a pecad fo deoid i cuirt an, an luan iar feil Micheil.
Calann Enair for Dardain & fiche fuirri, mu;
Endecas.

Risderd Butiler risi rati Cos Cruaid do marbad la mac Fachtna Morda.

Cathal mac Duind Meg Samradan
Dondchad Cam Lochlainn ri Corcu Mruad
o clainn Mailechlainn Lochlainn a n-eraicc a n-athar fein
Risded Mag Ragnaill adbur taisig na n-Eolusach iar n-ol usci bethad co himarcach, & dob usci marbtha do Risded.

Caislen Nua Findacan do bladad la Branachaib
Ingen Domnaill Briain ben Pilip meic Mathgamna Duinn Cennedid.

Murcertach Dubgindan.
Sluagad Artig la Tadc Mac Diarmada la rig Moigi Luirg d'iarraid a tigernais ar slicht Conchobair meicc Taithlig & for lucht Artig archena, amail roba dual d'fir a inait do gres.
Mac Diarmada do chur a cumcach ac Loch Laban i crich Artig Uchtlethain meic Tomintin d'U Conchobair Dond & do Clainn Murcertaig Mumnig Conchobair & do clainn Fergail Meic Diarmada & do lucht Artig budein & do Clainn Cethernaig & do Clainn Conchobair; & mar fuaratur imarcraid na nemcharat Mac Diarmata i mbaegal do dortsed fair cend i cend or ro batur fein da ored no tri ored do dainib re Mac n-Diarmada.
Dochuiredar chuci diblinaib & do dortsetar caeraigechd Conchobair etir cois & ech ina chend & tuccatur in fraiss do bai isna bodhadaib dia 'raili & do brised la Mac n-Diarmata forro & la Dondchad Mac n-Domnaill consapla Meic Diarmata & la Lochlainn Colach Mac Caba & la glaslaith Moigi Luirg archena hi tuss in lai forin cummascaig sluag-sin & nemcharad; & do marbad brotursach mor do fodainib la muintir Meic Diarmata; & cid ed dob e sin int aithes co n-anaithes fo deoid do muintir Meic Diarmata.
Oir doig am tuc fer ecin don debaid frithroisc urchur duaibsech do saigit fon mill moradbal do maithib in morsluaig do bai ic imditin ind ardflathai & aca anacal ar orchoitib na hirgaili.
do sechnait lasin soigit-sin doescursluag dimain & fodaine & galgata gaiscid & gaithlengaid in sluaig archena & do benastar na goithne dub diablaidi i corr bragatt na flatha co fiadnach.
Acht ata ni nama, a haithli na hurbada-sin cin forigtin & na tubuisti can turbrod fuaratur soerchlanna Slebe Segsa & curaid Cnuic in Scail & Tulchain Maelruanaid Moir re n-abrann cach co coitchenn anosa, ut in fili Mac Cosi:
Cnoc in Scail a ainm ar tus o re Nera fa é arus;
Tulchan Mail Ruanaid na rend bid e a ainm co ti an forcendetc.-, do facaibset an tir iar sin & tancatur da tigib & tucad Tadcc da adnacal a n-otharligi a senser; & a haithli adnaicti Taidc do rigsat Ruaidri mac Aedo Meic Diarmata, & dar mo debroth nirbo cloch a n-inat uigi sin; & fo fel Cros doronad in rognim-sin, amail indisis in cronicae duin
Magnus mac Aedo Uicind.
Aed hAnlide
Ceneoil Dobtha meic Aengais Augusti
hi Cluain Cairbthi for Sinna for comairce Beraig.
Mor ingen meic Gafraid Raigillig Martii.
Iohannes mac Mailmartain uicarius Uillae Templi Martii.
Aine ingen Briain Meg Tigernan Mai
Calann Enair for Aine & aen uathaid fuirri, mac Primus andus
Laigsech Nuallan adbar rig Fothart & Aed Tuathail adbar rig Mail & Bran Brain damna rig Faelan & Domnall mac Tomais Mec Murchada
don plaig
Maelruanaid mac Taidg Meic Dondchada ri n Ailella do ecc ina tig fein iar mbuaid n-ongtha & n-aithrige
a manistir na Bulli
Maidm dermar la Murchad Conchobair ri Falgi cona clainn & a clann maicne budein mar oen ris, & Cathal Dub & Tadc da mac rig Condacht budein becc marcach mar oen ris beus, ar ndol ar cuairt doib a n-Uib Falgi dochum Conchobair, for Gallaib na Mide & for Eogan mac ind Abad Conchobair & for cethernaib congmala Connacht mar aen ris, co ndeochatar na sluaig-sin diblinaib i nd Uachtar Gesille, & co ndeochaid mac ind Abbad co Cluain Immorruiss cona corachad budein co bali in Gilla Bude Meic Maelcorra; & dar mo debrod robad ferr doib na dechtais, co rruc forro ann sin in Calbach mac Murchada Conchobair & Cathal Conchobair seser marcach, co ndubairt in Gilla Buide, & aigin an Calbaig bai ar iasacht aigi ag denam lenna & se ar muin oclaich don tsluag: 'Focraim h'aigin det, a Chalbaig' 'Gaibim ais' ar in Calbach.
Dorat fer don toraig orchar aithesach do cloich cur ben ar toin an aigin, cur moig don tsluag asin fath-sin & cur marbad mac inn Apad arin monaid allathuaid don baili hisin, & ni hed amain acht nir luga na tri cet do doinib a n-esbaid ota sin co Cluain Aine a Crich na Cetach, ut audimus o cach co coitchenn.
Uair robas ag cur an air hisin o Cluain Imurruis co Cluain Aine, & do benad ardmindd Connacht uili dib in la-sin in Buacach Patri do bith a n-Oil Find.
Tadc mac Donnchada Birn
Tiri Briuin na Sinna obiit Toirrdelbach Occ mac Aeda meic Toirrdelbaig ri Connacht re da bliadain ar hi comflaith & Conchobair Ruad do marbad la Cathal Dub mac Conchobair Ruaid, & la Seaan mac hEmainn meic Hobert meic Sir Dauid a Burc & Mna Muman ingine meic Fedlimid, la Diarmait Tanaiden ler cuitiged co milita in morecht-sin, a tig Ricairt meic Seaain Buide meic Emaind meic Hoberd isin Crecan re taeb Fidicen hi Clainn Condmaig.
iss e sin in tres ri do rigaib Connacht do marbad a Clainn Connmaig Conchobar Maenmaigi mac Ruaidri meic Toirrdelbaig Moir, & Ruaidri mac Cathail Ruaid meic Conchobair Ruaid meic Murcertaig Mumnig meic Toirrdelbaig Moir Ri Erenn, Toirrdelbach Occ mac Aeda meic Toirrdelbaig Oicc, amail adubramar remaind, idus Decimbris arai laithi mis greine, dia Dardain immorro arai sechtmaine ined la déc ante festum natale nostri Iesu Christi.
Calann Enair for Sathurn & aili fuirri, mvii.
Cathal mac Conchobair Falgi do marbad la Clainn Feorais Seoan mac Taidc Ruairc adbur rig Brefne do ecc i Moig Luirc & a adnacal a n-Druim Lethan
Mac Taidc meic Mathgamna Duinn Cennedig tigerna Urmuman Uachtaraigi do marbad la Cerbaill.
Maidm mor la Gallaib & le Sgrub ar Gaidilaib Muman, du inar marbad Tadcc Cerbaill ri Eli, & feichem coitchenn do chliaraib Erenn & Alpan in Tadc hisin, & curro archise Dia dia anmain.
Murcertach Cellaig ardespoc Connacht, sai na hErenn uli ind ecna & a nderc & i ndoennacht, i Tuaim Da Gualann fo feil Micheil.
Maidm la Conchobair Ruad & le Cellaig inar marbad drem do Clainn t-Sithig, & ni fetur-so a n-anmann.
Maidm Cilli Achaid la Conchobair Ruad & la macaib Mailsechlainn Cellaig & la Ruaidri Mac Diarmata ri Moigi Luirc for Macc Uilliam Clainni Ricairt & for Cathal mac Ruaidri Conchobair, dar garmed gairm rig d'es Conchobair Duinn do marbad la Cathal Dub mac Conchobair Ruaid, cur brised for Clainn Ricairt & for Cathal mac Ruaidri, cor gabad ann Cathal mac Ruaidri & Uilliam Burcc and-side & cur marbad & cur gabad moran eli ann beus; & fo fel Iohannis Baptistae doronait na morgnima-sin.
Caislen Tobair Tulsci do brised reme-side la Brian mac Domnaill meic Murcerltaig Conchobair & la Clainn Dondchada, & Cathal mac Ruaidri do chor ar Carn Fraich doib.
Conmac Fergail do bas anabaid.

Sluagad la mac in Rig i Laignuib iar sin & Hitsin Diuit do marbad foran tsluagad-sin, & dob anba an esbaid sin.
Pestilencia magna isin Mide, Scrub ritiri rocroda & fer inait Rig Saxan ind Erind do ec don plaig-sin.

la Clainn Maircertaig i ndigaltus Magnusa meic Murcertaig meic Cathail do marbad a Clainn Cethernaig remi-sin.

Maelsechlainn mac Briain Meg Tigernan
Attaisech do denam do Maelsechlainn Mor Mag Eochacan & Fergal mac Fergail Ruaid Mec Eochacan meic Dondchada ina inatt iar sin.
Coss Risderd a Burcc do brised la coin do bai 'na rith & a ecc de sin co tubaisech.
Crech Beoil Leci la Tigernan Ruairc ar n Domnaill & ar Cathal Ruairc & for Eogan Ruairc & Domnaill & Cenel Conaill a foslongport allathall don es & Cathal & Eogan allaaboss don es cetna, & tucc in creich uadaib diblinaib.
Sluagad la Brian mac Domnaill meic Murcertaig Conchobair & la Conchobar Mac Dondchada ri Tiri hOilella & la clainn Tigernan Ruairc, cur cuiretur lon & biad, d'andeoin Condachd o Sliab suas uili & siat tinolti ara chinn uli etir cois & ech & galloclach, hi caslen Rosa Coman in Luan iar feil Micheil Archangeil.
do tsailitur o Sliab sis co mbetis Clann Ricaird ina fochair fein ag cur in bid-sin a caislen Rosa Coman & ni rabatur, acht Mac Uilliamb buiden becc marcach do tocht co Baili in Tobair ina coinne.
do fuabratur locad ann-side o nach tancatur sluag Clainni Ricaird cuctha amail ro gellsad, & adubairt Mac Donnchada nach locfad noco tuted noco cuired biad isin caislen, & adubairt re Mac Uilliam anmain and sin o nach raba lin trodai no tecmala do tabairtt do Chondachtaib, & da marbthar sinne is maith find tusa beo acar lenbaib inar ndiaid da cothagad' Cid tra acht do gluais Mac Donchada i rremthus na sliged & nir an se don reim & don ruathur-sin noco ranicc co Ros Comman, & do cuiretur lon isin caislen, & nir marbad acht oenoclaech dib & ruccsad fein a chorp leo; & ni menicc dorigned a n-Erinn riam sibal bad croda & bad calma ina in sibal-sin.
Muinter Churnin do marbad a cheli Seoan & Conla do marbad la Diarmait mac Murcertaig Curnin hi tig Dubgennan Baili Chailled Fobair, Diarmait fein do dol co tech Conchobair Cruim meic Taidcc Conchobair a tigerna & a derbchomalta, & Conchobar da gabail ina tig budein & a tidlacad do Muintir Ruairc & do Muintir Curnin & a beith tuilled & coictigis i llaim & a toitim la mac Seaan Curnin fo deoid.
Cathal Mac Dondchada Octobris & ni demin lem nach is i so bliadain in bad choir Conchobar mac Imair Anlide do chur sis.
Murcertach Mac Aedacan ollam bretheman Fer Teptha.

Conchobar Dochurtaig
Arda Midair & tigerna hInsi hEogain fer lan d'feli & d'enech.
Cathal mac Eogain Matadan ri t-Sil n-Anmchada.
Tuathal Maille do dol ar congbail hi Coced Ulad & a beith bliadain ann, & ac techt do dia tig lucht sechd long etir mnai & fir fo feil Choluim Cille cur erig casanfad in mara tiar doib & cur fuadaig Neptuin comsigthid na ngaeth in longes-sin lam des re hAlpain bud tuaid cur baided longa cona fairind dib-side, fo da mac Tuathail Mailli & im da mic meic Eogain Chonnachtaig Meic Subne & im Domnall mac Ballach mac meic Subne Girr, & da ar da cet maille riu etir maith & saith do bathad and beuss & Tuathal fein do techt a tir ar ecin ind Alpain.
Tomas Og Raigillig do dol ar indsaigid dochum Gall & fis d'fagbail reme & Gaill do beith indilti fora chinn & a lecen doib crecha mora do gabail iar sin, & nochtad do Tomas Occ & do Clainn Caba, & Mathgamain Mac Caba & Lochlainn Mac Caba do marbad ann & moran da muintir maille friu do marbad ann beuss.
ga do bein a cois Tomas & a beith losc o sin amach.

In Maigester Mochan

nobiles ignobiles, inar gabad Dardisech Gandlige, inar gabad an lin asa frith da cet marcc & cin arem ar luagib lesa ann-side, & inar gabad mac Barun Slane asa frith decc marcc cona luaiginnaib lesa.

Domnall mac Domnaill Mag Carthaig Carprich do ecc
Seon Stanlae fer inait Rig Saxan do techt a n-Erinn do milled Gaidel na hErenn fer nach tuc termann do chill na do thuaith na do aes dana na hErenn cach aen fora rucc se da clerchaib & da n-aes eladan in cach cerd do arcain do & a cur re fuacht & re faigdi do.
Niall mac Aeda Uginn do arcain do a n-Uisnech Mide.
Hanri Dalutun do dol fo mac Semais Diuit & fo muintir an Rig & bo sa mboin & capall san capall & caera san cairig & mucc san muicc do tabairt do do Muintir Uiccind & a n-idnacal a Condachtaib iar sin.
Seon Stanlai do aerad la Muintir Uicind iar sin.
ni raibi Seon Stanlai beo acht sechdmaine nama in tan fuair bas do nem na n-aer-sin; & is e sin an dara firt filed doronad ar Niall n Uiginn Clann Connmaig do lethad aidchi creiche Neill a Cladaind & Seon Stanlai do marbad do nem na n-aer.

in Dairsigig Ratha Guaire hi cetgemred na bliadna-so.
Saxain imda do techt ind Erinn Loard Furnamal & inadh Righ Saxan aice.
Laighis Morda do milled do & caslen na Culenntraigi caslen meic Fachtna Mordai & ar bo & ech & indili leis a hairg & do mill se meic na mac Bretnach & do croc se Geroid mac Tomais Caich d'fuil Geraltach.

Conchobair & a braithricha do ergi co hadlam inenfir ina condi & can esimal na orsclaigi do gabail uadaib acht a ndingidluthagad isind abainn dubaicen bai fora n-inchaib, & dias no triar do badad isind abainn-sin dib & Conchobair do imtecht imlan a cend Anligi.

Cocad etir Iarla Urmuman & Iarla Desmuman.
Geroit mac Iarla Desmuman do gabail le Buitilerachaib.
Port Lairge do gabail leo.
La catha do gabail etarro diblinaib.
Ni tanicc Iarla Urmuman dochum in chatha in la-sin; ar ba he gnath Saxan, ni tabradais cath Luain na iar medon lai laithi aili.
Tanicc Mac Risderd do chor in chatha tar sarachad an Iarla, & tanicc fris fein.
Tucsat fein & Geraltaig cath fichda fuilech da cheli & brestir for Buitilerachaib & do comarmed araib do adnacal dib cenmotha a ndodur coin & biasta.
Gabait Geraltaig Cill Coinnig & balti mora na Quntai, iar cur air a ndaine.
Iarla Urmuman cona Saxaib do chongbail an bali ana rabadur fein.
Brathair oc larla Urmuman do thecmail ar farci re cethri longaib do muintir Iarla Desmuman cona lucht maithis & a ngabail do.
Nert mor do fas a mac Butilerachaib lesin ngabail-sin.
Crecha anba la Ruaidri Mac n-Diarmata & la Cormac mac Ballach Mac n-Donnchada co ngasraid oicc slechta Conchobair Meic Donnchada for Clainn Connmaig & for Mac n-Diarmata cona braithrib o Beol Atha Duin Imdain, co rucsat seit d'fichtib bo leo a n-ecmais ellaig eli.
Crecha mora eli ina ndigail-side la Mac n-Diarmata & la hEmand mac Uilliam for Ruaidri Mac n-Diarmata a Cillin Arbelaig co haithisach mana tecmad in tubais ann Cormac mac Conchobair Meic Diarmata do marbad d'oenbuille tslegi, co rucsat cetri & cetri cet bo leo & seit in cech cet dib-side, & marbthur a lan da n-andainib.
Ruaidri mac Conchobair Duinn d'fuaslacad o Conchobair Donn.
Cathal Ruad mac Conchobair Ruaid d'fuaslacad leis uadai beus ar cetri marcc.
Maidm la Cathal Mag Ragnaill for clainn Mailsechlainn inar gabad a cend cunnraid Uilliam Mag Ragnaill & Toirrdelbach Mac Dubgaill constapla a ngalloclaech & mac Iriel Fergail.
Mag Ragnaill do gairm do Cathal & Conchobar do cumscagad iar caithem a aisi co mor.
Maidm for Fergail la mac Cuind Mailsechlainn & la Dilmainechaib & la Laisich mac Rosa isind Nuachongbail, inar gabad Emand Fergail, & ma's fir dom scelaigi doboenbar ar a n-esbaid uili etir gabail & marbad, im enfer do slicht Murcertaig Oic Fergail do marbad isin arem-sin; & dobo banne re frais don Angaili sin, or nir cian dia es Isin cor marbad ant oenmac taisig occ dobo mo muirer & muirigin & dob ferr do cocthoir & do crechari for Gallaib & Gaidelaib bitis ina agaid Tomas mac Cathail Fergail do marbad a mac Beol Atha na Palisi isin adaig for lurg a creichi la dreim do Dilmainechaib & do clainn Conchobair & do mac Murcertaig, co rucsad leo a cenn & a creich, iarna fagbail a n-uathad doine amail ba hannam leis.
Mac Branan Tomaltach Carrach mac Cuinn meicc Aeda, iarna beith sel foda i mbochta.
Errach & samrad rocruaid, conach tanicc a n-insamail o errach meic Toirrdelbaig anall.
Bliadain na n-Gras in bliadain-so, & moran do dol co San Sem inti.
In Gallim do traig & moran d'fagbail inti.

Brian mac Pilip Meg Udir, fer a aisi fein dob ferr enech & engnam i coiced Ulad uili, do marbad i toraigecht a creichi la clainn Airt Neill iar mbeith athaid a laim aca.

Indsaigid la hUilliam Burc mac Risderd a Burc for caislen Mulinn Adam, do digail a sula do benad as reme-side asin caslen-sin d'orchar do soigid, cor lenad e co Bali in Mutaig a toraigecht.
Impod do-som frisin toraig & coic duine don toraig do marbad lais fo mac Magnusa meic Diarmata Meic Dondchada & fo macaib Neill.
Do ben fer dib a suil as acan caislen-sin fecht riam.
Fer le hochtar do marbad do Ceneol Fiachach a trodan la feli Coluim Cille im chend maide bodha, fo mac Diarmata meic Aeda Budi Meg Eochacan & fo mac Conchobair Anabaid Meg acan & fo mac meic Fiachach Meg Eochacan, la Feraib Cell & la Clainn Colman.
Indsaigid la Tadc Conchobair & la Feraib Cell for Delbna Mec Cochlan cur gabad Tadc fein ann sin & mac Fedlim Conchobair & cur benad immad ech & etig dib.
Cur fuaslaiced Tadc ar cardis Crist & altrannus & da cet marc maille riu sin, & co ndeachaid d'es a tuaslaicti fo Feraib Tulach, & siat 'na n-altrannaib & 'na cardib aice, & co ruc arcti aidbli leis uadaib.
Cocad do fas etir Conchobair & Tadc triasan argain-sin batur ina n-altrannaib ac O Conchobair, cor hinnarbad Tadc a Clainn Mailugra iar marbad ech & iar lot daine etarro.
Flannacan & a mac do gabail la slicht Briain Ballaig & a tech do loscad a Coillin Carthaig & tromguin tsoigti do thabairt fair fein.
Crech odchi la slicht Briain Ballaig for Ruaidri mac Cathail Duib a n-Dori Carlinn.
Flannacan do lecan amach & cin a comus aici a tir do suidiugad & a mac do facbail astig a ngill ri comall.
Mac Cuind Mailsechlainn do gabail a fill a tig Petitig in Mulinn Chirr & in Petitich na altraind aici, & roigne ech & armb & etig do bein de & da muintir & moran do braigdib maithe do gabail and do Clainn Colman & d'Feraib Cell, im da mac meic Cuinn.
Conchobair Falgi do techt sluag diarme dochum an Mulinn Chirr & mac Mailsechlainn do tabairt do ar ecin, & a braigdi uli d'facbail astig, & tri cet bo & urad maith na tirtid-sin & treda mucc, & sid maille riu sin.
Crecha adbli la Tadc Conchobair & la Cenel Fiachach for Machuiri Cuircne cur aircsit in tir uili o Dun na Monad fo des & o Chill an Ibair amach.
Indsaigid la clainn Meg Ragnaill for Baili Tuama Usci cur losced in baili leo and & cur gabsad creich, & dochodar fein 'na cotidaib & cuirit a muintir & a creich timchell, & marbthar triar da muintir mac Cormaic meic Risded Meg Ragnaill & da mac Morda & dias no triar do lucht Muigi Trega fo mac Amlaib meic Matha meic Con Connacht Fergail.

Mac Risderd Butiler, ant aenchend fedna dobo mo arem & dob ardi clu do Gallaib Erenn.
Crechruathar la clainn Cellaig, Colla prioir Tigi Eoin & Ruaidri, la forgall Briain Brain Bregmaine & clainni Rosa meic Murcertaig Midig Fergail, co torchair and da mac Cellaig & se fir da muintir maille friu & Brian Brain & nebar da muintir & nibar aili do lucht an Chalaid fo Uilliam mac Dondchada meic an Priora, conider ar triit sin uli; & cia dorat Mag Amalgaid maidm is fair tucad.
Crech an Lacain la Tadc Mag Ragnaill ar tarraing Diarmata meic Lochlainn Oicc Anligi, & ni chualamur Gall na Gaidel reme sin riam da denam.

In Giustis & int Espac na Mide & Tomas Ploncet & fer le hochtar do maithib a muintiri do dol do imcosait ara celi co tech Rig Saxan.

Mirbaile mora la delb Mure Atha Truim
Tuilled le haisecc mar nar gnath d'fagbail do mac Mailsechlainn on Petidech a n-eraicc a fill fair a tir do loscad & do lomarcain ar tus & aisicc imlan iar tain.
Uilliam mac Maine meic Cuinn meic Tigerna slechta Conchobair Meic Branan.

Cocad mor etir slicht Uilliam Cellaig & clainn Dondchada Cellaig.
Feraind do benadur clann Uilliam do clainn Donnchada do bein ar ais isin cocad-sin.
Cocad mor etir clannaib Cellaig, Aeda meic Briain, clann ingine Eogain & clann ingine Meic Diarmata, & Tir Maine uli do loscad etarro, & doronsat sid iar marbad clainni Cellaig la Calraigib.
Calraigi do dichur a n-Ib Falgi, acht a mbarda nama a mac Bali Locha Luatha.

Tadc Conchobair lethri Connacht in Sathurn iar cetfel Mure in fogamair

Acht ata ni chena, dorochair and sin Cathal Ruad Conchobair la derbbrathair a mathar & la derbraithrib a athur.
In dara la deginach don Marta, Satharn Domnaig na Palmi, doronad an gnim-sin, co nach rabi caduss ac ollam na ac epscop a Sil Muiredaig.
Sicc romor & snechta & doinend dermair isin bliadain-sin co nar fas luib tria ttalmain na duilli tria crann co fel Brenaind co mbered an fer fa tresi an biad ar ecin asin eclais on tsacart & an Corp Naemda etir a di laim & a adme Oifrinn ime.
Aed mac Conchobair Meic Diarmata ri Moigi Luirc do ec & Conchobar Occ mac Conchobair Meic Diarmata do rigad ina inad do thuaith & do chill a tiri fein, acht clann Ruaidri Meic Diarmata nama.
Conne do gabail etir Mac n-Diarmata & Conchobair n-Dond & in clainn-sin & Donnchad Cellaig arna tarraing don clainn-sin Ruaidri Meic Diarmata.
Dol fo celi doib & brised for Conchobair n-Donn & Diarmait mac Ruaidri do marbad and & Tadc mac Ruaidri Budi do gabail and & mac Cathail Ruaid Conchobair dalta Taidc meic Ruaidri Budi.
Lenam do marbad do mac Diarmata Moir Conchobair bai a fochair a aiti & moran da cetheirn do marbad & d'fodbagad.

Sluagad la Gallaib Mide & Laigen a n-Uib Falgi cur marbad Seaan mac Meic Tomais for imruagad, int aenchenn fedna dob ferr do Gallaib Mide & Laigen.
Dopo bainne ri frais do Gallaib sin, ar do madmaiged ant Iarla & a Gaill arabarach & do gabad int Iarla and & do benad a arm & a eded de & do tinlaic Tadc.

Imthusa a ndechaid astech a Caislen Carpri badur Gaidil a n-imsuide ana timchell; dodeochaid muinter Atha Cliath ina torigtin, co rucsad leo iad d'aindeoin Conchobair & a Gaidel archena.

Roberd Bared.
Cocad romor for Machuiri Connacht, cor ergetar clann meic Fedlim uili & clann Taidc & Tuatha t-Sil Muredaig & clann Cellaig & clann Ruaidri Meic Diarmata d'Fedlim Find, co ndechaid Fedlim a cend Meic Diarmata foran Corr sliab.
Facbais a chaeraigecht for comuirci Meic Diarmata.

Ted fein & a lucht lenamna la Mac Uilliam Burc.
Tic Mac Branan & a braithricha dia tir.
Dubta & a brathair no a mac do marbad per dolum la clainn Mailruanaid meic Ruaidri Dubda.
Maidm mor for Argiallaib la Gallaib inar marbad moran, & inar gabad Aed Occ Mag Mathgamna.

Pestilencia magna a n-Ath Cliath & a Mide & i Laignib.
