Donnchad mac Murchertaig Dalaig.
Mac Briain meic Emainn
la clainn Conchobair meic Cathail iar techt ara ech dochum usci asin Caslen Nua & se ag clainn Tomas.
In caslen-sin do gabail forro la clainn Conchobair & la mac Mailsechlainn & a tir uli do loscad & do lomarcain, & sid do denam doib iar mbreith a mbo & iar marbad a ndaine & iar loscad a n-arba co himlan.
Calann Enair for Dardain & sesed fuirri
Semas mac espuic Risderd meic an Decanaig Moir meic Domnaill meic t-Seaan Galdai Fergail, ab Lethratha, sai occ uasal digdelba doennachtach, a tus a ratha & a aisi.
Dar le lucht a medaigti is d'formad beme sul na sochuidi adbath, & bennacht lais dochum nime.
Tadc mac Donnchada Cellaig adbar rig Mane.
Domnall Buidi Fergail lantaisech na hAngaili.
Laisech mac Rosa meic Conchobair meic Cathail Fergail.
Irial Fergail a n-inad Domnaill & Seaan a n-inad Irieil.
Aed mac Briain Cellaig & Aed mac Uilliam Cellaig ina inad, & nirbo cloch a n-inad uigi.
Aed Dub & Tadc da mac Dondchada meic Briain Ballaig & Tadc mac Briain meic Briain Ballaig & Aed Ruad mac Diarmata Moir meic Diarmata Conchobair do marbad i ngreis oidchi la Diarmait mac Conchobair & la clainn Diarmata Ruaid Conchobair & la Cathal mac Cathail meic meic Ruaidri Oicc Conchobair.
Dauid Mac Gosdelb
la Tomas Mac Feorais.
Donnchad mac Seoain meic Mailsechlainn Fergail do dol don Roim & a hecc thoir.
Maidm mor for Cellaig & for Clainn Uilliam Burc a Crois Moigi Craind la Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricairt & la Sil mac Briain, inar marbad Uilliam Caech mac Meic Uilliam Burc & da mac Cellaig & Aed Bude mac Toirrdelbaig Meic Domnaill a constapla galloclaech, & enbar d'uaslaib Clainni Domnaill mar aen ris, & nobiles & ig
Domnaill do toidecht a Condachtaib a mbaig a raind fein & sith do bein a Clainn Ricairt & a imthecht slan.
Insi Locha Carrcin do gabail for barda Feidlim Find d'O Conchobair Donn & do clainn meic Fedlim.
Crecha can comarem la Tadc Conchobair & la Mag Eochacan & la Clainn Feorais, cur arcsit o Imper co Bali Meic Uilliam.
Seoan mac Fedlim meic Fergail Raigillig
Caslen Cul Maili do gabail do clainn Cormaic Ballaig Meic Donnchada for slicht Cormaic Meic Dondchada in oc.
Mac Meic Uilliam Clainni Ricaird do galar oband.
Cristoir Plonced & Piarus mac Piarrais Dalatun & Semus Oc mac meic Semuis Dalatun
don plaig, & Prioir in Mulinn Chirr beus di mac an Petitig.
Seoan Dalatun
Toirrdelbach mac Ruaidri meic Cathail Conchobair do marbad, la feli na Croichi Naim isind fogamur, i r Rus Coman la clainn Domnaill Caim meic Magnusa Cellaig.
Cathal Raigillig ri Muintire Mailmorda.
Colla mac Magnusa Meg Mathgamna & aenfer da muintir do marbad la Brefnechaib a lurg a creichi fein.
Giustiss Saxanach do techt a n-Erinn & Tomas do aitherrach.
Calann Enair for Aine & sechtmad uathad fuirri
Urbaid & anicin romor do techt a n-Erinn Tomas Iarla, aen Iarla na hErenn uili ar cruth & deilb & denam, ar cach cerd as bad inmolta duine, ar cosc merle & mibes, ar tidnacal set & maine do thuathaib & ecalsib & d'filedaib hErend uili, do dol co Drochat Atha ar Cuirt moir i coinde in Giustis & Gall Mide, & a dichennad cin chair cin cinaid;
a Traig Li meic Dedad a n-otharligi a sinser; & do brisedar crideda fer n-Erenn & a mban don sceol-sin.
Ruaidri mac Conchobair Meic Dondchada ri n Ailella & Baili in Duin do ecc iar mbreith baire for deman & doman, coictigis ria fel Brigti.
Risderd Riad mac Uilliam Meic Dauid.
Gormlaith ingen Murchada meic Cormaic meic uxur Aoda Meic Suibne i mis Enair.
Conchobair Falgi do gabail do Gallaib
Toirrdelbach mac Seoain Raigillig do rigad
Cathal Occ mac Cathail Ruaid Meg Ragnaill, lantoisech Muintiri hEolais, do ec ina tig fein iar mbuaid ongtha & athrige isin cetdomnach don Chargus mor, & bendacht De lais ar febus a duas & ar med a derci & a doennachda & ar met a cride & a chaithme & a chonaigh, & do caithed an conach-sin re cliaraib & re comaighthib Erenn, re bochtuib & re haidilgnechaib in Chomded chumachtaig; & co cuitige Dia sin fria a anmuin i llaithe inn Fuigill.
Taisech do genam da mac do Tadc Mac Ragnaill ina inad, & toisech do gairm d'Uilliam Mag Ragnaill la slicht Mailsechlainn Meg Ragnaill.
In Gilla Dub mac Cormaic Ballaig Meic Dondchada
Torna Maolconuire ollam Sila Muredaig meic Fergusa a senchus & filidecht do eg ina tig fein i l Lius Ferban l-Gerbain iar mbuaid n-aithrige iar fel Patric, & a adnacal fo ditin Patric & San Froinses a n-Oil Finn, & Urard Mailconuire a n-ollamnacht da esi.
Art mac Cuind Mailsechlainn
Mide de iure do marbad i Cnuc Choscraig Mairt Chasg, iar ndol do for innsaigid forra.
Conchobar mac Emuind meic Mailsechlainn Anligi Sathurn Minchasg.
Conchobar Mailalaid epscop Ola Finn.
Morda & Mac Gilla Patric
din tregait.
Tigernan Occ mac Taidg Ruairc ri dingbala m Briuin & Chatha Aedha Finn iar mbuaidh o deman & doman.
Domnall mac Taidg Ruairc do rigad ina inad d'O Domnaill & dia chairdib archena; & slicht Tigernain meic Tigernain Moir meic Ualgairg do ergi do-sin go hegoir & Dondchad Losc mac Tigernain Moir do rigad doib fein & do Charprechuib & do Chlainn Donnchada.
Domnaill sluag diarme dar Erne anall & Ichtar Connacht do milled les.
Crecha diairmi do denam do for airther Tiri Fiachrach & Cuili Cnam & Coillid Luigne & a mbreith les dia tig.
Mac Uilliam Uachtarach & O Conchobair Donn cona sochraite Gall & Gaidel diblinaib do dol hi forigthin Ichtair Connacht & bali Ruairc do loscad leo, & gan do maith do denam acht sin & a toidecht dia tigh cin chath cin comaidh, & arbanna Thire hOilella & Carbre & Luigne cin blath cin buidechus dia cind.
Caslen Cule Maili do gabail do clainn Briain Meic Dondchada for clainn Chormaic Ballaig Meic Dondchada & a tabairt don muintir dar benadh e roime.
Caslen Bona Drobaisi bai ag Domnaill do tabairt do slicht Murchertaig Baccaig aris do.
Ricart a Burc do toidecht a Moigh Luirc.
Sid Moigi Luirc do denam do & a ndol diblinuib i conne Domnaill, & Domnaill do dol tar Erne resiu dochotur-som sis & cin a thecmail da cheli don chur-sin.
Ricart do impodh for ais for Machaire Connacht & braigde les o chlainn Conchobair Ruaid, & slicht Fedlim do milled les o nar damsad braigde do.
Clann Connmaig do milled le hEmand mac Uilliam fen cona clainn le huabar & dimus.
Crecha diairmi la Fedlimid Finn for Conchobair & a mbreith a Mag Luirc les.
Crecha anba aile les a n-Ib Maine & crech eli les o thslicht Feidlim Clerig & crech aile les o Muintir Birn co Cill Atrachta i conne Ricairt a Burc cona sluag, cur congaib se an sluag sechtmain cin sgailed o cheli fora lon fen abain, & do chongebad iat ni bad faide da n-andais aige.
Crech mor ele do breith les o Chiarraige Meic Cethernaigh & mac meic Aeda Caich Conchobair do marbad les in la-sin.
Emand mac Uilliam do ergi do for Imuire Uarain triit galloclaech & tri it do chethirn chongbala & marcsluag a tire fein, & moran do lot eturro & in crech do bein d'Fedlimid ann sin cenmotha a capuill.
Cathan.
In Deganach mac Muris meic Conchobair.
Moran don Mide & dona cundaibh Laignecha do milled la Geroid mac Iarla Desmuman i ndigail Tomais Iarla.
In Dilmainech Machaire Cuircne.
Ben Muman ingen Eoguin Conchobair uxur Aedha meic Briain Cellaig.
Aine ingen Meg Eochagan ben Meg Uidir.
Emann in Machaire Mac Gosdelb do marbad per dolum la a derbrathair fein la hUilliam Mac Gosdelb.
Conchobar Buide mac Cormaic Meic Branan.
Uaithne mac Meg Eochagan do marbad d'orchur do soigit i caslen Cnuicc I Choscraig.
Tadg Mac Tigernain in brugaid cetach conaich & Nuala ingen Meic Donnchada Riabaig Fergal a chommaim
Maidm mor for Gallaib Lethe Cathail inar marbad Oengus mac Alaxandair Meic Domnaill & mac Roberd Sabais tigerna Lethe Cathail & inar gabad Murcertach Ruad Neill tigerna Clainni Aeda Buide la Conn mac Aoda Buide Nell a mac Beind Uama, & ali multi nobiles & ig
Crecha anba eli la Fedlim Finn & la Conchobar mac Conchobair Meic Diarmata rig Moigi Luirc for Baile in Tobair, & Conchobair Donn fein do breith forra lin a thinail cenmothatt a thuatha, & Ruaidri Conchobair lin a tinoil & blod mor do Clainn Connmaig mar aen ris & slicht meic Fedlim uili abus do breith forro diblinaib, & a n-imtecht go haithesach imlan conicci in Sgor Mor Clainni Cathail meic Muredaigh.
Impod croda coscurach la Fedlimid & la Mac n-Diarmata forro ann sin & sraenmaidm sechranach do tabairt forra, co nach tabrad fer dib iasacht slati da cheli.
Eogan mac Toirrdelbaigh Doill meic Toirrdelbaig Oic Conchobair & Fedlim mac Toirrdelbaig Ruaid meic Briain Ballaig & ali multi nobiles & ig
Beris Fedlim an crech do chosaib tirmuib co mbuaid & coscar & fagbais a bidba fo mela & cudbed.
Ruaidri mac Diarmata Ruaidh meic Taidhg Conchobair & ingen Charpre Conchobair a uxar
do galar opann.
Doma mor isin bliadain-sin sechnon Erenn uile o plaigh & o fill & o finguil & o chocad coitchenn fo Erinn, co tegdis da pinginn arin puitel mbeg a samrad na bliadna-sa.
Crech mor la Tadg mac in Chalbaig forin Craibech hi Cois Ethne gur benadh tuilled leit do doinib dib & gar do daet da n-echaib imachair.
Lot in Dalatunaigh do tharruing in sibal & lot Meg Eochacan, & ruc Tadg in creich.
Crechuis Tadg aris in lucht cetna co ruc argne anba, & torchair mac Briain meic Laisig les.
Feradach mac Lochlainn Oic Anlige & mac meic Cormaic Anligi & araill da cethirn do marbad la clainn Uathne Anligi.
Calann Enair for Domnach; ochtmad fuirre.
Aed mac Uilliam Chellaig ri Maine, sai na hErenn uile, fer nar etigh dreich duine riam, do marbad hi fill la slicht Dondchada Chellaig Luan Inite in dara la ria fel Beraigh la clainn Bresail & Tadg mac Dondchada.
Da Chellaig do gairm ina diaid Uilliam mac Aeda meic Briain & Tadg Caech mac Uilliam Chellaig.
Risderd Oc Raigillig rodamna rig Brefne.
Risderd mac Tomais a Burc do tregad a tigernais & Ricart mac Emaind a Burc do rigad ina inad, & dar mo debrod ni cloch i n-inad ugi.
Tadg mac Briain Meic Dondchada
Eogan mac Aeda Buidhe Meg Eochacan ridamna Cheneoil Fiachach
o Clainn Colmain.
Ruaidri mac Dondchada meic Eogain Oic Dalaig, in lam chiuil chlarsige is binne bai i n-Erinn uile.
Gadra Eogan mac Tomaltaig, Oic meic Tomaltaig Moir ri Cula Find itir da fel Mure in fogamair.
Mac Gadra cetna Eogan, a shaith fein do mac, do eg do galar opand.
Diarmait mac Eogain Gadra do gabail tigernais a athar, & maith a maith do.
Mag Carthaig Mor ri Desmuman.
Tadg mac Magnusa meic Seoain Meic Branan
Corca Athclann do marbad per dolum la a derbrathair budein & la clainn a derbrathar, sechtmuin iar fel Micheil, dia hAine arai laithi sechtmaine, & da taisech ina inadh Domnall mac Cormaic fer urlamuis a marbtha-som & Uilliam mac Aoda mac meic Aeda.
Flainn tigerna t-Sil Mailruain & a derbrathair maille ris do marbad la Mailsechlainn Flainn, & taisech do gairm de fein iar sin.
luagad la n Domnaill i Connachtuib i cend Meic Uilliam Burc, co ndechatur diblinuib co Baile in Chlair & gur loiscset in baile d'aindeoin Tuadmuman & Meic Uilliam, co mbatur adaigh longphuirt ann & a ndiultadh fo bualad ann-siden, & do loscset Machuire Clainni Taidhg arabarach co ller & gur marbad moran ech & daine fo mac Conchobair Corcu Mruad leo Domnall.
Sluagadh reme-sidhe.
Eogan mac Duibgind mic Eogain aile mac Dubgaill do marbad ina tig fein per dolum la clainn Cholla meic Dubgaill.
Aed mac Uaithne Anligi & Tadg mac Muirchertaigh meic Tomaltuig Anlige
Calann Enair for Luan & fichet
Ogdoas.
Brian mac Taidg meic Meic Dondchada, tigerna Atha Cliath in Choruinn, do marbad la Tadg mac Briain Meic Dondchada & a chaoraigecht do bein de & blod mor dia muintir do marbad mar aen ris; & mac Meic Dondchada Toir Eogan do marbad for imruagad in la cetna-sin.
Brian mac Magnusa Mochan.
Ruaidri Bacach Neill do marbad la clainn Airt Neill & la slicht Enrigh Aimreidh.
Da mac Airt Neill & cethrur do slicht Enri do marbad i n-enlo la Conn mac Neill ina ndigail-side & maidm do thabairt forro.
Caslen Sligig do thabairt do chlainn Eogain Conchobair d'U Domnuill ar ulcuib re Ruaidri meic Briain & re clainn Toirrdealbaig Charraigh meic Domnaill.
Domnaill da asic doib doridisi & tigernus uatha as d'Ua Domnaill.
Da mac Eogain meic hI Conchobair Ruaid Domnall & Donnchad do marbad la Ruaidri mac hI Conchobair Duinn, & Conn mac Taidg Conchobair & Cathal mac Fedlim Find do gabail ann.
Connla mac Aeda Buide Meg Eochacan toisech Ceneil Fiachach do marbad forind Achad Buide Baile Atha ind Urchair la mac Airt meic Cuind I Maeilechlainn & la Clainn Cholmain i ndigaltus Airt meic Cuind do marbad lais-sim remi-side.
Sluagad la U Ruairc & la U n-Domnaill do dol for Cruachuin O Cupran do rigad hI Ruairc.
Ua Raigillig & Goill & Tellach Dunchada ara cind diblinuib & mac Aeda I Raigillig & mac in epscuip I Gallchobair do marbad eturro beos & eich & daine do lot etarro & O Domnuill & a sluagh d'impod & cin a lecan for Cruachuin don chur-sin.
Fuigell mallacht fer n-Erenn uile in Giustis Saxanach ler milled Tomas Iarla, cethramna do denam de le hIarla o Uaruic & la Diuci o Clarens a ndigail Tomas.
Giustis do denam do Iarla Cille Dara.
Indsoigid la Fedlimid Finn for chlainn Conchobair Ruaid la feli Croichi in Chomded isin fogamar & blod don feduin can ched da maithib do thecmail i cend baile Mailconuire & arrgad & etach in baile do thogbail leo & lotur as-side fa Enach?
crechatar in baile, & doronsat ni bad mmesa la cach ina sin Aed mac Dondchada Dubsuilig Conchobair do marbad leo & Brian mac mic M%e Gelbuide Conchobair, & imtigetar dar aindeoin a namat; & benais Maelconaire tuilled le haisic na snathaide dib & tidlaicid clann Domnaill da cined aisig can luach tabaig co brath.
Sith do denum d'Fedlimid Find fri slicht Conchobair Ruaid & fria cach co cotcind.
Nicalas mac Diarmata Carraig meic Murchada meic in Airchidechain Flannacan.
Tomaltach Mac Ceithernaig
Pilip Mag Uidir ridamna Fer Manach.
Calann Enair for Mairt & uathad fuirre
Conchobair Chorcu Mruad Conchobar
a suis clann a derbrathar.
Aed mac Eogain meic Domnaill meic Murcertuig
la slicht Ricairt a Burc & la Ruaidri mac Briain Conchobair do tharraing.
Tomas Plonced.
Domnall mac Cormaic meic Magnusa Meic Branan do marbad a l Lius n Dubthaig per dolum dar braguid mind & tslan rig & toisech t-Sil Muredaig la Conn mac Taidg Meic Branan iar n-umla do reme, & Emann mac Briain meic Magnusa do marbad mar oen ris.
Diarmait mac Murcertaig meic Aeda Conchobair
la clainn Conchobair Duinn Fedlim.
Aed mac Toirrdelbaig meic Ruadri meic Cathail Conchobair do marbad per dolum la slicht Eogain meic Ruaidri.
Mac Toirrdelbaig meic Fedlim meic Ruaidri do marbad d'orchur do tsoigit la fer do Manechaib.
Cathal mac Irial meic Fedlim Raigillig
Mac Uilliam meic Colla Meic Dubgoill do marbad la clainn Tomais meic Cathail Ferguil i n-Iarthar Mide oc techt on buannacht Laignig.
Cnomes imdo
Samrad & fogamar rotirim & na torti uile do techt co romoch.
Crecha anba la n Domnaill & la clainn Eogain Conchobair for caeraigecht Charpre & Clainni Dondchada alla anis do Slicech.
Mac Uilliam Burc do dol a Carpre & braigde les este.
Indsaigid la Mac n-Diarmata a n-Artich & Mac Cethernuig tanig do conngnam le lucht Artig do gabail les.
Cethai cloichsnechta d'ferthuin cachi taeba do Beltaini & tentech & tornech, cur mill moran blatha & ponuire & torad ar gach leith inar gabatur fo Erinn.
Cith dib so soir co mbid da ordlach no a tri in cach cloich de, co ndendais cneda mora arna dainib da mbendais, cur millsit l& matra a Moig Trega & im Chluain Lis Beci & in cach inadh inar gab.
Cith aile budthuaid curro mill moran i Mag Luirg & i manistir na Baille, & do tsnaifedh coiti for urlar in tempuill moir na manach, ut audiuimus o lucht in bali.
Flaithes Saxan do discail & cath do tabairt etarro la Casc & Iarlo o Uaruicc do marbad ann la horchur gunna & moran maille ris do tigernaib Saxan do marbad ann & in senri fein do gabail ann & a breth co Lundainn & a muchad iter da lebaid locais, o nir chubaid arm d'imbirt fair, & ilmile do doinib o sin amach; & gabais mac Diuici a d'Iorc lanrige Saxan & tanaig cach maith re lind i Saxanaib.
a Cu Coccriche Maelconuire adbur ollaman Shil Muredhaig do eg a mac Bale Locha Mesga a tig Meic Uilliam Burc
a Ros Riagla fa diden Dia & San Fronses & co n-airchisi Dia dia anmuin.
Comarba Cluana Conmaicne, red is mesa linn ina sin.
Briain do gabail dia braithrib fen.
Diarmait mac orchindig Ola Finn, sacart indraic idan, do marbad a suis fo chend feruinn.
In decanach Aed mac Diarmata Mochan do marbad for imtsreing na decanachta i n-abuinn Cille Icnichain.
Iarla do gairm do mac Tomas Iarla & a gabail la Clainn Charthaig.
Sluagad la n Domnuill a n-Ichtar Connacht cur crechloisc cuit meic in Chosnamuig Dubda do Tir Fiachrach.
Tadg Mac Diarmata Ruad tigerna Coillted Conchobair.
Ruaidri mac Briain Ballaig.
Sid do denam d'O Neill & d'O Domnaill amail dob ail le hO Neill, & mac Nell Budi do fuaslacad uad & nert a choiccid fein do gabail d'O Neill.
Indsoigid la Mac Gosdelb a ndiaid a braithrich budein & ingen Ferguil Oic Uiginn Elec do marbad doib uxur Conchobair Uiginn meic Ruaidri Oic, for Machuire na n-Oilech ina baile fein go donuige.
Cocad do erge itir Conchobair n-Donn & Ruaidri hUa Conchobair & mac Mailsechlainn Moduig do marbad eturro.
Tadg mac in Chalbaig Conchobair & mac Margrege in Enig ingine Cerbaill indraigthech Gall & Gaidel, do ecc don treguid.
Mac Priora Cille Magnenn do Geraltachaib do ecc don bas cetna.
Mac Dondchada meic Aeda Meg Uidir & Collae mac Oeda Meg Uidir do marbad
Mag Uidir do tregad a tigernuis & Emand a mac do gabail a inaid.
Crech la clainn Conchobair Falgi o Chenel Fiachach & Uatne mac Meg Eochacan & mac Neill Meic in t-Sinduigh & dias galloclaech do marbad leo.
Toirrdelbach Mailmuad do marbad d'orchur tsaigti
Nethe annma do beith isin bliadain-si blath na cno do techt fo fel Mure in fogamair & na geoid ar gur & silchur in t-Sathairn glass dia Luain.
Gobann na Brefne, in brugaid cetach conaig, do ecc
Gres do denam do lucht Artig a Cluain Ruis Iuchain i Moig Luirg gurro moid forra, gur marbad drong dib & gur gabad araile.
Calann Ienair for Cetain & aenmad fuirri, & inmad bliadain din cicalda & int ochtmad don cical solarda & in hi & bliadain
Eogan Mac Diarmata mac Conchobair in Aine ria fel Beruig.
Murcertach mac Tomaltuigh meic Imair Anligi.
Diarmait mac Seoain meic Moilsechlainn Ferguil
o clainn t-Seoain mic Domnaill Fergail.
Tomaltach mac Conchobair Meic Diarmata
Domnach na Paisi i mac Beol Atha Chasil Bracain o clainn Diarmata meic Ruaidri Meic Diarmata.
Uilliam mac Taidg Chaich meic Uilliam Chellaig
o mac Taidg meic Dondchada Chellaig.
Eogan mac in Fhindanaigh.
Teagmail iter Nell & O Domnaill & digbail romor do denam d'O Domnaill Mac Subne Fanad
& a mac do gabail a inaid Ruadri, & dar mo debrod maith in Mac Suibne.
Da mac Magnusa Chathain Gobraid & Ruadri Insescar do marbad la Mac Ugilin.
Maidm la Conn mac Aedo Buide foran Ruta & Mac Ugilin fen do marbad and Cormac & ali multi nobiles & ig
Mac Ugilin do marbad la hoirecht Chathan & in Ruta do chor as da los-sin.
Bresmaidm la slicht Mathgamna Raigillig for Tellach n-Dunchada cona comaentaigh Brefnech & Eolusach inar marbad da mac Ruaidri Raigillig & ali multi nobiles & ig
Morindsoigid la Cellaig forin Muine Liath.
Goill Iarthair Midhe do breith forro, Diudig & Petidig & Triialaig & Darsedaig & Dalatunaig, & brised ar Cellaig & Donnchad Cellaig & moran maille ris do ergabail ann & moran da cosigib & da cethernuibh do marbad.
Anmanna ingantacha do tidecht i nd Erinn o Righ Saxan gne baneich & dath buide fuirre & ingne bo acci & braige rofota & cend romor & erball rofata grana becfhindach; & cruithnecht & salann nochaithed, & gach ore da met do cuirti asa herball do thairngedh he, & do lecedh ara gluinib i in cach dorus da arde & do dol a marcaig fuirre.
Mac Siurtan Dexetra.
Iarla Oc Desmuman do lecin do Chlainn Charrthaig & Geroid mac in Iarla do anbfhaindechad lais.
Mane Sinnach, tigerna Muintiri Tadgan, & Tadg mac Maine do gabail a inaid.
Ualgarg mac Cathail Ballaig Ruairc
la muintir Eogain mic Lochlainn Ruairc.
Sluagad la Mac Uilliam Burc a n-Ib Maine do congnam la Tadg Caech Cellaig, & digbail romor do fo deoid iar ngabail neirt ar Manechaib o Suca siar & ar fagbail bragad uatha uile.
Coiccer noer arit do elod asin tsluag fo mac meic Bater a Burc & clainn Meic Muris & clainn Meic Siurtain & mac Meic in Miled et reliqua & a mbasgad uile etir gabail & marbad, acht Mac Siurtan fen do imthecht ar egin lotigti ar los a laime, & Mac Uilliam do imtecht fo mela.
Da mac Cathail Meg Ragnaill, Conchobar & Mailsechlainn, do marbad a n-oenlo la slicht Mailsechlainn Meg Ragnaill tri sechtmaine ria Notlaic ar marbad mac Conmaic meic Seoinin leo forin cocad-sin, & ar ndenam cosain don tir co Sliab Carbre & iar mbreith buada leo cusin lo-sin riam & ar ndortadh cech toictin forro nocur aith int enla.
In Gilla Glas mac Uigind do ecc i fogamur na bliadna-so.
Calann Enair for Aine; aile uathad fuirri;
Bliadain na n-Gras in bliadain-si.
Bodith mor
Ragnall mac Sefraid Meg Ragnaill adbur toisig Conmaicne.
Muircertach mac Fedlim Conchobair Falgi
Edubard mac Barun Delbnae do milled tria a mibesuib fein for Cuirt moir a n-Ath Cliath.
Crech la hArt in Bocain for Ledusachaib & Remann mac meic Ugin Ledus do marbad les & Lamalin mac Semais meic Barun Delbna do gabail do.
Morda do gabail d'Ua Gilla Patric ri Osraige.
Fedlim Mag Cochlan adbar righ Delbna.
Maelruanuidh mac Ferguil Meic Diarmata.
Maelruanaig mac Cathail meic Tomaltaig Meic Diarmata
la Cormac mac Ruaidri Meic Diarmata a mac Belach na hUrbron.
Dondchad mac Fergail meic Eogain meic Tigernain Moir Ruairc
O hUiginn Gillana Noem mac Ruadri Moir.
Conchobar mac Diarmata Conchobair Falgi.
Mac Murchada in t-Slebi Muris.
Brian Ger Flainn
Emann mac Domnaill Buide Ferguil.
Mac Aedagan Urmuman Gilla na Noem in
Uilliam mac Seoain meic Mailsechlainn Ferguil
Ercra greine in Luan ria mac Beltaine.
In cerc ag breith tri n-uige gech lai i n-Ard in Choillin a mbaile Murcertaigh Duib Meic Cinaith, & a ec fen iarom.
Tomas Mac Feoruis tigerna Atha na Rig & Conmaicne Duna Moir in senectute bona & a mac fein Tomas Oc ina inad, & ainm do gairm do mac Risderd Meic Feorais ina aduig.

Tadc mac Ruaidri Mec Donnchada
Sluaiged la Geroid Iarla Cille Dara a Cúiged Mumon co maithib Gall & Gaoidel Laigen leis, dar cumdaig caislen d'ainneoin Gaoidhel Muman ar Carroic Cítal.
Lenuis O Domnaill he began buidhne trid an Mide sa Mumain siar, tiagaid ar siubal a n-Ealla et gabaid caislen Cinn Tuirc & airgid an tir.
Tiagaid iar sin a n-Desmumoin Moir et gabaid caislen na Pailisi & caislen cois Mainge et tigid slan tare n-ais a Cundae Loimnig.
Doniat athtino I iar sin et cruinnighit Geraltaig na Muman im th Semas mac Iarla Desmuman et Goill Muman archena et Mag Carrthaig Riabhach & Cormac Oc mac Cormaic meic Taidc Me Carrthaig et Goill & Gaoidhil Midhe et Loighen & tiagaid co Luimnec et tinoilid Toirrdelbach mac Taidg Briain ri Tuadmuman et Mac Con Mara et Clann Ricaird & Sil Aódho morsluag ina n-aghaid, teid ant Iarla cona shluag trid Bealagh na Fadhbaighe et do Belach an Gamna, co ranic droichet comdaingen crainn dorinnedh d'Ó Briain ar Sinainn, do brised leisan Iarla an droichet-sin et anois oidche a foslongport sa tír, doní O Briain foslongport ele rena tháobh an oidhci cetna.
Arnamarac cuiris int Iarla a sluag a n-ordughad, & cuiris Goill & Gaoidhil Muman ar tus & cuiris Goill Midhe ar deredh a shluaig.
Tuirlingis Domnaill an becan buidhne do bi a mesc Ghall & gabaid an athghirre trid Mhóin na mac Brathur dochom Loimnigh, innsoighid na sluaig-sin Shil mac Briain na Goill & marbthar leo Barun Cingt et an Bernabalach Circistoban et moran do dheghdhaoinibh ele nac airmither ann so.
ni roibe do Ghallaib na do Gaoidhelaib don taob-sin aonnduine bad mo clú laimhe ina O Domnaill ac tabairt deirid sluaig Gall leis.
Calann Enair.
Aonbliadain dec et cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
O Concobair Failge Cathair mac Coinn meic an Calpaig, feithem coitcend congairec d'ecsib & d'ollamnaib Erenn & cend & gaiscid & gnathirgaili Iarthair Eorpa eisidhein, do marbad le cuid da chinedh fein clann Taidc Concobair et clann hSeain Ballaig Í Conchobair laim re Mainistir Feorais.
Dubthach mac Duthaig Duibhgennain, sai shaidhbir shochonaigh et fer lan d'egna & d'feli, d'fagbail bais isin bliadain-si.

Cenel Feradhaig do chrechadh do Maghnus O Domnaill an bliadain-si.
Mac Donnchada Thire hOilella Sean mac Taidc meic Briain Meic Donnchada, coinnel gaile et gaiscid Clainni Mailruanaid et feithem coitoenn d'eigsib & d'aes ealadan, d'fagbail bais ina longport fein a mac Baile in Duin, ni himlan do bi bliadain a tigernus; et Fergal mac Taidg meic Briain, adbar righ n Oilella, do marpad an bliadain cetna le clainn Ruaidri Meic Diarmata.

Da bliadain et cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
O Domnaill do techt on Roim iar forbadh a oilitri et iar fagbail onora moire o Righ Saxan fora cuairt.
O Clerigh Tuathal mac Taidc Caim Clerigh, sai re sencus & fer tighe oighed coitcinn, d'fagbail bais iar n-ongad & iar n-aithrige.
Niall mac Coinn meic Aodho Buidhe meic Briain Ballaig, tigerna Trin Congail & fer oinigh coitchinn d'feroib Erenn & medoighti ord & eclais et gac maithusa archena et ána oirtir Erenn, do dol d'ecc
Sluaiged le Geroid Iarla Cille Dara Giustis na hErenn ar Trian Congail, dar gab caislen Beoil Fersde et dar bris caislen Meic Eoin et dar airg na Glinne et moran don tir et tuc mac Nell meic Coinn a mbraighdenus leis.
Cocad mor etir O n-Domnaill Aodh & O Nell Art mac Aodho; et cocad eli itir O n-Domnaill & Mac Uilliam Burc Emand mac Ricaird; et do fhosdaig O Domnaill cet dec tuagh a Tir Conoill & a n-Ichtar Connacht & a Feraib Manach.
Gluaisis O Domnaill o Doire began buidhne et gapais caislen Beoil an Clair a coicrich Gaileng et fagpois barda and et teid tar ais co Tir Fiachrach.
Cruinnighis Mac Uilliam Burc et suighis fon mbaile, & arna cloisdin sin d'O Domnaill innsoighis in baile aris.
Facbais Mac Uilliam an baile et teid do chur lóin & bhárda a caislen Eisgrech Abann a Tir Fiachrach.
Arna cloisdin sin d'O Domhnaill lenais he tarrsna Shlebi Gamh.
Arna airiugad sin do Mac Uilliam fagbais a mac & uarda a caislen Eisgrec Abann et gabais fein roimhe docum Aird na Ríadh.
Beiridh O Domnaill radharc air et ligidh a mac air, teid Mac Uilliam fo shnamh na Múaidhi ass.
Lentar an cuid ele dá muintir tar Muaidh et bentar moran ech & éidigh dibh.
Suighis O Domnaill fa caislen Eisgreach Abann ann sin et gabais an caislen fo cenn ceitri la, & brisidh he iar sin et gabais mac Meic Uilliam Uillec mac Emainn & na bhardo uile & tic slan iarom.
Slúaiged leis O n-Domnaill a Tír Eogain co maithib Ichtair Connacht & co mbuannadhaibh imdho uime dar loisc da gac táobh co ranic Dun Genainn, & sídhaighis O Nell ris ar mbeith sechtmain sa tir da milledh, & maithis d'Ó Dhomnaill a roibhe eturra cios Cineil Moain & Innsi hEogain & Fher Manac uile.
Slúaighedh le Geróid Iarla Chille Dara Giuistis na hErenn tar Ath Lúain i Connachtaibh.
Crechais & loisgis Clainn Connmaigh.
Gabuis Ros Cumain & fagbais bharda ann.
Tét as sin a Magh Luirg & gabais caislen Bhaile na hUamha & millis moran don tír.
Tic Ó Domnaill sluagh mór da chois tresin Corrsliab do comrádh reisin Iarla & teid tar ais an oidhchi cetna da foslongport fein, co Breicsliab, & marbthar began da muintir a techt taris sa Bealach Buide; & suidhis iar sin fa chaislen Sligig & do mill duthaig shlechta Briain I Conchobair & ni ranic leis in caislen do gabáil in uair-sin.
Art mac Cuinn meic Nell Ghairb I Domnaill d'fagbail bais Obuinn do tháom thinnis a Múr na mac Brathar a n-Dun na n-Gall & a adhnacal sa mainesdir iar sin.
Calann Enair.
Tri bliadna dec et cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
Mairghrec inghen Concobair hI Briain ben Ruairc grianan glanruithnech na n-Gaoidel, an ben da dtuc Día rath & ríghe & rochonach, teallach feile & fircongbala, daonachta & derlaicti & deigheínigh d'éigsibh et d'ollamhnaibh, d'fannaibh & d'fíorthruaghaibh & da gac aon rigedh a les do thren no do truagh, an bhen nár eitigh aon fo athchuingid in gein roba beo, d'faghbail bais iar mbuaidh ongtha & aithrighe et a hadhnacal isin mhainesdir doroine fein a n-onoir Dhé & San Proinseis mainestir na Craoíbhe Léithi.
Donnchad mac Concobair hI Briain, fer crechach congháirec & cend fedhna feramail fírbheódho dobad mo oinech et uaisli & orrdercus da tanic do Dháil g Cais a comaimsir fris, do marbad a ngreis oidhqi le clainn Toirrdelbaig meic Murchada hI Briain.
O Domnaill Aodh do dul ar cuairt a cend Righ Alpan an bliadain-si.
Rosa mac Maghnuso Meg Mathgamhna tigerna Oirghiall.
Tadg mac Maoilsechlainn hI Chellaigh tigerna O Maine.
Máighisdir Muris O Fichellaig, doctuir diadhochta et se 'na airdespoc a Tuaim dobad mo clu cleirchechta thoir ina bus, do dol d'ecc an bliadain-si.
Geroid Iarla Cille Dara Giúisdis Erenn, ant ennduine rob ferr oinech et budh mo nert et clu et oirrdercus et is mo dorinne do gabaltus ar Ghaoideluibh et do bris do chaislenaib Gaoidel et dob ferr smacht et recht et righriaghail et is mo tuc da airneis fein d'feraib Erenn tanic do Ghallaib a n-Erinn riam, d'fagbail bais ola & ongthu et aitrighe a Cill Daro et a adhnocal a Tempall Crist a mac Baile Atha Cliath maille re tuirsi urmoir Gall & Gaidhel Erenn.
Sluaiged leis Nell Art mac Aodho a Trian Congail dar loisc Magh Line et dar chrech na Glinne, & ruc mac Nell meic Coinn & Mac Uibhlín ar chuid don tsluag & marbthar Aodh mac Nell don cur-sin.
Tecmaidh an sluag ele & an tóir da cheli arnamarach et marbthar Mac Uibilin Risderd mac Rúghraidhe & drong mor do Alpancoibh mailli fris, tig O Nell tar ais iar sin.
Sluaiged la Rig Alpan co maithib Alpan uime, da roibe mile fer congantu, a crichaib Saxan.
Loiscis et airgis an tir do gach táobh 'na timchell.
Cruinnighis Loard Seomurlin et a mac cliar hSaxan ina n-agaid.
Tucadh cath eturra & maighis ar Alpanachaib & marbthar Ri Alpan ann & Mac Ailin & Airdespoc Sanct Andrias et moran do tigernaib Alpan, & marbthar drong diairme do dháoinibh eturra.

Cathal Oc mac Domnaill meic Eogain Concobair do marbad a fiull grando do mac a athar fein Eoghan mac Domnaill; et as e Cathal mac a aosa is mo tuc et fuair tanic do slicht Briain Luighne meic Toirrdelbaig Moir, & ni he sin amain geall do bermais-ne ina lucht ar ceirde do, acht nac tanic do cinedhoip imdo a comaith a n-uaisle et a n-aithne et a n-einec, as dilechta truagh an ealadha da éis gan fer a himchair na a haltroim mar Chathal aice.

Emand a mac do righad ina inadh genco fuair a duthaig ueus; fer sein fa mó oinech & daonucht do Gallaib Erenn, bennacht na ndámh & na ndeóradh ria anmain.

Dá bliadain ar & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Cocad mor ar n-eirghi sa bliadain-si a rand iartharac na hEorpa etir cenelaib na Cristaigechta Romhanaigh & Edailligh & Almáinnigh & Spáinnigh & Saxanaigh d'énrann & d'encomairle a n-aghaid Righ Frangc a aonar acht Alpanaigh abain d'enrann re Righ Frangc, & moran cat & echt do imluadh eturra; & is amlaid fuaramar ó lucht sgaílte sgel & cuartaighe chúan, gurub ac Frangcaib do bi buaidh an chocaid-sin a n-aghaid na n-ilchenél.
Cocad adbal ar n-erghi a n-Erinn fein an bliadain sin et co hairithi a tuaiscert Erenn eidir n Domnaill & O Nell; & Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird & Goill & Gaoidil Connacht & Sil mac Briain & Sil Cerbaill ar cengal ris Ó Nell docom an chocaidhsin.
Ó Nell do thecht sluag mor co maithib Ulad & fecht Alpanac & moran do Ghallaib Midhe & gallóclaich Iarla Cille Dara a Tír Conaill & caislen Beoil Atha Senaigh do gabáil & Bun Drobaoisi & Bel Leici do loscad do, imthecht slan don dul-sin.
techt sluag mor ele 'na dhíaigh sin co luath a Tir Conaill & breith ar creich a Cionn Maghair & a lán don tír do milled.
O Domnaill do chruinniugad hsluaig moir eli a n-enait & Maghnus O Domnaill & maithi an tsluaig do dul a Tír Eogain & crecha mora & marbtha do denam doib.
O Neill do thinól hsluaig moir ele & Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Ricard mac Uilleg meic Uillec meic Uillec an Fhína & Goill & Gaoidil Connacht & O Cerbuill & clann Briain do cruinniugad 'na comdháil & do gealladur a coinne a celi a Tír Conaill; & tangadur an sluag Connachtach co Sligech, & tanic O Neill a Cenél Moáin & fecht Albanac aige fa mac Meic Domnaill Alusdur & moran do Ghallaib Midhe & do galloclaechaib Laignec.
Dala Domnaill & Ceneoil Conaill immorro, o nac rauadar lin laochraide na comtrom cathaigthe re cechtar don da hsluag-sin, is i comuirle dorinne fein & maithi Chineóil Conaill amus oidhce do thapairt ar O Neill & ara hsluag, dorinnedor coisighe da marchsluagh maille rena coirighthib; & do bi Ó Neill a foslonccport a Cnoc an Bhodha; & do innsaighedor Conollaig a hencomuirle iat gan congnam coicriche na carad aca & do brisedh ar Ó Neill an oidhchi-sin & do marbad moran da muintir etir Alpanacaibh & Erennachaib, co hairighthi do marbad moran do Gallaib & do galloclaechaib Laigen ann, & do marbad Mac Eoin na n-Glinnedh ann & moran Alpanac ele & drong mor do Clainn Domnaill Galloclaich & do Clainn t-Síthig, Ó Neill d'imthecht a cóir madma iar ndithiugad a muinntiri.
Ó Domnaill cona hsluag d'impódh maille re himad édalo d'echaib & d'étedh & gan comhnaide do dhénam doip no gur ghabhadar foslongport ac Beinn Gulpan; & an da Mac Uilliam & an da O Chonchobair & Mac Diarmata & O Cerbaill & clann hI Briain do beith sluag mor timchell hSligig, mur fuaradur derpscel an madma-sin do tabairt ar Ó Neill, acht ger mor a culad & a ndaoine, do imghedor a coir madhma, co nach fes d'Ó Domnaill a n-imtecht co ndecadur tar Coirshliab; & ger b'imdho cengal & combaidh dorinnedar na rannta-sin a n-agaid Conollach, gerb imdo ni da agra orra acna huaislib-sin, nior greamaighed & nir gnoaiged énni orra de sin.
Rugraidhe mac Gofradho meic Aodho Galldo & mac Me Cellaig na Brefne do marbad le sluag Neill a n-ucht Sgairbhe Innsi an Fráigh
Mac Meic hSuibhne Thíre Bághaine Brian an Coplaig & Diarmait mac Taidc Caim hI Cleirig & Aodh Mac an Baird & a lan ele fos do marbad a caislen Bheoil Atha Senuigh le sluag Neill.
Domnall mac Donnchada Ruairc, saí duine uasail na duthaig fein, do marbad le clainn Fheidlim Ruairc
Domnall mac Seain Chathain, saormaccam a chinidh fein & fer oinigh choitchinn d'ecsibh & d'aos eladna do marbad an bliadain-si.
Mag Gorman.
Maoilsechlainn, an ti dob ferr tuicsi & tech oighed don aos gradho, d'ecc an hoc. Maolruanaidh mac Cormaic meic Ruaidri Meic Diarmata, mac righ a aoísi & a inbhe is ferr tanic do maicne Maolruanaid a comaimsir fris, do ecc aran Carraic mac Bic & a ádhnacal a n-othurlighe a athar & a senathar a mainesdir na Buille.
Domnall Cleirech mac Seain meic Aibhne Chathain, cenn oinigh & engnama, testa & tuaruscbala an tuaisceirt, do marbad do clainn Gilla Patraic meic Maghnusa Chathain per dolum a altranda & a chairde Crist.
Rugraidhe mac Aodho Óic meic Aodho Ruaid Meg Mathgamna d'ecc in bliadain-sin.
Calann Enair.
Tri bliadna & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Doinend mor a tús na bliadna-sin & cocad úathmar adbalmor ar fedh an domhain ar muir & ar tír, & co hairithi etir O n-Domnaill & Ó Neill; & O Domnaill do beith a foslongport re hedh an erraig-sin a n-Glinn Fhinne, & Maghnus O Domnaill do dul a n-Alpain et techt slan iar crichniugad a cuarta; et O Domnaill do dol fa dó an bliadain-sin a Tir Eogain et techt slan iar milled morain et sith do denom deiredh bliadna doib gan echta oirrderca do denam eturra acht mar sin.
Ó Cathan Donnchad mac Seain Cathan, relta enigh & orrdercais, daonachta & daghoinigh a dhúthaige fein, d'ecc & dá thigerna do gairm i n-aghaid a celi 'na inadh Sean mac Tomais Cathan et Gofraidh mac Gofradho I Cathan, íat araon a cocad et a n-imresain fan tigernus.
Mac Briain Tadg mac Toirrdelbaig, fer a aosa dob ferr oinech et uaisle et rer mo egla a esgarad et dob ferddo cenn dam & deoradh & is lugha do diult re dreich nduine im ni da n-iarfad, arna marbad co mirathmar d'urchor do gunna leisan Giuistis Piarus Ruad Builter mar as gnath sai d'fagbail a n-aiscid.
Mac Gilla Eaáin Lachlainn mac Echaird do marbad a fiull leisin Ridire Mac Ailin a mbaile Rig Alpan
Mag Tigernain Ferghal mac Gilla Isa Oig meic Gilla Isa meic Briain
Tellaigh Dunchada, fer dércach daonachtach, d'fagbail bais ina baile fein & a derbrathair do gabail inaidh.
Eogan mac Feidlim meic Donnchada meic Tigernain Oic Ruairc do bathad ar Loch Glenna Édo.
Rosa mac Ruaidri meic Briain Meg Uidir d'fagbail bais a mbraighdenus acan comorbo Maguidir Cu Connacht.
Aodh mac Airt Thúathail, mac a aisi & a inme dobad mo clu einigh & uaisle da fhine, do marbad le Branachaib.
Mac Con Midhe Maoilsechlainn mac Seain meic hSolaim, sái re dán
Sluaigedh adbalmor la hIarla Cille Dara Geroid Iarla & la Gallaib Midhe & la Neill Conn mac Coinn meic Enri meic Eogain, ar Concobair Failge & ar Conoll Mordo & ar Gaoidil Laigin archena.
Na Gaoídil-sin uile d'anmoin ar sith Neill eturra & ant Iarla tar eis a ndernadur conuigi sin.
Neill do denam na sithi-sin.
Geill & braighde na n-Gaoidel-sin do tauairt a n-urlaim an Iarla d'O Neill a ngill re gac agra & re gac iarmordhacht da roibhe aige orra, & a sgarad fa shithcain re celi.
O Máille Cormac mac Eogain, feithem coitcenn & cend oinigh & engnamo Iarthair Connacht.
Domnall mac Tomais Maille do gabail a inaidh.
Insoigid le hO n-Domnaill & lena comaonta thíre & coigcriche co Brefhne Ruairc.
Gac nec dob innlúaidh dá roibhe sa tír ara cionn dochuadar le a crobhaib & le a crechaib a ndíamhraibh & and imdorchaib da n-imcoimet & do fabgadar clann Ruairc a n-úaiti shluaig & sochuide ar cionn an tsluaig.
O Domnaill d'imthecht an tire don turus-sin & an tir do loscad leis, & dobad lor da roibhe 'na n-agaid a ndernadar do dith doib, uair ni rucadar ara feidm na ar fognam do tabairt le cele don toisc-sin nogur fagaib Ó Domnaill in tir.
Sith do denamh doib iar sin.
Calann Enair.
Ceitri bliadna et cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
Doinend mor et ár for spreidh a tús na bliadna-sin.
Dis mac Domnaill Niall Garb & Eogan do cengal combadha cogaid re celi a n-agaid Domnaill, a mbeith tamall mar sin ac buaidhred an tire nogur cuiredh futha fein dol a n-agaid a celi; et Eogan do gabail baile Neill Gairb iar sin crannog Locha Bethad et si ara inchib fein, Niall d'fagbail an tire & innsoighid fhado do tauairt do aran mbaile et beith a celg a comfoccus dó, Eogan d'fagbail a fhesa sin et Niall d'innsoighid dó, a ndol fa celi ann sin et Eogan do marbad sa cachumusc-sin et Niall do lot et a dul d'eg do ghonaibh an luit-sin fo cenn aimsire girre 'na dhíaidh sin; & ni hurusa co tanic lucht a n-aosa do Cenel Conoill doba mó d'echtaib ina an dis-sin.
An ced mhí do hsamradh dorinnedh na marbhtha-sin.
Semass mac Briain Uaine Gallcubair, adbar comorba na Cairrge, d'fagbail bais
Diarmaid mac in Gilla Duib Briain, fer a tigernais fein dob ferr 'na aimsir do cend dámh & deorad & dobad mo muirer & moirtheghlach & dobad buaine blad & buaintesto & fer réidhighthi cest & caingen etir chairdib & nemcairdibh et is mó do saoíledh d'anmain re húain & re hinme a dhúthaige fein et fer cumainn & comparta d'aos ealadan ar dháonacht & ar deighenec, d'fagbail bais óngtha & aithrige a mac Baile Még Dhúbhda & bennacht De & na ndamh docom nime le a anmain.
Sluaiged les Ó n-Domnaill a Tir Eogain dar loisc & dar mill urmor an tire, & techt slan iarom.
Sluaiged leisan Giuisdis Geroid Iarla Cille Dara & les O Neill Conn mac Coinn a Tir Conaill a mi Medhoin Foghmair, sluaigedh leis O n-Domnaill a n-oircill na sluag-sin do cosnam a criche friu & moran Albanach ar techt cuige fon am-sin clann Eoin Cathánaigh & Mac Domnaill Galloclaech & daoine uaisle eli a hAlbain.
Dala an Ghiusdis & Neill dogabadur forbaisi & foslongport a Port na Tri Namad, Ó Domnaill cona hsluag do gabáil foslongpuirt a n-Druim Lighen, gellad buailti do beth eturu arnamarach, Maghnas O Domnaill & drong d'Alpanachaib do dul do hsoighdeoracht an oidchi-sin ar hsluag Gall et mac Broin do marbad leo an Calbach mac Broin meic Thaidc, echt mor na dhuthaig fein; et coinne hsithi do chengal etir na maithib-sin arnamarach, co nderna in Giusdis sith etir O n-Domhnaill et O Neill & he fein a slanaibh etura, dorinnedh sith & cairdes Crist mar an cetna etir an Giuisdis et O Domnaill.
ar filled don Giuisdis & d'O Neill fuaradur Aodh mac Nell meic Coinn meic Aodo Buidhe meic Briain Ballaig sluag mor ac milled Thire hEogain; & mar do chuala se na sluaig-sin do beith cuige do cuir a sluag fein roimhe le cuid do crechaib & d'édálaibh an tire et do an fein a fad a ndiaigh a muintire ar began daoine, noco rugadur tromlach an tsluaig ele air et gur innsaigedor he arna fagbail a mbaogal, gur marbad leo aran lathair-sin he.
ni thanic san aimsir deighenaigh do Cenel Eogain a comaith ar uaisle & ar oinec & ar orrdercas, ar delp & ar deighbesaib riogh & rotigernadh et ar clu a clann maicne do cosnom & is ferr do ditin & do deghcaomain a righe & a rotigernus co huair bhaoghail an bais.
Uair dob eisein ceinnleitir chothaigthe & congbalo a cinidh et fiorthobar na fele et cend uidhe an uird fhiled et relta hsoluis hsoinenta tslechta Coinn Cetcathaig, ni himarcach linn re radho nar fagaib se a n-Erinn d'uaislib Gaoidel na Gall domháoin et digbail is mo d'áos gacu dána sa doman ina Aodh mac Neill, &rl.-.
Mac Uibilin Cormac mac Seain Duib meic Domnaill do lott & do gabail a haithle an marbtha-sin le muintir Neill.
Inghen Domnaill Gormlaith ingen Aodho Ruaid ben Aodha meic Neill meic Cuinn ben dercac daonachtach deigheinigh da tuc Dia clú Ó sochraidh saogalta & dar ndoigh an flaithus firinnech fa deiredh, do dol d'ecc a mí medhoin erraig; et amhail tucadur an lanamhain-siu coimidecht daonachta & deigheinigh da celi sa saogal co haimsir a mbais, co tucaid a n-anmanna caomna & coimedecht ghlóire dá cheli a comhfhochair an Coimdedh.
Cocadh mor etir Cathanchaib an bliadain-sin dar marbad Cu Maighe mac Briain Finn Cathain et mac Ruaidri an Ruta Fer Dorchu; et marbthar aran cocad-sin fos le Gofraidh Cathain Aodh Carrach mac Dochartaigh et drong mor da muintir mar aon ris ar ndul do congnam le Sean mac Tomais Chathain.
Cú Maighe Ballach mac Domnaill I Chathain, fer a fhédhno fein dob ferr do duine uasal dá chinedh, do marbad le cuid don Rúta in hóc andó.
Mac Donnchada Thíre hOilella Ruaidri mac Tomaltaig meic Briain, d'fagbail bais et cocad mor idir Clainn n-Donnchada fa tigernus an tíre, & Mac Donnchada do ghairm do Chormac mac Taidc meic Briain.
O Conchobair Ciarraige Conmac mac Concobair do dol ar creich a n-Duthaig Ealla & Cormac Óc mac Cormaic meic Taidc do breith air & brisedh ar O Conchobair et he fein do lot & do gabail & Concobar mac Diarmata meic an Ghilla Duibh Briain do marbad ann & Diarmait mac Cormaic Maille, echt mor eli, do marbad ann fós.
Mag Carrthaig Riabac Domnall mac Finghin meic Diarmada do dol ar siubal creiche a n-Glinn Fhlesgi & breth air co hanordoighthi ac facbail an glenda & he fein do ghabail & cuid da daoinib do buain de.
Cathal Óc mac Meg Radhnaill, taoisec nertmar nosorrderc, tigerna Muintire hEolais & Cu Chulainn na Conmaicnec ar tréighib gaile & gaiscid et fer da tucadur tuath & eclais toil & tromgradh & aos gacu dana co deghthairsi, ar med & ar minca a tidhloiced & a tromtoirbert da gac aon, do marbad per dolum a mac Bealach Corrdoire a Muintir Cerballain le clainn Maoíl Mhíadhaig, gan adbar gan fhachain acht líamhantus breigi do denam air fa mhnaí Maoilmiadhaigh.
Mac Suibhne Thíre Bághaine Niall mac Eoghain, consapal dob ferr lam & dobad cruaide craidhe et comoirle et dob ferr tech oiged et uad mo muirer et is lia do bris do bernadhaib baogail da clainn maicne fein, do dul d'ecc iar n-ongad & iar n-aitrighe na caislen fhein a Rathain.
Inghen Briain Mor inghen Toirrdelbaig meic Taidc Briain ben Donnchada meic Mathamna Briain, do dul d'ecc an bliadain-sin.
Aibhilin ingen Ridire an Glenna ben Conchobair Ciarraighe, deighben dercach daonachtach, do dul d'eg
Toirrdhélpach mac Feidlim Buide meic Cairbre Conchobair do marbad le Toirrdelbach Ruad mac Taidc Buide meic Cathail Ruaid

bliadna & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
O Domnaill Aodh mac Aodho Ruaid & O Nell Conn mac Coinn do dul docom na comuirle moire, tús na bliadna-sa, a cend an Giuistis & maithi Gall & Gaoidel ann d'urmor, & tar eis a saothraighthi ann sin & morain tagra do denam and a n-agaid a cele da cairdib Gall & Gaoidel et doib fein nir cuiredh a crich sith do denam eturra an uair-sin, acht techt da tighib & ced cogad do beith eturra.
O Domnaill do dol fa dó a Tír Eogain an bliadain-si & moran don tir do milled & do loscad & gan tecmail ris uime sin.
Sith do denomh eturra tús foghmair amhail aderadh an Giuisdis et Maghnus O Domnaill.
Gniom uathmar arna denam a n-Erinn an bliadain-sin Espoc Lethglinne arna marbad a mebail le mac an Abad Meic Murchada & he faris fein maille re gradh & re sithcháin; & an méd ara ruc Iarla Cille Dara do lucht lamaighthi an gnima-sin, ruc leis iad gusan ait a ndernadh an dorath & an drochcomuirle-sin et tuc fo dera a fendadh beo ar tus et a n-apaige & a n-inathair do buain estib et a loscad diblinib 'na fiadhnaise iar sin.
O Cathain Sean mac Tomais do marbad do chuid da chined fein mac Ruaidri an Ruta Cathain & mac Gofraidh Cathain oidhci Lughnusa do shonnradh.
Espoc Cille Da Lúa Toirrdelbach mac Mathgamna Briain do dul d'ecc, ant en Gaoidel is mo fuair et is mo do sgaoil don tsaogal a coimre & a comaimsir fris, fer lan d'oinech & do daonacht ant espoc-sin et cosanta a chóra a tír & a coicrich, do dheoin & d'aindeoin, fer chuirthi sluaig moir co minic a cend a chéli do milled a esgcarad, co nac roibhe a comfhocus do 'na duthaig fein na a nduthaig eli mac Gaoidil nar ghab a thuillme et a tuarusdal; et ni eli fos, dob e ant espoc-sin ant echt osna hechtaib et an esbaid os gach esbaid da tarla re heladain a n-enaimsir ris.
An Decanach mac Briain Ruaid Meic Conmidhe, fer tighe oiged coitcinn do chach, a mac Cerball do dol d'ecc an hóc.
Inghen Duibhgennain Caiterfina do dol d'ecc iar n-ongad & iar n-aitrighe im fel Coluim Cille et a hadnacal co honorach a mainesdir Duin na n-Gall.

Tadg mac Eogain meic Thigernain Ruairc, dámhna & deghádhbar righ & rotigerna, do marbad la clainn Tigernain
Ó Neill Cond & Maghnus O Domnaill do dol a cend an Giuisdis do denam hsithi Conollach & Eoghanach, ar tinol morain do maithib Gall & Gaoidel da sidhughad nirb eidir a síthugad and sin, tangadar aimhreidh da tigibh.
Ó Raighillig Eogan do dol d'ecc et cogadh mor d'erghe idir a cinedh fa tigernus an tire nogur goired O Raighillig d'Fergal mac Seain meic Cathail do molad an Ghiúisdis et mhoráin do mhaithib Gall & Gaoidel, ge do badur daoine budh sine ina he a cur chuige.
Cocad mor ar n-erghi a n-Ichtar Connocht an bliadain-sin a n-urmor uile do cengal re celi a n-aghaid Domnaill, fa Brian mac Feidhlim Conchobair et fa mac Cathail Oic I Conchobair & fa hslicht Cormaic Meic Donnchada, & Iochtar Cairpre do crechad leo.
O Domnaill do brisiudh chaislein na Gráinsighi, dul a Magh Luirg do 'na dhíaigh sin & an tir do milled & do loscad les.
An t-Shíol Concobair-sin & an Clann Donnchada do bi aran cocad do cruinnechad et techt co Sligec doib & cur co maith dochom an caislein nogur marbad duine maith da muintir Ruaidri Ballach mac Airt.
imthecht doib an la-sin et cruinnechad fo chenn aithghirre aris et techt co Sligec doib do milled ghort et do chur dochom an baile.
O Domnaill d'fagbail sceil a mbeith mar sin et gluasacht cuctha et breith orra & a madmugad leis et cuid mor da ndaoinib do bhúain dib et edail mor ech & airm & éidid.
O Neill Conn do thecht do toirmesc oibre caislein do tinnsgain Maghnus O Domnaill do denam a Port na Tri Namad, Maghnus do thegmail re tus an tsluaig & mac Seain Neill Enri do gabáil les, Ó Neill d'imthecht a coir madhma.
O Cathain Gofraidh mac Gofradho do marbad a n-ucht Belaig an Chamáin le mac Neill le Niall Óc an cetmhí do shamhrad, & Niall fein do gabáil fa cend athghoirid 'na diaigh sin leis Ó Neill ocus a beith a mbráighdenus fhada.
Sean mac Aodho Meic Diarmata, an bethir beodho, do marbad le slicht Conchobair Ruaid iarna fhághbail a mbaogal for Mullach Croiche.
luaigedh la hIarla Cille Dara for Machaire Connacht ar forgall Concobair Ruaid, gur gab Baile Tobair Brighdi & an Caislen Riabach Chlainni Faghartaig ro thídhnaic d'Ua Conchobair iad.
Crecha mora do denom la clainn Ruaidri Meic Diarmata a Cuirr an Droichit ar Concobair Ruad & cuicfher no seiser da muintir do fhagbail doib.
Crecha mora do denam d'O Conchobair ar hslicht Taidc Meic Branain ina chinaidh-sin et Ruaidri mac Coinn Meic Branain do marbad le clainn Echmharcaig meic Conchobair Buide & le Toirrdelbach Ruad mac Taidc Buide a tempoll Tulcho & an tempall do loscad fair.
Aodh mac Taidc do dhíbirt asa dhúthaig Mac Branain.
Morhsluaiged le Ruairc Brian mac Eoghain meic Tigernáin a Muintir Eolois dar ghab nert for gac aird don tír et dar bhen geill & eideredha co hainndeonach dib fa dheóigh.
Mag Amhalgaidh do marbad le Maoilsechlainn dar sárughad an Iarla.
Mac Chathain Gofraidh mac Donnchada, adbar tigerna a thire fein, do dhul ar siubal chreiche a n-Glend Chon Cadhain a mí Ienair do thshinnredh, he fein d'fácbháil et nac frith enfhocal da sgelaib nogo frith a corp an tsechtmain déighenach don Chorghus ar cionn, Enri mac Nell meic Briain tigerna Baile na Bragad do marbad ann et moran eli do marbad & do lethad and maille riu da muintir.
Maidm do tabairt do mac Meic Piarais ar clainn Emainn meic Tomais Buitilér, du inar marbad Conchobar Oc mac Conchobair Cháoich Domnaill do bi 'na Consabla galloclaech et 'na laim maith co minic, co hairithe an la-sin, uair nir léic med a menman et fepus a laime do anacal do ghabail arna thaircsin do; et do thuit moran do daoinib maithi san maidm-sin do marcsluag et do ghalloclaechaib.
O Dochartaig Echmarcach tigerna hInnsi hEogain d'fagbail bhais a n-eirr a aoisi
et cocad mor idir a chinedh fa tigemus an tire, tigema do gairm do Geralt mac Domnaill meic Feidhlim Dochartaig.
Sloiged leis O n-Domnaill a Tir Amalghaidh do congnam le slicht Ricaird a Burc, Cáorthannan & Cros Máoilína do ghaabail et do brised dho et braighdi et édala mora asda sin et sith d'fagbail itir hsliocht Ricaird a Burc & Bairedachaib; et foslongport do denam do ara fhilled fa chaislen Chúl Máile et sith et praighde do buain do hslicht Cormaic Meic Donnchada, &rl.-.

Mac Donnchada Tire hOilella Cormac mac Taidg meic Briain do dol d'ecc et cocad mor itir Clainn n-Donnchada fa tigernus an tire 'na dhiaigh nogur goired Mac Donnchada d'Eogan mac Donnchada meic Murchada.

Domnall mac Feidlim meic Toirrdelbaig Carraig hI Conchobair.
O Clerigh an Gilla Riabach mac Taidc Chaim, sai re heladain & fer saidhbir, d'fagbail bais a n-aibid San Pronséis a mi medhoin Erraig.
Domnall mac an Espuic Gallcubair do marbad le cuid do hslicht Aonghais Gallcubair.
An Docduir mac Eogain Duinn Slébi, saí re leighus & annsna healadnaibh ele d'urmor & fer conaigh moiret tighi oiged, do dul d'ecc an tres la ria féil San Proinséis.
Mag Uidir do dol d'ecc an bliadain-si Concobar, & tigerna do denom don Comorba Mag Uidir 'na inadh.
Toirrdelbach mac Egnecain Domnaill do dol d'ecc.
Feidlim mac Gofradha meic hSeain Luirg Domnaill.
Sloiged leis O n-Domhnaill a Moigh Luirg & an tir do milled idir arbar & fhoirgnem et an Caislen Mor & an Bennada do ghabail do et caislen an Calaid et Baile na hUamha et an Caislen Ríabach, a mbrisedh diblinibh, marcach maith do marbad don tsluag a n-ucht an Belaig Buide Aodh Buide mac an Dubaltaig Gallchubair.
Caislen Lifhir do dhénomh le Maghnus O n-Domnaill a thinnsgna in Cetain iar fel Brenainn & a crichnugad le cuid don tsamhrad, itir obair crainn & chloichi, & cocad hI Neill air.
Maghnus Domhnaill do dul ar siubal chreche a n-Glinn Eli ar Aodh mac Buidhe O n-Domnaill & crech do tabairt leis, dis ocmarcach da muintir do marbad mac Domnaill meic Feidhlim meic Aonghais Óig Gallchubair & mac Briain Meic an Decánaigh.
Mac Maghnusa Me Guidir Tomás do dul d'ecc, sai clerigh & meic léighinn.
Ruaidri mac Murchada Meic hSúibne do mharbad da brathrib fein
Uilliam mac Aindrias Me Graith, fer saidbris moir & biadhtac maith, a ben do dol d'ecc a n-enló co n-oidhci.
Caitilin ingen Coinn meic Domnaill I Nell, ben dércach daonachtach do bi ac feraib maithi ac Ó Raigillig ar tus et ac Ruairc 'na diaigh sin, d'ecc iar n-ongad & iar n-aitrighe.
Iarla Chille Dara & mac Iarla Urmuman do dul a Saxanaibh tre imthnuth et tre innlach a cele, & a inadh fein a n-Erinn d'facbail don Giuisdis ac Barun Delbna.
Domnall mac Fergail Bhirnn d'ecc & a bainchele Lasair Fhina inghen hSeain meic an Priora.
Tadg mac Cairbre Birnn do gabail a inaidh da éis ar belaibh hsinnserhslechta Cormaic Birnn & Maoilsechlainn a brathair do gabail na tánaisdechta.
Mor ingen Maoilsechlainn Meic Cába uxor Aínligi, an ben dob fherr da tanic a Cenél Doftha riamh, banaltra damh & deorad na hErenn, aithghin Moire Muman ar clú & ar crabadh et ar deighbesibh, ben is mo tuc d'ofrail & d'almsanaibh bidh et édaigh do bochtaib & d'aighilgnechaib an Coimded & da gac aon riged a les, a heg ar lar a longpuirt fein a Purt Locha Leisi & a hadhnacal a mainesdir Oile Finn fo ditin De & San Proinseis.
In Prioir Óc Fergail Tomas mac Emuinn meic Rosa, tigerna Chalaid na hAngaile & an cóicedh cúibhrenn is ferr do bi do Clannaib Rugraidhe, do marbad le clainn Emainn Cellaig & la slicht Fédhlim meic Gillananaem Fergail & a triur mac maille
Forbhais a no a do hsechtmhainibh le clainn Ruaidri Meic Diarmata & le clainn Taidc Meic Diarmata & le Mac n-Dúbhgaill & le slicht Conchobair Ruaid & le slicht Fedhlim Finn & le slicht Taidc Meic Branain fa Chaislen Ríabach Chlainni Fagartaig, & muc ingnad do denam chuigi do shailgibh daracha et cetri rothada imluith fuighthi.
Diarmaid mac Taidc Ruaid meic Cairpri & marcach maith do Clainn Maoilruanaidh do marbadh a timcell an baile & an muc do gerradh fa dheóigh la Tuathal Ruad mac Cuinn & le bardaib an baile & an caislen do cosnam co harrachta doib co tanic an ní innrus gac n-inill & disgaílus gac daingen & an teidm nach eidir d'fulang an gorta, gurb eigin doib an caislen do tabairt amach, ro maithed a n-anmanna doibh.
Calann Enair.
Ocht mbliadna fichet et cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Ingen Briain Finnghuala inghen Concobair, an ben as mó do cosoin do clu a comaimsir ria do tháob a cuirp & a hanmo, do dol d'ecc ar caithem a haoisi & a haimsire re daonacht ar tús, ar mbeith bliadain ar fhichit a n-aibid an tres uird ac denam crabaid et daonachta et deghoibrighthi do taobh De et an tsaogail.
O Briain Toirrdelbach mac Taidc, an mac Gaoidil dob faide re huaisli et re henech do Leth Mogha et oigri diles Bhriain Bhóromha meic Cinneidig ar congbail cogaid re Gallaib d'fagbail bais iar n-ongad et iar n-aitrighe et a mac do rigad ina inad Conchobar mac Toirrdelbaig.
Mac Diarmata Moighe Luirg Cormac mac Ruaidri Meic Diarmata, feichem coitcend conghairec ar enec & ar feli & ar fhiordaonacht d'aos gaca cerde, mir cruadha na Connachtach an Cormac-sin et fer cosanta a criche et a chaomcarat ara escairdib e, a dul d'ecc iar n-ongad et iar n-aithridhi a ndeired a aoisi & a aimsire et a derbrathair fein Diarmait do gabail a inaidh.
Conn mac Neill meic Airt Neill, cend fedhna do Chinél Eogain, do marbad le mac Airt Neill; et dis mac Neill clann Airt Oic, Énri & Cormac, do bi a llaim ac Neill a bfad roime-sin, do tabairt do chlainn Coinn meic Neill et clann Coind do crochad na deisi mac righ-sin.
Caislen Cul Maile do gabail ar Mac n-Donnchada da derbrathair fein do Murcertach mac Donnchada meic Murchada, Mac Donnchada fein & a mac Murchad do gabáil fo cenn goirid 'na diaigh sin leis O n-Dubda et le Murcertach Mac n-Donnchada, mac eli Meic Donnchada do marbad don dul-sin Donnchad.
Sloighed leis O n-Domnaill a Magh Luirg a rabadar moran Albanac fa Alusdrann mac Eoin Cathanaigh, an Belach Buide do gerradh doib et braighdi & cios d'fagbail on tir, & techt slan iarom.
O Ruairc Eogan mac Tigernain Ruairc, cinnleitir na Conmaicnech et oidri súaithnid sen Fergail et uaithne enigh et orrdercois iarthair na hEorpa et triath tuicsec toirpertec tromchonaigh et fer cendsaighti a comarsann & cothaigthe gac cruadhcogaid arna coicrichaib et ursa uaisle & fhiorfhuloing hslechta Aodha Finn meic Fergna meic Ferghusa, d'fagbail bais a n-aibid San Froinseis iar n-ongad et iar n-aitrighe.
Mac Suibne Fánad Domnall Óc ar cur aibidi an Uird Mure uime la fhéli Mure san geimhred.
Gaoth mor ar techt sa bliadain-si an Aoine ria Notlaic et do leg moran do crannaib & d'oibrechaib croinn et cloichi ar fud Erenn & co hairithi múr mainesdrec Duin na n-Gall do brisedh di, do fhúadoigh et do bris moran d'artraighibh ar muir & ar tír.
Muris mac Donnchada Beigléighinn, saí re leighus, d'fagbail bais ongtha & aithrighe.
Maghnus mac Domnaill Meic Aodhagain.
O Máoil Míadaigh taoisec Theallaig Cerbhallain Cathal mac Domnaill meic Uaithne Buidhe.
Calann Enair.
Noi mbliadna fichet et cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
Conn Oc Baigill tánuisde a thalman fein do marbad le clainn Baigill an bliadain-si.
Iarla Desmuman Semus, ant enmac Goild uad mo clú enigh et uaisle do bi a n-Erinn et do bi na ursainn cocaid re Gallaib et re Gaoidelaib et dob ferr do cenn dámh & deorad, do dul d'ecc a lar a aoisi et a inme do galar obann tri n-oidhci, im fel San Seain.
Fedlim mac Conchobair Baigill do marbad le clainn Baigill.
Mac Meic Dubgaill na hAlpan do marbad le hAodh mac Buidhe O n-Domnaill a ndorus caislein Cule Meic an Trein d'enbuilde claidib.
Caislen Cuile Meic an Trein do gabáil fo cend athghoirid 'na diaigh sin le Maghnus O n-Domnaill et a brised.
O hUiginn Domnall Cam, saí re dan & re fogluim, do dol d'ecc.
Mac Uiginn Aodh mac Glaisne, saí re dan.
Brian Ballach mac Neill meic Cuinn do marbad le Cormac Mac Uibhelin et he ar muinnterus Briain fein ac faguail Cairrge Ferghusa.
An Cosnomaigh mac Fergail meic Donnchada Duib Meic Aodagain, an fer fa horrderca a fenechus & re filidecht & sepultus a n-Oil Finn.
Domnall mac Eoin Meic Birrthagra, adbar ollaman an tuaisceirt re berla Fene, d'ecc;
Semus mac Ruaidri Meic Birrthagra mur an cetna.
Mac Cailin Cailin mac Gilla Espuic, enrogha a n-Oirir Ghaoidhelaib uile ar engnam & ar oinec.
Domnall mac Aodho meic Domhnaill Mac Aodhagan Urmuman cenn egna & eolais Lethe Mogha.
Mac Feorais Dhúna Moir Maoilir.

mbliadna fichet et cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
Caitilin inghen Murchada Meic hSuibhni ben Dochartaig d'ecc.
Rois ingen Cathain ben Dochartaig d'ecc.
sloiged leis Ó n-Domnaill a mi medhoin hsamhraid a coiced Connocht dar gabadh leis trid Coilltib Conchobair ar fad et as-sin trid an Tanuisdecht Moighi Luirg et do Charadh Droma Ruisc tar Sinoinn, & Muinter Eolais do milled & do loscad leis; et cuid da dháoinib do buain de fa caislen Liath Droma Maghnus mac Fir Dorca Meic hSuibne et mac Meic Coilín Toirrdelbach Dub; et gabais as sin aris tar Sinoinn siar et do Machaire Connacht et do droichet Beoil Atha Modho tar Succu et Clann Chunnmaig do loscad et do chrechadh leis, baile Meic Dabhí Glinnsge et Cill Cruáin do loscad leis et edala imdho do tabairt asa tir, Baile an Tobair do milled & do loscad leis et cios cosanta d'facbail ar Ó Conchocair Ruad se pinginne sa chethramhain da dhúthaig; et gabais trid an mac Belach mac Buide ara fhilled gan dith do denam do.
Tech cranngaile is ferr do bi a n-Erinn ac Mac Contsnama ar Loch Aillinne do loscad leis o n-Domnaill & an Brefne o Sliab siar do milled do.
Sorcha ingen Aodho Oic meic Aodho an Enigh meic Neill meic Coinn uxor Neill Conn mac Coinn meic Enrí, do dol d'ecc.
Cathal mac Ruaidri Meic Diarmata, cenn fedhna is mo do bhuaidhir & do bhúainmill da bhidhbadaib & da escaraid a comaimsir fris et dob ferr do cenn damh & deorad & deibhlen & d'aos gaca cerde archena, d'ecc.
Mac Artain
Chineoil Fhoghurtaig.
Mac Domnaill Colla mac Colla consable Tiri hEogain meic Neill Noígiallaig.
Cumsgrach mac Maoilruanaidh meic Conchobair Meg Radhnaill.
Crech mor do denam d'Aodh Buide Ó Dhomnaill a n-Gailengaib.
Sloiged leis O n-Domnaill a mi medhoin foghmair ar Mac Uilliam Burc, dar mill cuid don tir et sith do denam doib iar sin, & O Domnaill do thecht slan acht marcach maith do marbad don tsluag Aod mac Conchobair Riabaig Duibidir.
Rugraidhe Ó Dochartaig, echt mor 'na duthaig fein, d'ecc.
Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Ricard mac Uilleic meic Uilleic meic Uilleic an Fhína, cinnletir Gall & Gaoidel Uachtair Connacht et an ti dob ferr enec & uaisle & dobad daingne smacht & riagail tanic do hslicht Uilliam Congcuir re cian d'aimsir, d'fagbail bais do galar aithgherr an mí deiginech d'errach.
Caibidil na mac Brathar Minur a n-Dun na n-Gall an bliadain-sin et O Domnaill da tabairt amach uile o thús co deredh maille re caithem mor & re sochraidhecht orrdherc onora
Espoc Oile Finn ant Espoc Gregac d'ecc, ni hoilbeim don daonacht ant ecc-sin.

Ingen Meic an Baird Una d'ecc.
Ingen Torrdelbaig Baigill d'ecc in hóc ando.

Mac Docartaig Niall mac Conchobair Carraig.
Diarmait mac Seain meic Aodho mec Maoilruanaidh, duine dob eile & dob firuaisle do slicht Maolruanaid Meic Donnchada, d'eg.
Cocad mor a Tír Conoill an bliadain-si itir O n-Domnaill & a mac Maghnus O Domnaill, O Domnaill do cur shluaig moir a n-enait & dol a nduthaig Maghnusa & an tir do milled do et mac Donnchada Chaoich Meg Uidir, duine uasal maith d'Feroib Manac, do marpad aran sluaigedh-sin ar imruacad a n-ucht Sgairbe Bechóige; et Maghnus do thecht a Tir Aodho iar sin & moran don tir do milledh.
Mac Uibilin Cormac, cend féthno maith et fer enig coitchinn, d'fagbail bais co hobann
Sluaigedh leisan n-Giuisdis Saxanach Uilliam Sgeimeltún a Tir Eogain et O Domnaill do dol na coinne et caislen Chinn Aird do brised et an tir do milledh, & Brian mac Lochlainn Meic Shuibhne Consabla galloclaech Iarla Urmuman do marbhadh a mbruigin aran sluaigedh-sin.
Illann Buide mac Maoilsechlainn meic Illainn Meic an Legha, saí re leigius, d'ecc in bliadain-sin.
Sile Óc ingen Cairbre Birnn, ben a haoisi & a hinbhe dob ferr dealp & daonacht & deighbhesa da tanic d'inghin taoisigh do Shiol Muredaig meic Fergusa 'na coimre, d'fagbail bais et a hadhnacal a Ros Chumain a n-othurlighe a sen et a sinnser.
Tuathal mac Í Dhomhnallain Mhachaire Maonmuighi.
Gilla Patraic mac Ádhoimh Meic an Baird.

Da bliadain ar & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
O Domnaill do dol a cend an Giuisdis Uilliam Sgemhaltun et rann do cengal ris et an Giuisdis Saxanac-sin do thecht a Tir Eogain et Dun Genoinn do brised do & an tir do milled.
Iarla Cille Dara, Geroid mac Geroid, do thecht o Shaxanaibh & Giuisdisecht na hErenn do tabairt leis on Righ.
O Domnaill do dol a Moigh Luirg & Mac Domnaill leis Alasdrann mac Eoin Cathanaigh, & crecha & loisce do denam doibh & sith do denam co luath 'na diaigh sin eturra.
Clann Neill clann Airt Oic, Domnall et Tuathal, do bi a fad a mbraighdenus ac O Nell, do crochad leis
Eogan mac Tigernain Ruairc, sai duine uasuil & adbar tigerna ar uaisle et ar enech & ar oirbert da tabrad Dia re no aimsir do, do marbad le clainn Máoilmiadhaig a mbaile na mac Brathar a n-Droim Da Eithíar.
Mac Meg Flannchaid Toirrdelbach do marbad da dis brathar fein a ndorus baile Meg Flannchaid, & O Ruairc Brian mac Eogain meic Tigernain Ruairc do milled morain a n-Dartraighe trid-sin.
Ingen Meic Shuibne Fhanad Máire ben Í Bhaigill d'fagbail bais co hobann arna hescur da hech a ndorus a baile fein.
O Maoilconaire Torna mac Torna, fer a inaidh is ferr tanic a n-ollamnocht hSiol Muredaig, & O Maolconaire do ghairm do Choncobar mac Domnaill Ruaid Maoilconuire 'na inadh, a dhul d'ecc co luath 'na diaigh sin.
Caislen Aird na Ríadh do gabáil le clainn Dúbda ar mac Seain a Burc, & cocad mor eturra & slicht Ricaird a Burc & moran crech & marbtha do denam doib ara cele
O Cerbháill Maolruanaid mac Seain Cerbaill, ant en Ghaoidel dob uaisle & dob orrderca a Leith Mogha & is mo do mill fa Gallaib et da lesoigh fa Ghaoídelaib et an fer nar diult re drech nduine an géin ro boi 'na bethaid, d'fagbail bais.
Comorba Fidhnaca Brian.
Mac Uibilin Ualter mac Geroid do marbad a n-eclais Duine Bó & Concobar mac Enri Cathain, fer toictec tromconaigh, do loscad ann & Mac Conuladh do gabáil ann.
Clann Domnaill Cleirigh Cathain dorinne na gnioma-sin.
Mac Iarla Urmuman Tomas mac Piarais Ruaid do marbad a n-Osraige le Diarmait Mac Gilla Patraic adbar righ Osraidhe, ni mor narb e-sein echt Maoile Moire.
Daigh nirbo cian iar sin gur toirbhredh Diarmait la a derbrathair fein la Mac Gilla Patraic don Iarla Urmuimnec, ro cenglad Diarmait iarom lasan Iarla a ndigail a meic & gac uilc archena da ndernad le Diarmait ris riamh.
Dub Chábblaigh ingen Choncobair meic Ruaidri Buide ben Concobair Óic meic Murcertaigh.

Caislen Sligig do gabáil le Tadc Oc mac Taidc meic Aodho I Conchobair ar innsoigid oidhci ar fagbail thseólta & cur amach air o cuid do lucht coimeto an caislein fein.
Caislen Aird na Ríadh do gabail do clainn Tomais a Burc ar clainn Dubhda san oidhce mur an cetna.
Crech mor do denam d'Ó Domnaill ar n Éghra mac Buidhe itir dá Abainn.
Niall mac Murchada Meic hSuibhne do marbad ar droichet Sligig, ant ocmacamh dob ferr do shlicht Donnchada Moir
Muircertach mac Feidlim meic Toirrdelbaig Carraig Conchobair do crochad leis O n-Domnaill ar faigthi caislein Enaigh ar ndiultad an baile do tabairt ass da clainn et da braithrib fein.
Mac Diarmata Moighe Luirg Diarmait mac Ruaidri Meic Diarmata rea raidhti Diarmait an Enigh, cend forais et firchongbala gacu filed et tócbala gacu truaigh & cothaigthe gac clainni & furtaighthe gacu hesbada, & dlái dhíana na daonachta, an fer is mo do dháil & do dherlaic da tanic do maicne Maoilruanaidh Moir a coimre & a comaimsir fris, do marbad per dolum le clainn Eogain meic Thaidc Meic Diarmata et Eogan mac Taidc do gabáil tigernais 'na diaigh.
Maolruanaidh Óc mac Maoilruanaidh Cerbaill do dol d'ecc.
O Maolmuaidh Domnall Caoch mac an Cosnamoigh do marbad per dolum lena derbrathair & le mac a derbrathar ar faighti Loinn Eala et O Maoilmuaidh do gairm da derbrathair do Chathaoir.
Emand mac Coinn meic Neill do marbad le clainn Meg Uidir.
Feidlimid Bacach mac Neill meic Coind, enrogha mac righ Chlainni Aodho Buidhe.

Ceitri bliadna ar & cet & mile aois an Tigerna.
Mac Meic Eochada Donnchad mac Maolmure Meic Eochada, adbar ollamhan Chóicid Laighen gan imresuin et fer a hsaothair fein dob ferr and gach uile gne don ealadhoin, dob ferr do thighesac, do marbad co tubaisdech d'aonurchar do gha le derbhráthribh a mathar fein clann Túathail.
Toirrdelbach Dub O Dimasuigh do marpad per dolum lena brathribh fein Muircertach Oc Ua Dimasaigh & le cuid ele da brathribh ar slanaib De et Éibhín Naoimh; et Murcertach Oc fein do marbad co lúath 'na dhíaigh sin leis Ó Mórrdha tre chumhochtaib Dé & Éibhín.
Eogan mac Aodho meic Nell meic Coinn, an mac righ dob ferr do hslicht Aodho Buide, do marbad le hAlbanchaib d'enurchar do hsoighid ar Loch Cúan.
Eogan mac Taidc meic Ruaidri Óic meic Ruaidri Caoich Meic Diarmata, do bi bliadain a tigernus Moighi Luirg, fer lan d'einech et d'uaisle et cenn fedhna crechach conghairech et fer nar chodoil gan crech no comaidh co hainndeónach ona escaraid et fer maoínedh & moronora do thabairt d'aos gacu dána co deghordaighthi, d'faghbail bais ar Carraic Meic Diarmata iar n-ongadh & iar n-aitrighe et Mac Diarmata do ghairm 'na inadh d'Aodh mac Cormaic meic Ruaidri Meic Diarmata; et clann Taidg Meic Diarmata do gabáil na Cairrge ar Mac n-Diarmata iar sin.
Iarla Cille Dara Geroid mac Geroid meic Tomais do dol a Saxanaibh fa thoghairm Righ Saxan et ant Iarla do chur chom pais ant enmac Goill doba mó do sgél do bi re linn a n-Erinn; et mac an Iarla Tomás do milled muinter Righ Saxan a ndigail a athar in gac ait a rabadar a n-Erinn gac uile duine da roibe a Muinechan as ar fedh na Midhe, a mbailti do brised & a mbraighde do buin dib; et Airdespoc Baile Atha Cliath do marbad aran cocad-sin; et Giuisdis Saxanach do thecht a n-Erinn on Righ et bailti meic an Iarla do brisedh d'urmor dó & an Midhe uile do milled itir cill & tuaith & uilc imdo do genamh eturra & co hairithi Magh Núad do gabail leisan Giusidis Saxanach & echta mora do muintir an Iarla do marbad ann.
Ó Conchobair Ruad Tadc Buide mac Cathail Ruaid d'fagbail bais an bliadain-sin & O Conchobair do gairm da mac 'na inadh do Toirrdelbach Ruad.
Brian mac Seain Maoilmúaidh do marbad a feall le cuid da chined fein.
Ó Gallcubair Emann mac Eoin meic Tuathail d'fagbail bais oboinn
Cormac mac Fergail Meic an Baird, saí re dan & duine dob ferr da cinedh fein do taob dercc & dáonachta, d'fagbail bais do galar obann iar n-ongad & iar n-aithrige.

Murcertach mac Donnchada meic Murchada & a dhias mac Sean Glas & Fergal do marbad le n Egra mac Buidhe arna cur amach co meplach do neoch da muintir fein a Maigh Imlech in hóc ando.

Eignecan mac Domnaill Domnaill do marbad le clain Baigill mur an cetna co nemmaith.
Maoilsechlainn mac Cairbre Birn, ant enmac taoisigh dobo mó sonus et sáibhres et dobo mo clú daonachta & deighenigh et ant enmac leighinn dobo coimhdheisi et dobad clisti ann gac uile eladain da roibhe a cúig coicedhoibh Erenn, do marbad le clainn Cathail Meic Diarmata oidhci fheli Brenainn a Mullach na Sithi, ant enfer dobad coitchinne cumaidh & cíantuirsi ag áos egna & eládna na hErenn, & bennacht De & na ndamh le anmoin.
Inghen Neill Siubhán ingen Coinn meic Énrí meic Eogain ben Maghnusa Domnaill, d'fagbail bais as lár a haoisi & a hinme & a huile maithessa, & a hadnacal co honorac a manisdir Duin na n-Gall.
Maidm mor do tabairt le Mac Amhlaib an bliadain-si inar marbad tigerna na Claonglaisi & Mac Gibun & corughad mor do Chlainn t-Síthig, marbthar ann fós mac Maoílmuire meic Briain Meic hSúibhne consable Meic Amhlaibh a tosac an imbuailti.
Tomás mac Iarla Cilde Dara do chengal re Gáoidhelaib dheisceirt Erenn an bliadain-si a n-aghaid an Ghiuisdis hSasanaigh tar éis a mainér & a bhailted do buain do mac an Iarla et he fein & gac rann da roibhe aige d'innarba asin Midhe, & a cur a n-ucht hSiol mac Briain & Choncobair Fhailghe et cocad maith aige gá dhenam.
Is ann sin tanic duine cumhochtach do muintir Righ Saxan a n-Erinn Loard Linard; & tanic a cend meic an Iarla & tuc cheilg uime et do gheall parrdún dó a hucht an Righ, ruc leis a Saxanuibh hé; et gabtar mac an Iarla et curthar a tur an Righ hé a mbraighdenus et tanic Loard Linard a n-Erinn arís.
fuair an Giúsdis do bi abus bas Uilliam Sgemeltun et gabais Loard Linard fedhmannus an Righ chuige.
tuc clann Iarla móir Cille Dara chuige fora inchaib fein clann Geróid meic Thomais, Semus & Oiliuér, Seán & Risderd, & ar mbeith doibh for taobad & for inchaib Loard Linard & siad na coimedecht fein do gab a n-aoínecht iad & do chuir d'innsoigid Righ Sasan iad, & curthar a tur an Righ iad mur a roibe oigre na hiarlochta Tomas mac an Iarla; & ar mbeith tuilled & bliadain a laimh dóibh fein & do Tomas do cuired docom bais a cethrur iad a fíadhnaise luchta na catrach; & ni thanic do Ghallaib Erenn fer a aosa fein dobad mó do sgel do thaob daonachta et cendois fédhna ina in Tomas-sin mac ann Iarla, & ni mo senmoir da tanic a ndeired na haimsire ina a girre do bi slicht na hiarlachta da sgris a hErinn & tren Erenn uile aca re fado d'aimsir roime sin.
Gurob mesa a cinn bliadna sibh, a chethernnadha dona duilp, is balech do dallabhair sinn.

Ó Cellaig in hoc ando.
Maithi Ichtair Connacht Tadc Occ mac Taidc meic Aodho et Tadc mac Cathail Oic Conchobair et Clann Donnchada et clann Dubdho, do dol ar hslicht Ricaird a Burc ar tarroing an Espuic Bairéd, cáoraighecht an tíri do dol rompo a Termann Oiridh et ant Espoc dá tabairt asin termann d'innsoigid an tsluaig, gan a n-aisec da éis a n-onoir a Naoimh.
