Comorba Droma Airbelaig Cathal mac Seoinin meic hSeain Maoilmocherghi, fer beotlusach buanconáigh, d'fagbail bais
O Conchobair do gairm do Tadc Oc mac Taidc meic Aodo meic Toirrdelbaig Carraig Conchobair, & nirb e sin ainm bad gnath leisin te bad tigerna do hSiol Conchobair a n-Ichtar Connacht do gairm de, acht Mac Domnaill Meic Murcertaigh et is d'furuaisliugad a aicme et do derrsgnugad dona rigaib roimhe doron-somh an claochladh comanma sin do gairm de.
Ant Ua Conchobair nua-sin & mac Cathail Óic Conchobair do dol ar siubal innsoighthe a Clainn Goisdealb et ni rucadar ar morán creichi, & dochuadar timcell Cille Colmain baile meic Rúghraide Meic Gosdelb, tanic fein a laim Conchobair asin baile maille re luirech comhradhach do bi aige luirech Meic Feorais, tuc Conchobair an braighi-sin co Sligech a ngiull rena lanfhuasclad.
Cocad suthain sirbhúan idir O n-Domnaill et maithi Ichtair Connacht acht Brian O Ruairc amháin gan congnam le cechtar dibh an tan-sin.
Sluaigedh adbalmor do cruinniugad leis O n-Domnaill a n-éninadh Mag Uidir & mac Nell Niall Óc mac Airt et Aodh mac Maoilmórdha Raigillig co n-eirghi amach Raigillig, tangadur clann Domnaill ann acht Magnus 'na aonar do bi a n-esaonta rena a athair, tangadar Clann t-Suibne & O Baigill a sochraide Domnaill.
Gluaisis an sluag sénta somothaigthe-sin im dheógh lái ó Áth Senaigh gur gabadar sosadh & ssithlongport idir Duibh & Drobaoís, tar eis a tomaltais do caithem doib do cuiredor lucht foraire & forcoimeda aran sluag d'egla amais longpuirt do thabairt do hSil Conchobair orra, oir do badar cruinn ara cinn a n-enunadh a Sligech & gelladh buailti aca d'O Domnaill.
as e dochuaid d'foraire do hsluag Domnaill an oidhce-sin O Baigill, uair dobad doigh leis go bfuigbad drem ecin da lucht imresna & imarbhágha a n-Ichtar Connacht ac techt do thabairt amuis longpuirt ar O n-Domnaill; et dochuaid muinter Aodho Buide Domnaill a foraire mur an cetna, & do buailedh O Baighill et iad fein fa cele a cripuscal na maidne muiche et do innsoighedor muinter meic Domhnaill a coinde et a comdáil a celi & Ó Baigill cona marcsluag a richt dreme ecin d'Ichtar Connacht.
Ní har buga na ag buantethed do gab O Baigill chuigi a innsoigid da escairdib, uair dobudh derbdeimin leis gurb iad do bi cuigi, acht ruc bann dicra degh thaban 'na coinne & 'na comhairchis et nir an ara n-enech gan dol 'na mesc co nemhcoimedoch, co ndorchoir co tubaisdech trochamail lena a fhírchairid budhéin; et is lanmor an uiresbaid do bochtoib et d'aghailgnechaib, d'anbhannaibh & d'ollamhnaib an tuitim-sin Nell Baigill.
Nior thoirmeisc an moirecht-sin a thriall na a thinnsgedal fa n Domnaill, iar techt an lái do innsoigh co Finnír gur gab comnaidhe & comoirisemh isin maigin-sin co herghi greine arnamarach.
Tet marcsluag meic Cathail Óic Muinnter Airt Ó hSligech co Bragad Chúillid & foghabaid cuid do marcsluag an tsluaig ann et tíagaid a coir imruagtha ría aroile co Belach Duin Iaraind.
Marbthar marcac do Muintir Airt isin tachar-sin & delaoid re cele iar sin.
Anaidh O Domnaill ina foslongport fein an oidhci-sin et eirghis co moch arnamarach et teid co Fersaid Randa in Liagain do dul tairis a Cuil Irre.
Do bi O Conchobair cona tinól a Sligech ag ordugad a muintire do dol a coinne Domnaill co Fersaid Ranna an Liagáin, mur ar marbad Liagan laochmilidh d'Omhorachaib le Lugh Lamfado ac techt d'innsoigid catha Maige Turedh d'Fomhorachaib ac saigid na císchána fá rabadar Eiriunnuigh re cían d'aimsir, conid úadho ainmnighther an Fersad-sin.
An fad do bi in lan mara isin bfersaid do bi na sluaig-sin ac breith breithe ara cheli, as i comairle dorinne O Concobair, o nac roibe coimhlin daoine re n Domnaill, gan tachur fris agan Fersaid ar ndul d'O Domnaill a n-ordugad et ar suigiugad a gonnadh mor re hucht na Fersde noco fagbad inimthechta
Tet Domnaill tar Fersaid arna fagbail gan cosnam et tet drem do muinntir Conchobair d'iarraid imruaicthe ar muintir Domnaill.
Ni himchomhaircech do fregrad ant iaratus-sin, uair do innsoighedar a celi co menmnach michéllidhi moraigentach, marbthar echt mor do muintir Conchobair an la-sin Maoilsechlainn mac Taidc meic Ruaidri Meic Donnchada d'urchor do gondo et marbtur marcach maith ele d'urchor do gha do muintir Domnaill Semus Ballach mac Neill meic hSeain.
Dealaighid rea celi iar sin.
teid O Domnaill co duthaig slechta Briain Conchobair et do bi tri hoidhqi ac milled arba & ac loscad bhailted & mhonadh.
Do bbi Ó Conchobair a foslongport a mac Bel an Droichid.
Tet O Domnaill tar Traigh siar a Tir Fhiachrach Múaidhe & millid moran da gac ernail maithesa inti archena, uair do bi an tír uile ara chomus acht cuid da caislenaibh amáin, rugadar ar moran do cháoraighecht an tíre timchell hSlebi Gamh.
Tiaghaid tar Muaidh síar ar tarraing hslechta Ricaird a Burc a ndiaigh chodach do caoraighecht chlainni Dubhda.
Gabthur inghen Uaitéir a Burc leo, ben Eogain Dubda, maille rena creich.
Do bi do met d'edálaibh et d'airgtibh fuair O Domnaill co tabarthaí mart no dhá mbart ar enbonn annsa foslongport.
Mac Diarmata & clann Taidc Meic Diarmata & clann Meic Dabí do thecht do congnam le hIchtar Connacht a n-agaid Domnaill.
Triallaidh Ó Domnaill tar ais iar ndenam a tosca & a turais isin tir-sin amail bad loinn leis, do bi a n-urlaimhe acna maithib-sin Ichtoir Chonnacht co tibhraidis tachur d'Ó Domnaill ac techt tar ais do et ni tucador acht liamhán imruagtha, oir nir fhuirig O Domnaill o do fhag Tír Fhíacrach noco ndechaid co Droim Clíab, & do bi a coirighthib a comnaide aran comad-sin.
Marbthur marcach do muintir meic Cathail Oic Conchobair aran imruagad-sin ac dul tar Fersaid Randa an Liagain don tsluag Aodh Ballach mac Briain meic Aodho, mac Meic Diarmata do tromlot Aodh mac Eogain meic Thaidc.
Tet O Domnaill da thigh gan umla gan orroim d'fagbail o maithib Ichtair Connacht don dul-sin.
Conchobar Carrach mac Fedhlim Dochartaig do marbad per dolum le clainn Aodho Gruama Dochartaig.
Mac Donnchada do gairm do Donnchad mac Taidc meic Ruaidri et gan Mac Donnchada fein d'ecc & se a n-err a aoisi iarna dallad Eogan mac Donnchada meic Murchada, & cogad ac clainn Eogain re Mac Donnchada fan ainm-sin et gan ni suaithnid do milled eturra.
An Gilla Dub mac Aodho meic Ruaidri Conchobair d'fagbail bais an bliadain-sin.
Sluaigedh le Conchobair Sligig & le Ruairc & le mac Cathail Óic Conchobair ar tarroing Meic Diarmado & clainni Taidc Meic Diarmada ar Toirrdelbach Ruad mac Taidc Buide et na Cluainti do milled doib itir cill & tuaith.
Dol as sin annsna Tuathaib & Muinter Ainlidhe do tabairt bragad doib et gan a milledh doibh, a ndol a sin a Mainechaib & gac aon fa caraid d'Ua Conchobair dib do milled, acht ar ainic Ruairc dibh.
Uair ni do denedh millte dochuaid Ruairc aran sluaigedh-sin, acht da fecain an fedfad sichain do dhenamh itir Mac n-Diarmata cona braithrib & Conchobair Ruad.
Gabaitt in sluag-sin caislen an Turruic & brisid e.
Tic Donnchad mac Emainn Cheallaigh cucu do bragaid d'ecla a duthaige fein do milled.
Triallaid an sluag-sin tara n-ais iar ndenom a tosca & a turais amail ba loinn leo et berar na braighdi-sin co Sligech mac Áinlighi & mac Ceallaigh, rucadar comhla brec an Turraic co leo Sligech.
Sloighed oile an bliadain-sin lesin n-Giusdis Saxanach annsa Mumain siar, dar gabh Carraic O g Coinnell et dar briss droichet Murchada Briain ar Sinainn, ma's fior do bi cuid do Donnchad mac Briain isna gnimaib-sin.
Ruairc do ghairm do Brian mac Eogain mec Tigernain.
Caislen an Chairthi do ghabail & a legadh le Ruairc an bliadain-si.
Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Sean mac Ricaird meic Emainn d'ecc an bliadain-si et cocad mor itir Clainn Ricaird fan tigernus, da Mac Uilliam do ghairm isin tír do Risderd Bacach & d'Uillec mac Ricaird Óig, & Uillec na Cenn a congnam le Risderd mac Bacach.
Donnchad Dubh mac Conchobair meic Ruaidhri Buide, fer saibhris & tighe oidhed coitcinn, d'fagbail báis ongtha & aitrighe.
Mag Flannchaid Feradhach mac Uilliam meic Taidc, taoísec Dartraighe, fer dercach daonachtach d'aos gaca cerde, d'fagbail bais don ghalar brec.
Ó Raighillig Ferghal mac Seain meic Cathail ri mhaicne muinter Maoílmordha, fer feili & firenigh, d'aghpáil bais iar Cumain & Sacarfíc.
Domnall mac Donnchada Cellaigh, cend fedhna maith & tanaisde Maine o Charaidh co Grén, & mac a derbrathar maille ris Egnecan mac Maoilsechlainn meic Donnchada Chellaig, a marbad a fill mar aon le Maoilsechlainn mac Uilliam meic Maoilsechlainn Cellaigh o Fhedhaibh Atha Lúain ar forchongra chlainni Taidc meic Donnchada Cellaig clann derbrathar Domnaill budein.
Clann Meic Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Sean Dub & Remand Ruad dias mac Ricaird meic Uilleic, a marbad le clainn Meic Uilliam ele clann Ricaird Oic ar mbreth a fóraighecht forra a haithle crech an tíre do thinol & do teclomad doibh.
Mac Goisdealb Sean mac an Gilla Duib, nec derrlaictech daonachtach deghchennais fedhna, do marbad per dolum do cuid da cinedh fein
O Concobair Fhailge Brian mac Cathair meic Coinn meic an Calpaig, do dhibirt asa dhuthaig et a caisléin uile do brisiudh & moran da muinntir do marbad inntip, leisin n-Giuisdis Saxanach Loard Linard; et fos tre formad & tre imdell a derbrathar Cathail Ruaid dorinnedh na huilc-sin.
Calann Enair.
mbliadna ar fichit et cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Taisec Muinter Cinaidhe Tadc mac Aodho meic Aodho Meic Contsnamha, fer nairec nosorrderc daonachtach deighinigh, d'fagbail bais
O Gadra Eogan mac Diarmada meic Eogain, tigerna Cúle Ó Finn, d'ecc
Mac Uilliam Burc Tepoid mac Uilleic meic Emainn
& cogad fana inbe da éis.
Sluaiged leis Ó Neill Conn a Trian Congail dar mill & dar crech moran don tír, & mac Neill do gabáil a mac Bel Fersde ar deredh an tsluaig, & O Neill do thecht da thigh iarom.
tigerna Trin Congail Niall Óc mac Neill meic Coinn d'fagbail bais co hobonn fon am-sin & O Nell do fhilled arís a Trian Congail, & a mac do bi a laimh d'faghail dó, & imresain fa tigernus Trin Congail.
Mac Raighillig Brian mac Fergail, echt mór & duine maith uasal, do marbad le muintir an Ghiusdis hSasanaigh ar techt doib ar creich a Clainn Mathgamhna.
Mac Meic hSuibhne Maolmure do marbad le clainn Murchada Meic Súibhne
Cocad idir Aodh mac Buidhe O n-Domnaill & Magnus O Domnaill & clainn Baigill, & caislen Duin na n-Gall d'fagbail d'Aodh & sin do beith 'na buaidhred aran tír; et cuid do slicht an Espuic Gallcubair do marbad le clainn Baigill mac Toirrdelbaig Oic meic Briaín & dias mac Eogain Ballaigh meic Briain, co tuilled maille
Sluaiged leisin n-Giuisdis Saxanach a n-Ibh Failghi et caislen an Daingin ant enbaile dobad daingne inadh & ordugad a n-Erinn do brised do et echta & edala mora d'fagbail ann sin, & bailti Conchobair uile do beith ara comus & an tír do milled.
Ó Domnaill Aodh Dubh mac Aodho Ruaid meic Neill Gairb meic Toirrdelbaig an Fhina, tigerna Tiri Conoill & Ichtair Connacht & Fer Manach & Chinél Moáin & Innsi hEoghain, do chuir a lan do crichib & do chendadhachaib fo chíos et fo dlighed dob faide uadho ina sin; et nirb ingnad gac umla & gac orraim da bfuair se, uair ni facus a bhúaidh age bhidhbadhaib a n-ait cosgair na comlainn, ni thuc troigh theithid riamh roimh uathad na roimh thsochuide on lo fuair tigernus co laithi a bháis da bliadain ar, is minic risin re-sin ruc coscur a namad & buaidh a bidbad et do imdhigh a tíre et a tigernais da n-aindeoin et ruc a cruidh & a cethra & a n-edala uatha iar mbuaidh et cosgar; et nirb ingnad sén na sonus dar éirigh do, uair is é dobad mo meid & maisi 'na aimsir fein, ger mor a meid et a menma do bi a lán d'uaisle et d'einech ann & do treighibh tigernais ann gach enmodh, mar ata aithne et enech, dérc & daonacht, recht et riagail et cosc droichbés et medugad maithesa; uair ni ró linn re radho nach tanic do tslicht Neill Naigiallaig, gan urlamhus Erenn uile aige, tigerna is goire dochuaid do righe na hErenn ina in tigerna-sin ar treisi & ar tochas, ar deilb et ar denam, ar enech et ar uaisle, ar fephus smachta et ar cruas cride fria naimhdibh et ar eolus imdha ar ealadhnaibh; et ni heth fós acht do saoiledh et do creidedh co mor do rer thairngiri na Naomh et na comarrtha cosmaile tarla air fein et aran aimsir rea linn gurb e-sin int Aodh Engach do gelladar fáithi & fisidh & ardnaoim eolchu Erenn do thecht a ndeiredh aimsire, o nárb é ni shaoílim a thecht co bruinne mbráthu et co deóigh an doman; et ni cunntabairt mana beidis Gaoídil ar ndul a mbeiginbhe et a nemhcomall co cuirfedh chuinn thigernais Erenn, do rer cosamhlachta co n-eireochad sin leis, o'tconnairc se Gaoidil Erenn ar ndul chunn michoinghill & chuinn nemhcreidemhna d'ennduine & iad anumal drochsmachta, do chengail se rann re Righ Saxan, innus nar luidh nert Gall air & co roibhe tren Leithi Coinn aige gan amharus do rer gnaith fer n-Gaoidel, uair is minic tuc se sluaigedh timcill ar gac tír dibh sin & tuc a ngeill & a mbraighde da tír fein da toil, amhail tucudar na righa airmid filidh et Remenna Rigraidhe co Cruachain & co hEmain & co hOilech; et nirb ingnad deighhsén dar eirigh do, oir do bi se 'na mac lanamna postu & 'na oigri diles dingmalo agan tír et doba nádúir do maith a athar & a mathar & a maith fein do beith ann, tarla an dá lán-sin a n-entsoightec ac Áodh Domnaill, indus nar cuiredh na ceitri duile a n-enpersainn a n-Erinn san aimsir dhéighenaigh dob imláine a treighibh tigernais et ann gac maith archena ana O Domnaill Aodh Dub mac Aodho Ruaid, ceinnleitir & cosantac Chenéil Conoill, sambail Coinn Cetchathaig ar chocad & ar comerghe chathu & comlainn et medh imlan Airtt Enfhir ar enech & ar fhirinne et cosamhlacht Cairbre ar coimghlicus et ar eolas in gac ealadhain dar gnath ac Gaoidhealaibh, damh comhair Guaire meic Colmain ar thógbail dámh & deóradh et brathair diles dingmalta do Brian Boroma meic Ceinn Eidigh o fholaighecht et o ghnim, mur ata tocbail ord & eclaisi & sgris bithbenach a aosa ainnrechta et innsoighid fora bidhbadaibh co breith & mbuadho; et amail tuc Dia na tidhlaicti mora-sin sa saogal do gurob a flaithus De gabus a anam sosadh iar cumhsgugad on thsaogal; et an cuiged lá do mí Iúil fuair bas a mainesdir Duin na n-Gall ar ndol a n-aibid hSan Pronses da thoil et da aontaigh fein maille re resún maith, & Dardáoin araí laithi sechtmaine ternó on tsaogal iar n-ongad et iar n-aithrige do moladh na hEclaisi; et a mac Magnus O Domnaill do righad 'na inadh do ched et do comoirle Chonollach & chomhorbadh Coluim Cille amhail fa dúal dó.
Sloiged leis O n-Domnaill Magnus a n-Ichtar Connacht a mí medhoin foghmair dar mill moran arbha & dar loisc et dar imdhigh Ichtar Connacht Cairpri & Tir Fhíachrach & an da Luighne et an Corann & Tir Oilella roime anuas; et gabthur baile Eghra Ríabaigh leis Ó n-Domnaill don dul-sin et tuc einec d'Ó Egra fein ar mbeith fora comus, co tuc leis a mbraighdenus he.
Ma Guidir Cú Chonnocht mac Con Connacht meic Briain Meg Uidir tigerna Fer Manach, fer dercach daonachtach dobo mo clú laimhe et uaisle et oinigh da tanic do slicht na Colla re cian d'aimsir et do chuir Ó Chlúain Éis co Caolusce fa umla & fa smacht; et dobad maith an smacht-sin, uair ní thanic 'na dbuthaig fein re chian d'aimsir tigerna dob ferr recht & ríagail et is mo do choisc goid & eigen & aos gaca huilc eli archena et do chuir na tírthi 'na suighe co socoir sichánta & is mó dar eirigh sonus & saibres rea linn; a marbad ar Crechan for Loch Erne per dolum le slicht Tomais Me Guidhir & le slicht Toirrdelbaig Meg Uidir an bliadain-si et a adhnacal a n-Daiminis ar tus, fo dhítin De & Molaisi, a thócbail a gcinn athaidh iar sin leisna Braithribh Minura & a tabairt co mainesdir Duin na n-Gall, &rl.-.
Mac Aodho meic Neill meic Cuinn meic Aodho Buide Niall, adbar tigerna Trín Congail & fer denma uaisle & oinigh & rer cosmail lenmhain luirg a thseinnser ar clú & ar chaithem leith re diol damh & deorad, eges & ollam, ar enec & ar uaisle, do marbad le hAlbanchaib.
O Conchobair Failge do gabáil a dhuthaige fein do nemhthoil an Ghiuisdis th Saxanaigh & a braithrech fein clann Conchobair, & cuid da ndaoínib do buain dhibh & tren a tire féin do gabáil uile dó amail bad cóir d'fer a inaidh.
Barun Delbna Risderd mac Cristoir meic hSemais, sgiath ditin & clíath ghaoíthe Gall re Gaoídeluib, ridire rathmur rocrodho coctac coinglecach, do dol d'ecc 'na baile fein iar mbuaidh ongtha et aithrige, acht gerb imdha guasachta gliad asar ternó conuige sin.
Mac Maoilsechlainn Semus mac Murchada do marbad le mac Conchobair Failghe, fer dobad mó clú et cathreim 'na comhaoís do Chenél Fiachach meic Neill
Mac Raighillig Cathaoír Modarrdha mac Seain meic Cathail do marbad a tóraighecht le Saxanaibh.
Mac Dochartaig Niall Caoch mac Gerailt do marbad a ngreis oidhci le Rugraidhe mac Fedhlim Dochartaig a mac Baile na Cananac for Termand Doire.
Ó Flannagan Tuaithe Ratha Gilla Isa & a mac do marbad co nemmaith leisan cuid eli da chinedh fein, uilc imdha do beith gá ndénam a Feraibh Manach do losgad et do chrechad an bliadain-si a haithle bais Me Guidir.
Crech & loscad do denam a Clainn Amhlaibh don Chalpach Domnaill, & crech ele do denam ar Cathán do.
Calann Enair for Mháirt.
Ocht mbliadna ar fhichid & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Mac Domnaill Aodh Buide mac Aodho Duib meic Aodho Ruaid, rídamhna Thíre Conoill, fer lan d'aithne & d'einech & d'eolus a n-ealádnaibh & dob ferr do baranta laimhe a ngortuib gliad et a mbernnadhaib baogail et is mo do saoiledh do rochtain tigernais a tíre fein do rer airrdenadh & treidhe tigerna da tucudh Día do hsáogal do he, d'fagbail bais an bliadain-si do ghalar aithgerr a Cill O Dónair iar Comaín & Sacarbaic an Aoine iar feil Patraic.
Niall mac Coinn meic Airt Neill, mac righ maith ina roibe uaisle et oinech, do marbad le mac Neill Neill for greis oidhci a caislen na hOmaighe ar fagbail chor amach o chuid éigin da roibhe astigh fein; et Niall Ó Neill do brised an caislein 'na diaigh sin & bheith a ndiaigh an marbtha-sin ara mac fein.
Mac Meg Flannchaid, adbar taoisigh Dartraige Cathaoír mac Feradhaig meic Uilliam Meg Flannchaid, a n-Dun Cairbre a mí Mái.
Sluaiged leis O n-Domnaill Maghnus a n-Iochtar Connacht dar ghabh caislen Sligig co haithesach do bi fa hseolad maith bardadh et ordanais et do bi a fad reime sin a gabáil rena athair gan gabáil.
ar ngabáil an caislein-sin teid a Maigh Luirg et millter an tir co himlan leis, ac filledh tar ais do, ar techt timchell Magha Gadhra, marbthar mac maith Domnaill d'urchor do gondo co tubaisdech fon mbaile-sin Niall Garb mac Maghnusa meic Aodho Duib; et tangadar slan acht sin ar milled Maighe Luirg et Ichtair Connocht acht an cuid tanic le humla dochom Domnaill dibh.
Delp Mure mirbhailech do bi a mac Baile Atha Truim, dar creidedar Erennaigh uile re cian d'aimsir roime sin & do hslanaiged doill et buidhir & bacaig & gac aingces archena, do loscad le Saxanachaib et an Bachall Isu do bi a mac Baile Atha Cliath ac deanam mirbaile et fert n-oirrderc a n-Erinn o aimsir Patraic cusin re-si, do bi a laimh Crist fein dia mbai idir daoinuib, & do bi a laimh Mháoisi meic Amra ac traghadh Mara Ruaid ria Macaib Isrehel.
ni hedh amain acht ni roibhe croch naomh na delp Mure na imáigh orrdeirc a n-Erinn ara ndechaid a cumachta nar loisced leo, ni mo do bi ord dona n-ordaib ara ndechaid a cumochta a n-Erinn nar sgrisadar & an & an Eclais abus & toir ac coinnelbhathad na Saxanach trid sin.
ni derbh lim nac arin mbliadain-si fúas da so.
Misi Seán & is misdi me gan Dolp agam.
Calann Enair.
Nai mbliadna ar & cet mile ais an Tigerna.
O Briain ri Tuadmuman, Concobar mac Toirrdelbaig meic Taidc, d'faghbail pais an pliadain-si iar mbeith treimsi a tigernus Tuadmuman & an tir co toictech tromconaigh rea linn, Murchad mac Toirrdelbaig meic Taidc do rigad 'na inadh amhail do thuill a gnimartha et a áirilled conuige sin.
Sloiged leis O n-Domnaill a n-Ichtar Connacht Maghnas, itir Nodloic & feil Brigde, dar ben cios et braighdi dib.
O Neill Cond do beith a n-Dun na n-Gall ar Caisc an bliadain-si et caithemh sáibhir sochraid do dhenomh d'O Domnaill rena linn, amhail dobad cubaidh, O Domnaill & O Neill do denam gac uile cengail da daingne et da treise re chele ann sin.
Mac Me Guidir Cormac mac Con Chonnocht meic Con Chonnacht meic Briain Me Guidir, mac righ maith co n-uaisle et co n-enech, do marbad a mepail le muintir a derbrathar fein a fiadhnaise an derbrathar, &rl.
Sluaiged leis Ó Neill & le hO n-Domnaill do ched et do comoirle a celi sa Midhe et an tír do milled et do loscad leo co Temhraigh, nar thinóil Gaoídil co Gallaibh ar deiredh na haimsiri aon tsluaigedh as mó leir milledh do maithes na Midhe ana in sluagh-sin & dob áidhble étala óir & airgid et umha & iarainn & gac uile maithusa ele airchena.
Baile Atha Fhir Dhía do lomargain leo etir innmus & edáil, ar bfilled don tsluaigedh-sin doibh & iad lan d'uaill & do dhimus et d'edail lenais an Giuisdis Saxanach iad Loard Linard et leirthinol na mbailted mor & na Midhe etir cill & tuaith et a roibhe do hSaxanchaib a n-Erinn et a mbai do cobhlaighib arna cuantuib gaca taoba dibh coblach romor do bi ar cuan Cairlinne, & beiris an tinol-sin an Ghiusdis ar hsluag Gaoidel a n-Oirghiallaibh et a mac Bel Atha hÓa co hairithi, ni ranic leisan sluag n-Gaoidhelach dol and ordugad amhail bad coir, na urmaisin ar comairle a ndeghdhaoínedh do denom re cosnom na re cothughad, acht imthecht co hanordoighthe et morán da n-edalaib fein & d'édalaibh Gall d'fagbail ann sin ac sluag na Saxanach, gan a beg d'echtoib orrderca d'fagbail doibh ge do imtighsed co hanordaigthi, conadh he Maolmure Mergech mac Eoin Ruaid Meic hSuibhne scel is mó do fágbad do Conallchaib ann.
Mag Aongusa Murcertach do gabail le cuid d'Oirgiallaib iarna fagbail a n-uaiti sluaig ar ndeghail rea muintir aran siubal-sin et a beith tamall a laim gos iseal noco ndernadh meabal fair iar sin ar comoirle choda da cinedh fein cennach do gabáil do cinn a cur docum bais.
Niall Óc O Baigill do marbad le Conchobar mac Baigill o.

Da bliadan et cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Dias mac Uaiter meic Ricaird a Burc do marbad Risderd & Tomas.
Mainesdir Chluana Ramada do thabairt dona Braithribh Bochta de Obseruancia an bliadain-si ar forailedh Briain & maithi Túadmuman et do ced et do comoirle uachtaran an da Ord-sin San Pronsés
Saxain do beith ac díbert iarsma na n-Ord ar fud Erenn et co hairithi mainester Muinechain do milled doibh & gairrdián na mac Brathar maille re cuid ele dona bráithribh do dhicennadh doibh.
Caislen Líathdroma do denam an bliadhain-si leis O Ruairc Brian, d'ainndeoin a luchta cogaid ar gac leith Magh Luirg & an da Muintir Eolais & Ó Raighillig, & a mac fein Conn maille re cuid móir d'feraibh Brefne a cocad ris fós; & an caislen do denam dhó re hathghoirid amlaid sin & moran do milled fa Magh Luirg aran cocad-sin do.
Foslongport do denam d'Ó Domnaill fa crannoig Locha Bethad tús an tsamraidh ar chlainn Domnaill Donnchad & Rughraide, sáothair imdho do denam cucu & nar búadhaiged an baile fa dheóigh orra.
Dias mac Baigill Niall & Conchobar do comtuitim le chele an bliadain-si Niall do dol d'iaraidh Conchobair a Luachrus & cealg oidhchi do dhénamh do a tempoll hSenchain, Conchobar do thecht ar fud an tíri arnamarach lena ghnoaighthib fein & Niall cona muintir d'eirghi 'na diaigh asin tempall; et o'dconnairc Conchobar chuigi iad, beith ar imthecht do tar traigh Lúachrais sios, & a muinter do sgaradh ris et Niall da lenmain co rogér roimh a cuidechta féin & breith ar Conchobar da ainndeoin; & Conchobar d'fuirech re Niall co beódha laidir and sin & bualadh a celi doib gan choigill gan chomoiresem & Niall do marbad aran lathair-sin ar tus et Conchobar do beith buailti & muinter Neill do thecht aran lathair et Conchobar do tuitim leo.
nirbo bas iar midhlaochus comhtuitim na deisi-sin, co nach roibhe da feine fein re haimsir imchéin roime sin días ocmacam dobad mo d'echtaib anait an clann-sin Baigill.
Clann Uilliam meic an Espuic Gallcubair Aodh Grúamdho & Uilliam Óc do marbad le clainn Baigill le Domnall & le Toirrdelbach a ndigail marbtha a n-athar.
Sluaigedh leis n Domnaill Maghnus a Connochtoib an bliadain-si da ndechaid a Magh Luirg & a Clainn Chunnmaig, dar mhill & dar loisc iad co himlan & dar crech an Coirsliab, toighecht slan iar mbuaidh & choscur.
sluaigedh ele le n Domnaill an bliadain cetna fa mac Neill Niall mac Airt Oig tanuisde Thíre hEogain et fa mac Meic Domnaill na hAlpan Colla mac Alusdrainn maille re morán Albanac.
imthecht ar tús a Feraibh Manach & moran do milledh innti & gellta d'faghbail rena riar iar sin; et gabáil a sin trid Brefne Ruairc et roime co Coirsliab et foslongport an Coirshlebi do denam dho, nogur gherr se an Belach Buide & gach belach ele sháoil se do cor air; & Clann Maoilruanaidh do thecht a cenn Domnaill iar sin & braighde do tabairt do rena breith fein, impodh slan da turus d'Ó Domnaill.
Clann Domnaill Donnchad Cairbrec & Sean Luirg do beith a cocad ar n Domnaill & crandóc Locha Bethoc do beith aca & iat ac buaidhredh an tiri co mor este, O Domnaill da ngabail araon & do gabáil Eignecain meic Domhnaill a mac Baile na Congbala, & Sean O Domnaill do crochad dó et Eignecan & Donnchad do chor a mbraighdenus fa daoirsi & fa dhochor mor, crannoc Locha Bethad do milled d'O Domnaill.
O Dochartaig Geralt mac Domnaill, fer co n-uaisle et co n-enec, d'fagbail báis ar caithem a aoisi re daonacht & re deighenec conuigi sin.
O Baighill do denam do Domnall mac Neill Baigill.
An Giuisdis Saxanach do bi a n-Erinn do dol a Saxanaib fo cuiredh Rig Saxan, iar milled ord & egluis & minn mirbailech Erenn uile d'urmor et iar ndenam olc n-imda bad fado re a n-innisin; et Hanndalín Salasder Giuisdis ele do thecht a n-Erinn 'na inadh.
Ri Alpan do chor gharma ar maithib an chinidh Alpanaigh et a techt chuigi aran cuan a roibhe se, dul annsa loing a roibhe an Ri doibh et an Ri da ngabail itir Gall & Ghaoídel, & na Goill do lecin amac a cinn tamaill 'na diaigh sin & mac Meic Domnaill Semus do congbail a laimh do.
an meid fuair ar foghnam maille ris da chinedh et da dhaoínibh do beith a mbraighdenus mur an cetna, dibirt on Righ ar a raibhe fa rer dibh iar sin.
Sean mac Coind Domnaill do marbad le clainn Murchada Meic Shúibhni na Tuath

Bliadain & da fichit & cet & mile ais in Tigerna, doinenn dermair a tus na bliadna-sin itir hsic & tsnechta, nar lig trebadh na tighedhus do denam a n-Erinn.
Tuathal Balp mac Seain meic Ruaidri Gallchubair, saí dhuine oirecht do mhaithib Conollach, d'ecc.
O Domnaill do dol a cend an Giuisdis hSasanaigh conuigi an Cabhán & sith & cengal do denam doib re celi maille re honoir & re rebherens d'faghbail d'Ó Domnaill.
Maidm mor do thabairt do Mac Uibhelin Rúghraide mac Ualter ar clainn Aodho Neill, dú inur marpad Aonghus mac Maolmure Meic Suibhne & moran do ghalloclaechuib Conallach maille ris, & do marbad ann mar an cétna coruchad galloclaech do Chlainn Domnaill & a lán eli ar gac leth nach airmither ann so; & Mac Uibhelin do dol sluag mor fa cend gairid 'na diaigh sin ar clainn Aodho Neill et clann Aodho Conn & Domnall do marbadh leis.
O Cerbaill Fer gan Ainm mac Maoilrúanaidh, cenn oinigh & engnama hslechta Taidc meic Céin ar fheli & ar uaisli, do marbad per dolum, é dall, le clainn hSeáin Cerbaill & le mac Maoilmúaidb Seán mac Domnaill Chaoich Maoilmuaidh, ge do bhí O Cerbaill dall díradhairc ann sin dorinne se cosnam & congnam maith dá marbad.
An crannóc oirrtherach ar Loch Glendo Dallain do gabáil do clainn Domnaill meic Donnchada Ruairc ar Donnchad mac Donnchada Ruairc, & fa cenn goirid 'na diaigh sin tucadur clann Donnchada Í Ruairc Domnall & Fer gan Ainm innsoigid aran crannoic & do loisgsed an baile gan fhis, mothaighter iad & lenaid clann Domnaill iad & berid orra.
Marbthur & baiter ann Fer gan Ainm mac Donnchada, gabtur ann Domnall & crochthar iar sin le clainn Domnaill Ruairc.
Sluaigedh leis Ó n-Domnaill a coinne an Giuisdis a Tir Eogain & an tir d'imthecht & do milled leo don toisc-sin et an Giusidis d'impodh ar ais fan Midhi et O Domnaill d'filled tar ais trid Tír Eogain & techt slan gan tachar na tecmail d'fagbail ac techt na ac imthecht trid Tir Eogain dó.
O Domnaill do dol fo cend athghoirid 'na diaigh sin don taobh soir do Loch, a Feroib Manach, & Cuil na n-Oirer & an taobh soir do Loch Érne do milled leis don tír & don loch, oir do badur báid & artraighe aige ac milled a n-oilén & a thsluag ac milled an tiri, gur fhagaib a ndith arbha co mor an bliadain-sin iad.
Sluaigedh ele le n Domnaill fo cend goirid 'na diaigh sin a Feroibh Manach dan taobh thíar do Loch Éirni, & do chuir a artraighe aran Loch & do gabh fein et a hsluag don tir, co ro millset an tir a coinne a celi co rangador co hInis Sgellenn, brister an caislen leó don dol-sin et tangadar tar a n-ais iar mbuaid & cosgar don cur-sin.
Domnall mac Neill Gairb Domnaill do marbad leis O mac Baigill ar ndol do Domnall do congnam le Toirrdelbach mac Baigill a n-agaid h-Baigill; & ruaic do tabairtt doib d'Ó Baigill ar tus et O Baigill d'filled orra-san & brised roimhe & mac Neill Domnaill do marbad don ruaic-sin leis O mac Baigill; et ni docha lim iná gurub annsa bliadain-si romam dá bás meic Neill Gairb.
Mac an Baird Tíri Conoild Conchobar Ruad mac Fergail, saí re dan & re fóghlaim & fer tighi oiged coitchinn, d'fagbail bais iar n-ongad & iar n-aitrighe.
Calann Enair.
Da bliadain & da & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Sluaiged le n Domnaill a n-Ichtar Connacht & clann Domaill Calbach & Aodh & O Dochartaig do dol roime an sluag co Baile in Muta & crech do denam doibh & techt slan a cend Domnaill; et maithi Ichtair Connacht do thecht a cenn Domnaill, co hairithi Mac Donnchada Baile an Muta, tar eis a creiche, & a chis d'íc ris Ó n-Domnaill don dol-sin doibh.
O Conchobair Ruad Toirrdelbach Ruad mac Taidc Buide do gabáil le Ruaidri mac Taidc Meic Diarmata
Comorba Termoinn Me Graith Torrdelbach mac Aindriasa
Crech do denam don Chalbach O Domnaill ar shlicht Aodho Ballaig meic Domnaill.
Mac Con Midhe Brian Dorcho mac Solaim, sai re dan & re foghlaim & fer toicthech tromchonáigh & fer tighe oighed coitchinn, d'ecc im fel Coluim Cille.
Cormac mac Diarmata Clérigh Brathair Minur.
Sluaiged le hO n-Domnaill et leis Ó Ruairc Brian mac Eogain an bliadain-si co Ruta Meic Uibhelin, da chuid nó tri do denam da sluag re hucht na Banna et imtecht tar fersdib na Banna doibh fonn innus-sin, Mac Uibhilin & drong mor do Shaxanchaib do beith don taobh thall don Banna rompo.
Acht ata ni chena, ranic O'Domnaill & O Ruairc cona sluag tar Banna maille re gúasacht romor et nir fhechadur do Mac Uibilin na dá hSaxanchaib ina do ghúais bhaiti da fuaradur et tucudur dá sgeimhledh no a tri sgeimhled soir edrad & Cnoc Leaaid et sgeimledh eli súas chois Bhanna, tarla moran crech & édala riu ar gac taobh & co hairithi tarla ris O Ruairc & resin Calbach O n-Domnaill & re Cathain édala aidble & imad crech, innus co roibhe gac sluag dibh a foslongport ar leith an oidhci-sin cona crechoibh; et as í comuirle dorine O Domnaill & Ó Ruairc arnamarac na crecha-sin do marbad d'urmor.
Mac Uibilin do thecht a cend Domnaill & Ruairc 'na diaigh sin & cendoch mor d'echaib & do buaibh do thabairt úadha et sith do denam doib iar sin et Domnaill do thecht slan cona shluag tar Banna; et nírbh innann lé Ruairc & techt slán aní do imdhigh air marcach maith da muintir do bháthad sa Bhanna Tadhg mac Briain meic Maghnusa Meic Diarmada Ruaid, fer daonachtach deghdelba dob ferr aithne & eolus ar ealadhain da tanic d'feraibh a áosa do hslicht Diarmata Daill a coimré ris.
Mac Uibhelin Rugraidhe mac Ualtair do techt ar siubal creiche ar Cathain et crech mór do chur roime do et Cathain da lenmain a tóruigecht Maghnus mac Donnchada Cathain et buannaidhe moro do Clainn t-Suibhne tarla aige an uair-sin slicht Ruaidri Meic hSuibhni, brisedh doibh sin ar Mac Uibhilin & ar moran Albanach do bi maille ris, innus gur facbad ár mór daine dibh fa mac Alusdroinn Carraigh meic Meic Domnaill & fa Mac th Seáin & fa morán eli nac airmither ann so do hsluag Meic Uibilín; et Mac Uibhilín fein & mac Meic Domnaill do imthecht ar ecin & morán da muintir do bhathad aran mac Banna maille rer marbad dib.
Sluaigedh le Mac Uibhelin ina dhiáigh sin ar O Cathan et an Treisinér Saxanach & drem mor do hSaxanaibh maille ris et caislen Cathain Leim an Madaidh do gabáil doibh & an med do bardaib do bi ann do marbad doib et Mac Uibilin d'imtecht slan iar cosgar don cur-sin.
Mac Uibhilin fo cenn goirit 'na diaigh sin do thoghairm morain do Clainn t-Suibhne chuige ar buannacht slicht Ruadri Meic hSuíbhne & mac Donnchada meic Meic Shuibhni na Tuath & mac Murchada Meic Suibhne et mac Meic Shuibhne Bhághuinigh maille re moran eli do maithib óganac Clainni Suibhne; et ar ndol doib sin a cenn Meic Uibhlin do badar a maithIsin fa muirnn & fa moronoir a mbaile Meic Uibilin a cengal a cuir et a cunnartha; & doronadh comuirle meplach mirunach le mac Meic Domnaill et le hAlbanchaibh do bi ann sin & le muintir Meic Uibilin na galloclaich-sin Clainni t-Suibhne d'innsoigid tar eis gac cengail da ndernadur roime sin, & doronsad amhlaid.
Tar eis baile Meic Uibhilín d'fagbail doibh do innsoigedor an Clann t-Suibhne-sin gan fhios gan airechadh, innus gur marbadur a n-urmor uile ar enlathair ann sin, & co hairithi marbthar ann mac Meic Shuibhne Baghainigh & mac Murchada Meic Shuibni, co nac mór tánic ar ais dibh a farrad ar marbad aran lathair-sin.
Lucht loinge faide tanic do denam chena a hIarthar Connacht a Tir Conaill do tuitim le Toirrdelbach mac Meic Shuibhni Bhaghainigh, co nac dechaid fer inneste sgel as dibh acht an duine uasal do bi aca mac Fhlaithbertaigh do anacal do mac Meic hSuibhne; et a Rachrainn Muintire Birnn dorinnedh na gnima-sin le mac Meic hSuibne.
Duibgend mac Dubhtaig meic Maoilsechlainn meic Matha Glais Duibgennain, ollam sochraidh saoircerdach re senchus et fer tighe oidhed, d'ecc in hoc ando.
Sluaigedh le n Domnaill a n-Íchtar Connocht an foghmur-sin et maithi Ichtair Connacht do thecht 'na cend maille re sithchain et a chís et a tigernus d'ic co humal ris.
ni fado ar sgaoiledh do thsluag Domnaill co tanic Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Uilleg na Cend mac Ricaird, Mac Uilliam Burc Dauid mac Uilleic sluag mor ele a n-Ichtur Connacht; et gabthur leo baile Flannagan Bel Atha Uachtair et ticid fein & Mac Diarmado & clann Taidc Meic Diarmada a n-Ichtar Connacht; et ticid maithe Ichtair Connacht a cenn Meic Uilliam ann sin et gabais Mac Uilliam iat & beris leis a Clainn Ricaird iad O Dubhda & Mac Donnchada in Corainn & cuid do Clainn t-Suibhne Connachtaigh Maolmure mac Colla Meic Suibne, & Maolmure mac Colla d'fagbail bais annsa braighdenus-sin a mbaile Meic Uilliam Chlainni Ricaird.
a cionn hsechtmaini 'na diaigh sin Maolmure mac Eogain Meic Shuibne do marbad le clainn Maoilmure meic Colla & he ac idhlocad chlainni Dubhda; & fa cend raithe 'na diaigh sin iad fein d'innarba & a mbailti do brised & fer dib fein do marbad & moran da lucht lenamna.
Mac Aodho Neill Fedlim Dubh, ant enmac do mair ac Aodh Mergec, do marbad an bliadain-si.
Mac Domnaill an Ca Ibach do dol a cenn an Giuisdis & a shith fein & sith Domnaill do denam dó risan n-Giusdis, & impodh slan do iar sin.
Maghnus O Domnaill do tabairt Tuath Rátha & Luirg do hSean mac Con Connacht Meg Uidir ar milled morain fa Mag Uidir reme sin d'O Domnaill, & Mag Uidir arna thabhairt fein d'O Domnaill & do thabairt a thíre & a thalman do et do tabairt eirghe amac ar fein & ara thalmain co gnathach rena lind ara hson sin, no cáin san erghe amach nac fuighti; et tuc fos leth erca marbthu duine ar fedh Fer Manach uile d'Ó Dhomnaill.
Mac Neill Feidhlim Caoch mac Coinn meic Coinn, mac righ maith do Chenél Eogain, do marbad le Mac n-Domnaill Gallóclaech co tupaisdech d'enbuille ga, dias mac eli Neill d'fagbail bais an bliadain-si.
Brian mac Neill meic Airtt Óic Neill, ant ocmac righ dobad mó clu uaisle & oinigh tanic do Chenel Eogain meic Neill re cian d'aimsir, d'fagbail bais re hadhart sa t-Sencaislen do hsunrad.
O Neill Conn mac Coinn do dol a cend Righ Saxan an bliadain-si & Rí Saxan do ghairm iarla de, a cur d'fiachaib air gan Neill do ghairm de as sin suas, O Neill do thecht slan iar sin.
Calann Enair.
Tri bliadna & da fhichid & v cet et mile ais an Tigerna.
Mac Meic Suibhne Fanad Maolmure mac Domnaill Óic, adbar tigerna Fhanad, do marbad le clainn Meic Suibne Fanad le clainn Toirrdelbaig meic Ruaidri meic Maoilmure, & lamh maith do denamh dó re hucht a marbtha amail doba minic leis, gur marbad leis an Dubhaltac mac Fir Dorcho Meic Suibhne, an baranta laime is ferr do bi 'na agaid, ni hedh amain acht da mbeth comtrom aige do digheoladh e fein co maith, conid dona sgelaibh dobad mo do Clainn th Suibni in mac-sin Domnaill.
Mac Meic Suibhne Tiri Baghaine d'fagbail bais a tus a aoisi & a inme Eóin mac Neill.
Mac Baigill Brian mac Neill do marbad a fell le clainn Óic Baigill.
Espoc Ratha Botha ant Espoc Ó Gallcubair d'ecc
Mag Uidiri Sean do techt ar siubal creiche a n-Dartraighe et clann Domnaill do dol leis aran siubal-sin Rugraidhe & Nechtoin, & ar sgaoiledh ar sgeimeltaib doibh fedh an tire Nechtain do marbad d'urchar do gha.
O Domnaill Maghnus do dol docom na comoirle moire et a braithre fein Eignecan & Donnchad do bi a laim aige re fado roime sin do breith leis, a ligen ar comairle an Giuisdis et na comoirle moire, & techt doib fo sith & cairdes Crist re cele; & Cunn O Domnaill do bi a fad etir Gallaib reme-sin do hsidhughad ris O n-Domnaill an uair-sin, & Conn do dol a Saxanaibh an uair-sin ar cuairt ar cend an Righ, ar ndol reme sin a cenn an Righ do & ar faghbail onora moire uadho; et O Domnaill ar techt slan on comairle don dol-sin.
Caislen Lifir do fhagaib O Domnaill a n-orrlaim Cathaoír meic Thuathail et thslechta Aodha Gallchubair, an Caislen do ghabail doib & doirseoir Domnaill & a lucht fedhma do cur amach doib; & O Domnaill & an Calbach O Domnaill do beith a ndiaigh an caislein orrthu et moran do dhainibh do marbad eturra & an Calbach, & co hairithe an Dubaltac mac Colla Meic hSuibhne do marbad eturra arin cocad-sin & moran sbreidhe & airnéisi do milled d'O Domnaill fa hslicht Aodho Í Gallchubair fan caislen-sin.
Muirghes mac Paidin meic Lochlainn meic Maoilsechlainn Maoilchonaire, féigi na filidhechta & grianan an tsenchusa & fer foillsighthi gac fesa & gac fireolais dona fealmacaibh et cend forais & foghloma gac fhirealadhna & fer dercach daonachtach saibhir sochonaigh, d'faghbail bais ongtha & aitrighe ar mbreith bhuadho o dhoman & o dhemhan & a adhnocal fo ditin De & Patraic a n-Oil Finn.
Rí Alban do dol d'ecc a tus a aoisi & a treisi ar mbrised madhma ar hSaxanaibh reme sin, & gan oigri d'fagbail 'na inadh acht lenam mna a cionn a hocht sechtmaine, Rí Saxan a gabail forneirt ar Alpain ann sin.
Mac Dochartaig Cathaoir mac Gerailt do marbad le clainn I Dochartaig.
Mac Aodho Gruama I Dochartiag do marbad leisin clainn cetna; & Ó Domnaill do dol sluag mor ar Ó n-Dochartaig do digail na marbtha-sin, & braighde hI Dochartaig d'fagbail d'O Domnaill 'na diaigh sin a ngill rena breith fein.
O Dochartaig do gabail Cathaoír meic Tuathail Gallchubair & a tabairt d'O Domnaill et O Domnaill do gabail Toirrdelbaig meic Feidlim Finn hI Gallchubair et a tabairt leis fa caislen Lifir, & nac bfuair se an baile astu don dol-sin.
Slicht Eoghuin Meic hSuibhne et slicht Cormaic Meic Donnchada do dol ar siubal chreiche ar n Eghra mac Buidhi et Ó Concobair Tadc mac Taidc meic Aodho et hEgra do breith orrthu & a madmughad & maithi na Clainni Suibhne-sin do gabail Ruaidri mac Dubgaill & clann Maolmuri meic Eogain; et marbthar ann cuid do hslicht Cormaic Meic Donnchada.
O Maoilsechlainn Fethlimidh Óc do marbad le Mag Eochagan.
Mac Suibhne na Tuath & a mac Brian do gabail le coblach o Iarthar Connacht a n-Innsibh Meic an Duirnn & a mbreith leo a laim.
Cocad mor idir Mag Uidir et slicht Toirrdelbaig Meg Uidir & slicht Toirrdelbaig do milled morain fa Mag Uidir.
Mag Uidir do dol a cend Domnaill et athdaingniugad sithi do denam doib ar droim na sithi doronsat remhe.
Mac Uilliam Clainni Ricaird Uilleg na Cend d'ecc & cocad mor a Cloinn Ricaird 'na diaigh sin fan tigernus & Mac Uilliam do gairm d'Uillec mac Ricaird Óic.
a Burc.
Msi miolus o maoilc-
Calann Enair.
Ceitri bliadna & da & cet & mile ais an Tigerna.
Iarla Desmuman Semus mac Semus meic Seain, ar bfagbail a lan d'imresain & d'esaonta fa thosac a tigernais et ar mugad & ar morcennsugad na coigcrich 'na comfhoccus, d'fagbail bais an bliadain-si.
Mac Domnaill an Calbach do dol a cenn an Giusdis th Saxanaigh et caiptin no dó Sasanach co mbuidin moir do thabairt leis co Tír Conoill & costus mor et caithem sochraid do denam d'O Domnaill riu, & dol fa caislen Lifir et braigdi thslechta Aodho Gallchubair do bi ac Ó Domnaill re tamall reme sin do thabairt a laim na Saxanac Cathaoír mac Tuathail & mac Fedlim Finn Í Gallchubair.
mur do chuirsed na Sasanaigh docum an baile marbthar Saxanach dib co luath fan mbaile, marbthur Cathaoir mac Tuathail leisna Sasanchaib aran lathair-sin ann a gheimlib fein, dobeir Aodh O Domnaill & an cuid ele do thslicht Aodho an caislen as mac Fedlim Finn & as mac ele Tuathail do bi a laim et fagbaid fein an tír; & léigis O Domnaill imtecht dona Saxanchaib ar n-ic thuarasdail moir
Mac Nell Niall mac Airt Oic ar fagbail báis an bliadain-si ant enmac righ is mó do fuloing do dhúadh & do dochar cocaid etir Cenel Eogain.
Cenel Conoill da tanic do hslicht Neill Noigiallaig riam, soigtec inbhe & ardtigernais Chenéil Eogain, fer lán d'aithne & d'enec et d'ealadain & do cheól beóil & laime, d'ecc sa t-Senchaislen.
Sluaigeth le n Domnaill co Ruta Meic Uibilin dar gabadh leis Innsi an Locain ara raibhe caislen croinn & daingen maith ac Mac Uibilin; et O Domnaill d'fagbail an baile-sin iarna gabáil ac Ó Cathan.
Caislen Baile an Lacha fós do gabáil d'Ó Domnaill don dul-sin et imarcaid édalo d'fagbail ands bailtib-sin, Inis Locha Burrann & inis Locha Lethinnsi do gabáil le n Domnaill don dol-sin & moran édalo d'fagbáil orrthu mur an cetna, an tír do loscad leis co léir & techt slán iar sin.
Mac Suibhne Fanad Toirrdelbach do marbad
Cocad etir O n-Domnaill & O Neill an bliadain-si & O Domnaill do dol a celg a comghar don t-Sencaislen & marbad do denam leis & braigdi do gabail dó mac Briain & tuilled eli.
O Neill ar ndenam chreiche chois Fhinne.
An Calbach ar ndenam chreiche a Tir Eoghain.
O Domnaill ar ndenam creiche moire ele a Tir Eogain.
Clann Meic Domnaill na hAlban Semus & Colla do thecht fecht Albanac ar tarroing Meic Uibilin & Innsi an Locain do gabáil doibh fein & do Mac Uibilin ar bardoib Cathain & Brian mac Donnchada Cathain & a raibhe maille ris do loscad edir duine & edail & crecha & ededh, & creacha & digla mora do denam do Mac Uibilin ar O Cathain.
O Catháin ar fasdódh thslechta Ruaidri Meic Suibhne, & lá da tanic Mac Uibilin tar Banna Ó Catháin & a ghalloclaich ar mbreith air & tóraigecht trom ar mbuain do & a creach do buain de et moran daoine do lot et do marbad uime.
Crech mor eli do denam leis O Cathain aran Ruta 'na diaigh sin.
Murchad mac Meic hSuibhne na Tuath, sai re henec & re huaisle, d'ecc
Donnchad Mac Suibne a derbrathair eli d'ecc.
Cocad mor itir clainn Meic Shuibhne na Tuath et caislen Meic hSuibne do gabáil le clainn Murchada Meic Suibni & le Brian Mac Suibne; et Mac Suibne do ghairm d'Eogan Óc mac Meic Shuibne et Mac Suibne do gairm do Thoirrdelbach mac Murchada Meic Suibne; & clann Donnchada Meic Suibne do dol astec maille re sithcain sa caislen-sin Meic hSuibne a cenn chlainni Murchada & Briain Meic Suibne & Toirrdelbach mac Murchada & Brian ele mac Meic hSuibni do marbad leo & an baile do thabairt do Mac hSuibni & tigernus gan imresain d'fuirec aige o sin amach.
Mac Suibni Eogan mac Domnaill meic Neill d'fagbail bais a mbráighdenus a n-Iarthar Connacht ac Muintir Maille ar caithem a aoísi re daonacht.
Calann Ienair for Dardaoin.
Da bliadain & tri fichid & cet & mile aois an Tigerna an tan testa an bile buadha & an dos díona & an crab cnudnis & an lam costaid & cothaighthe chlainni Cuinn Chétchathaig Brian mac Eogain meic Tigernain meic Thaidhg meic Tigernain Moir Í Ruairc, fer is mo do cuir na cricha & na comursanna fá chíos & fo canachus do fein, fer bud mó enech & airdtidhlaicthi d'aois ciuil & oirpetid & ealadan, fer is mo do chenduigh dán & deghmolad don Adamclainn, fer is mo tuc do thuillmib & do thuaruslaib d'uaislib & d'ardmhaithib Erenn, fer is mó dorinne ferann cairti & cloidhim gaca taoba 'na timcell, fer is mo do cheannaig & d'ol d'fion gan chuan gan cosced do bi a n-Erinn an fer-sin & fer dob ferr istir & dob uaisil & dob oirrderca cemenda rea cuimnechad, fer ar nach rucad buaidh troda na teacmala, fer brisdi gaca bearna & gaca bealaig ara-bhidhbhadaibh co haindeonach, fer u mó ór & airged & innmusa, cuirn et cuaich & cupana, arm & édedh & ordanas, cruidh & cethra & caomhairgedha, amail adeir an seanfhocal do shonnradha an te sgaoileas gurab é chruinnigheas.
Caoga & da bliadain mile bliadain is coic ced o tanic Crist i mac Beithil co breith Briain o Bretnechuibh.
